### [1] [Hierarchical localization in disordered Apollonian networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11846)
*Eduardo M. K. Souza,Francisco A. B. F. de Moura,Guilherme M. A. Almeida*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了阿波罗网络（Apollonian network）在存在对角和非对角无序时的局域化特性，揭示了局域化程度与网络层次拓扑结构及能量的强相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究复杂网络中拓扑结构与无序（disorder）如何共同影响局域化行为，特别关注阿波罗网络这一具有层次结构的复杂网络模型。

Method: 通过采用位点分辨的局域化度量（site-resolved localization measure），分析阿波罗网络在对角无序（diagonal disorder）和非对角无序（off-diagonal disorder）条件下的局域化特性。

Result: 研究发现局域化程度强烈依赖于能量并与网络层次拓扑相关：在谱边缘（spectral edges），本征态强局域于源自前几代的高度连接位点；在零能附近，局域化与最低度位点相关。对角无序增强负能区域的局域化，而非对角无序则削弱该区域的局域化。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明拓扑结构和无序共同塑造复杂网络中的局域化行为，枢纽节点（hub）主导谱边缘但对能带中心贡献可忽略，其相关局域态对无序具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: We investigate localization properties of the Apollonian network (AN) in the presence of diagonal and off-diagonal disorder. By employing a site-resolved localization measure, we show that the localization degree is strongly dependent on the energy and tied to the hierarchical topology of the network. At the spectral edges, eigenstates are strongly localized on highly connected sites originating from previous generations, a behavior that persists under both disorder mechanisms. In contrast, around zero energy localization is associated with the lowest-degree sites. As disorder breaks the underlying C3 symmetry of the AN, it promotes spatial reconfiguration of these states while preserving their support on low-degree nodes. For diagonal disorder, localization is enhanced over a broad range of negative energies, whereas off-diagonal disorder induces weakening of localization in this region. Finally, we show that the hub dominates the spectral edges but has negligible contribution near the band center, indicating that its associated localized states are robust against disorder. These results highlight how topology and disorder jointly shape localization in complex networks.

</details>


### [2] [Mobility-edge-embedded Hofstadter butterfly from a tilt-induced quasiperiodic potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12472)
*Sanghoon Lee,Kyoung-Min Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究在倾斜诱导的准周期势中实现了"迁移率边嵌入的Hofstadter蝴蝶"（MEE-HB），将分形能谱与迁移率边相结合，为探索分形结构与局域化之间的相互作用提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hofstadter蝴蝶（Hofstadter butterfly）和迁移率边（mobility edges）是准周期系统的标志性现象，但二者之间的相互作用机制尚不明确。研究旨在探索这两种现象在倾斜诱导准周期势中的收敛与交织。

Method: 通过在方形晶格上引入相对于晶轴倾斜的周期势构建准周期势，该构型在光学晶格实验中易于实现。采用紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）进行分析，并推导出类Harper方程（Harper-like equation）来解释现象起源。

Result: 研究发现了"迁移率边嵌入的Hofstadter蝴蝶"（MEE-HB），表现为包含迁移率边的分形能级分裂图案，其中迁移率边分隔扩展态与局域态。分形图案源于一维准周期势，而迁移率边则来自有效长程跳跃（effective long-range hopping）。

Conclusion: MEE-HB的分形维度为0.8-1.0，显著高于标准蝴蝶的0.4-0.6范围，表明其谱集密度更高。倾斜诱导势成为探索分形结构与局域化相互作用的通用平台。

Abstract: The Hofstadter butterfly (HB) and mobility edges (MEs) are hallmark phenomena of quasiperiodic systems, yet their interplay remains elusive. Here, we demonstrate their convergence within a tilt-induced quasiperiodic potential on a square lattice, giving rise to a ``mobility-edge-embedded Hofstadter butterfly'' (MEE-HB). This potential is generated by aligning a periodic potential at an angle relative to the lattice axes--a configuration readily accessible in optical lattice experiments. Using a tight-binding model, we show that the MEE-HB manifests as a fractal energy splitting pattern hosting MEs that separate extended and localized states. Our Harper-like equation shows that the fractal pattern originates from 1D quasiperiodic potentials, while MEs stem from effective long-range hopping. Notably, the MEE-HB exhibits a fractal dimension of 0.8--1.0, significantly exceeding the 0.4--0.6 range of the standard butterfly, indicating a denser spectral set. Our findings establish tilt-induced potentials as a versatile platform for exploring the interplay between fractal structures and localization.

</details>


### [3] [Quantum percolation in honeycomb lattices under random spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12732)
*W. S. Oliveira,Julián Faúndez,Welles Morgado*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了蜂窝晶格中具有位点稀释和随机自旋轨道耦合的量子渗流现象，通过精确对角化和有限尺寸标度分析，揭示了金属-绝缘体转变的临界行为及其对自旋轨道耦合的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解量子渗流（quantum percolation）在蜂窝晶格中的行为，特别是位点稀释和随机自旋轨道耦合（random spin-orbit coupling）如何影响金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）的临界特性。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）结合有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis），研究量子渗流阈值 $p_q$ 和关联长度指数 $ν$，并分析谱统计（spectral statistics）在自旋轨道耦合存在时的对称性变化。

Result: 无自旋轨道耦合时，量子渗流阈值 $p_q$ 保持有限且显著高于经典位点渗流阈值 $p_c$；存在自旋轨道耦合时，谱统计从高斯正交系综（Gaussian orthogonal ensemble）交叉到高斯辛系综（Gaussian symplectic ensemble），同时 $p_q$ 系统性地向更低占据概率移动，表明自旋轨道耦合促进离域化（delocalization）。

Conclusion: 自旋轨道耦合通过改变对称性类别（symmetry class）影响量子渗流行为，当耦合足够强时，$p_q$ 趋于饱和，临界指数接近二维辛普适性类别（two-dimensional symplectic universality class）的预期值。

Abstract: We investigate quantum percolation in a honeycomb lattice with site dilution and random spin-orbit coupling. Using exact diagonalization combined with finite-size scaling analysis, we study the metal-insulator transition, extracting the quantum percolation threshold $p_q$, and the correlation-length exponent, $ν$. In the absence of spin-orbit coupling, we find that $p_q$ remains finite and demonstrate that the quantum threshold is significantly higher than the classical site-percolation threshold $p_c$ of the honeycomb lattice. When spin-orbit coupling is present, the spectral statistics exhibit a crossover from the Gaussian orthogonal ensemble to the Gaussian symplectic ensemble, reflecting the change in symmetry class. Simultaneously, the quantum percolation threshold shifts systematically to lower occupation probabilities, indicating that the spin-orbit coupling favors delocalization. For sufficiently strong spin-orbit coupling, $p_q$ tends to saturate, while the critical exponent approaches the expected one of the two-dimensional symplectic universality class.

</details>


### [4] [Localization and Flat Bands in Edge-Inflated Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12759)
*Richard Berkovits*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文研究通过边缘膨胀（edge inflation）方法生成的晶格中的局域化和平带形成，分析了三种平带机制及其在无序条件下的鲁棒性，发现几何结构本身可在有序和无序系统中产生鲁棒局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究边缘膨胀晶格中的局域化和平带形成机制，探索几何结构如何在不同类型的无序扰动下产生鲁棒局域化现象，为理解几何诱导的局域化提供理论框架。

Method: 通过将每个键（bond）替换为有限紧束缚链（finite tight-binding chain），对有序的Lieb-L、super^Lhoneycomb和super^Ltriangular晶格进行分析，并考察其对键无序、位点无序、随机磁通和膨胀过程随机性的响应。

Result: 识别出三类平带：链诱导平带（chain-induced flat bands）、对称保护零能平带（symmetry-protected zero-energy flat bands）和近平连接带（nearly flat junction bands）。零能手性带和连接诱导平带在某些扰动下保持鲁棒，随机边缘膨胀图中也保留显著平带特征，零能态数量可由匹配亏数（matching deficiency）N-2ν(G)估计。

Conclusion: 边缘膨胀晶格构成了一类广泛的系统，其中几何结构本身可在有序和无序环境中产生鲁棒局域化，局部树状结构继续控制低能零度（nullity），为几何诱导局域化研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study localization and flat-band formation in lattices generated by repeated edge inflation of square, honeycomb, and triangular parent lattices. Replacing each bond by a finite tight-binding chain produces several distinct classes of flat bands: chain-induced flat bands at the eigenenergies of the inserted chains, symmetry-protected zero-energy flat bands in bipartite edge-inflated lattices, and nearly flat junction bands near the spectral edges for sufficiently long chains. We analyze these mechanisms for ordered Lieb-$L$, super$^{L}$honeycomb, and super$^{L}$triangular lattices, and examine their response to bond disorder, site disorder, random magnetic flux, and randomness in the inflation process itself. While bond and site disorder broaden most flat bands, the zero-energy chiral band and the junction-induced flat bands remain robust under certain perturbations. Remarkably, substantial flat-band features also persist in randomly edge-inflated graphs, even in the absence of translational symmetry. In particular, the number of zero-energy states is found to be well estimated by the matching deficiency $N-2ν(G)$, indicating that local tree-like structure continues to control the low-energy nullity. These results identify edge-inflated lattices as a broad class of systems in which geometry alone generates robust localization in both ordered and random settings.

</details>

### [5] [Light-Matter-Coupling formalism for magnons: probing quantum geometry with light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11931)
*Ying Shing Liu,Emil Viñas Boström,Michael A. Sentef,Silvia Viola Kusminskiy*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究建立了拉曼圆二色性（Raman circular dichroism）与磁振子量子几何之间的理论联系，为实验探测拓扑磁振子的量子几何特性提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑系统中集体磁激发的波函数具有非平凡的量子几何特性，但实验探测仍面临挑战。虽然拉曼圆二色性（Raman circular dichroism, RCD）已成为有前景的探测手段，但其与磁振子量子几何之间的基本联系尚未明确，且因磁振子呈电中性而变得复杂。

Method: 研究展示了在广泛条件下，Fleury-Loudon拉曼顶点可直接从有效磁振子哈密顿量的光-物质耦合展开中获得，绕过了基于虚拟电子过程的传统微观推导。这建立了RCD与磁振子能带贝里曲率（Berry curvature）之间的解析联系。

Result: 将该理论应用于单层CrI₃，预测了拓扑磁振子在RCD中的有限温度特征。这些结果为磁振子系统中的量子几何敏感光学探测建立了通用途径。

Conclusion: 研究确定了拉曼圆二色性与磁振子量子几何之间的联系条件与机制，为实验探测拓扑磁振子的量子几何特性提供了理论框架和具体预测。

Abstract: Nontrivial quantum geometry is a key feature of the wavefunctions of collective magnetic excitations in topological systems, but accessing it experimentally remains an open challenge. While Raman circular dichroism (RCD) has emerged as a promising probe, the fundamental link between the RCD and magnon quantum geometry has remained unsettled, and complicated by the fact that magnons are charge neutral. Here, we identify when and why this link exists. We show that, under broad conditions, the Fleury-Loudon Raman vertex can be obtained directly from a light-matter coupling expansion of the effective magnon Hamiltonian, bypassing the conventional microscopic derivation based on virtual electronic processes. This yields an analytical connection between the RCD and the Berry curvature of magnon bands. Applied to monolayer CrI\textsubscript{3}, our theory predicts finite temperature signatures of topological magnons in the RCD. These results establish a general route to quantum-geometry sensitive optical probes in magnonic systems.

</details>


### [6] [High-harmonic generation in systems with chiral Bloch states: application to rhombohedral graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11984)
*Jessica O. de Almeida,Wilton J. M. Kort-Kamp,Mathias S. Scheurer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了菱面体堆叠石墨烯（rhombohedral graphene）中的高次谐波产生（HHG）现象，揭示了布洛赫态的手性（chirality）和量子几何特性对非线性光学响应的关键影响，以及层数n与谐波阶次之间的线性标度关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯中的高次谐波产生（HHG）已被成功证明，而菱面体堆叠石墨烯作为关联多层石墨烯系统的代表性体系，其有趣的能带结构和增强的关联效应激发了对其非线性光学性质的研究兴趣。

Method: 研究分析了菱面体堆叠n层石墨烯系统中手性布洛赫态（chiral Bloch states）对高次谐波产生的影响，探讨了布洛赫态的"缠绕"（winding）特性、动量空间中的量子几何分布，以及相互作用诱导的能谷分裂效应。

Result: 发现布洛赫态的缠绕特性与层数n呈线性标度关系，主导谐波阶次也呈现相同标度；动量空间中的量子几何分布特征在强激光脉冲初期的时间依赖动量分布中留下印记；两个能谷的手性相反性在圆二色性（circular dichroism）的n依赖性中直接可见。

Conclusion: 菱面体石墨烯为探索丰富的非线性光学现象提供了一个有前景的平台，其手性布洛赫态和量子几何特性对高次谐波产生具有决定性影响，这些发现对光学信息处理应用具有潜在价值。

Abstract: Nonlinear light-matter interaction and, in particular, high-harmonic generation (HHG) are fundamentally interesting and frequently discussed as versatile probes of quantum materials with potential for optical information processing applications. Meanwhile, there has also been significant progress in graphene-based multilayer systems to engineer interesting band structures and boost correlation effects. Motivated by the successful demonstration of HHG in graphene, we here study this effect in rhombohedral stacks of $n$ layers of graphene, a recent very prominent representative of correlated multilayer graphene systems. We show how the chiral Bloch states of the valleys of this system crucially affect the HHG. The "winding" of the Bloch states scales linearly with $n$, just like the dominant harmonic order. The location of the strongest quantum geometry in momentum space on a ring of finite radius is shown to be imprinted on the time-dependent momentum distribution at the beginning of the strong laser pulse. We further demonstrate that the presence of an interaction-induced splitting of the two valleys leads to a complex interplay of the opposite chiralities of the two valleys, directly visible in the $n$ dependence of the circular dichroism. We also analyze the impact of doping and identify a quantity that tracks the net chirality of the occupied states. Our findings show that rhombohedral graphene constitutes a promising platform for exploring rich nonlinear optical phenomena.

</details>


### [7] [Polymer-free van der Waals assembly of 2D material heterostructures using muscovite crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12264)
*Ian Babich,Timofey M. Savilov,Natalia A. Mamchik,Kristina Vaklinova,Nansi Zhou,Denis S. Baranov,Dmitrii A. Litvinov,Virgil Gavriliuc,Yue Yuan,Amoz Chua,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Mario Lanza,Maciej Koperski,Kostya S. Novoselov,Alexey I. Berdyugin,Makars Šiškins*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于薄云母（mica）晶体的无聚合物转移技术，通过温度控制云母粘附力实现二维材料的确定性拾取、堆叠和释放，为范德华（van der Waals）异质结的自动化制备提供了洁净、无污染的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 范德华（vdW）异质结的原子层可调性要求界面原子级洁净，但当前基于聚合物的转移方法无法满足确定性和洁净度要求。需要开发一种能够动态、确定性控制粘附力且不留下有机污染物的解决方案。

Method: 采用薄云母（mica）晶体作为转移介质，通过温度控制云母的粘附特性，实现二维材料的确定性拾取、堆叠和释放。云母的晶体无机特性确保了原始界面并抑制应变。

Result: 该方法能够组装具有挑战性的范德华异质结，包括具有暴露导电层、莫尔（moiré）超晶格和悬浮膜的结构。与现有制造流程完全兼容，为自动化制备提供了可行策略。

Conclusion: 基于云母的无聚合物转移技术代表了范德华异质结制造向自动化发展的有前景策略，解决了当前方法在确定性和界面洁净度方面的关键限制。

Abstract: The advent of van der Waals (vdW) heterostructures has enabled formation of bespoke materials with atomic precision, where numerous quantum and topological phenomena have already been discovered. This atomic-layer tunability, however, comes at a cost: individual 2D layers must be picked up, moved, and placed in a deterministic manner while keeping their interfaces atomically clean. Recent advances in machine learning and robotics place even stronger emphasis on the deterministic aspect of vdW assembly. Current polymer-based transfer methods satisfy neither the determinism nor cleanliness requirements. To this end, solutions are needed where adhesion can be dynamically and deterministically controlled without leaving organic contamination. Here, we present a polymer free transfer technique employing thin muscovite (mica) crystals. Temperature control over mica adhesion enables deterministic pick-up, stacking, and release of 2D materials, while their crystalline, inorganic nature ensures pristine interfaces and suppresses strain. Fully compatible with existing fabrication workflows, this approach enables the assembly of demanding vdW heterostructures, including those with exposed conductive layers, moiré superlattices and suspended membranes. Our method represents a promising strategy for vdW heterostructure fabrication toward its automatization.

</details>


### [8] [Interplay of strain-induced axial gauge fields and intrinsic band-topology in the magnetoelectric conductivity of gapped nodal rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12275)
*Firdous Haidar,Muhammed Jaffar A.,Ipsita Mandal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文计算了具有理想带隙节点环（GNR）的半金属在三种不同平面霍尔构型下的磁电导率，特别关注应变诱导的轴向赝磁场（B₅）与贝里曲率（BC）、轨道磁矩（OMM）对齐所产生的独特输运特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索应变诱导的轴向赝磁场（axial pseudomagnetic field B₅）如何影响带隙节点环（gapped nodal ring）半金属的磁电输运性质，特别是其与贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和轨道磁矩（orbital magnetic moment）的对齐效应。

Method: 方法包括计算三种不同平面霍尔构型（planar-Hall configurations）下的磁电导率，在同时存在外电场E、磁场B和应变诱导轴向赝磁场B₅的条件下，将先前分析扩展到包含B₅效应。

Result: 结果显示B₅的涡旋状场线与贝里曲率和轨道磁矩共线对齐，导致B₅与BC或OMM诱导量的点积在费米面上与角度无关，产生线性于B₅的非零积分。此外，第一种构型中的部分平面霍尔电导完全不受应变影响。

Conclusion: 结论表明应变诱导特征在带隙节点环材料输运测量中具有可实验验证的独特信号，其中应变不敏感部分可作为拓扑输运的内部参考，为识别GNR材料中的应变效应提供了具体预测。

Abstract: We compute the magnetoelectric conductivity of a semimetal hosting an ideal gapped nodal ring (GNR) in three distinct planar-Hall configurations, in the simultaneous presence of an external electric field $\boldsymbol{E}$, a magnetic field $\boldsymbol{B}$, and a strain-induced axial pseudomagnetic field $\boldsymbol{B}_5$. The latter arises from a nonuniform lattice deformation and couples to antipodal points on the toroidal Fermi surface with opposite signs, reflecting its chiral nature. Extending our earlier analysis to include $\boldsymbol{B}_5$, we demonstrate how its vortex-like field lines -- co-aligned with the Berry curvature (BC) and orbital magnetic moment (OMM) -- imprint qualitatively distinct signatures on the conductivity tensor. In particular, this alignment causes the dot product of $\boldsymbol{B}_5$ with the BC or OMM-induced quantities to be angle-independent on the Fermi surface, generating a nonvanishing integral linear-in-$B_5$, which is not possible for isotropic nodal points harbouring BC-monopoles. We show that a part of the planar-Hall conductivity in the first set-up remains completely immune to strain, providing a strain-insensitive internal reference for topological transport. Our explicit analytical expressions offer concrete and experimentally testable predictions for identifying strain-induced signatures in transport measurements on GNR materials.

</details>


### [9] [Giant and Helical Exciton Dipole from Berry Curvature in Flat Chern Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12295)
*Kaijie Yang,Huiyuan Zheng,Xiaodong Xu,Di Xiao,Ting Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了莫尔平带（moiré flat bands）中激子（excitons）具有与莫尔晶格参数相当的巨大电偶极矩（~10^2德拜），并通过贝特-萨佩特方程（Bethe-Salpeter equations）揭示了外电场可调控激子从弗伦克尔（Frenkel）到万尼尔（Wannier）类型的转变，进而诱导偶极-偶极相互作用形成四极双激子（quadrupolar biexcitons）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索莫尔平带系统中激子的电偶极矩特性及其与能带拓扑的关联，为在太赫兹（terahertz）区域调控多体相互作用提供新途径。

Method: 通过求解贝特-萨佩特方程（Bethe-Salpeter equations）分析扭曲MoTe₂在空穴填充因子为1时的激子性质，研究外电场对激子类型转变的影响。

Result: 发现激子具有约10^2德拜的巨大电偶极矩，其最低能激子支在动量空间呈现面内螺旋纹理（helical texture）；外电场可诱导弗伦克尔到万尼尔激子转变并反转偶极纹理螺旋性，吸引性偶极-偶极相互作用导致四极双激子形成。

Conclusion: 研究确立了能带拓扑（band topology）作为调控激子偶极矩的可调参数，为在太赫兹区域操纵多体相互作用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We show that excitons forming between moiré flat Chern bands possess a substantial electric dipole moment comparable to the moiré lattice parameter times the elementary charge ($\sim10^2$ Debye). At a hole filling factor of one in twisted MoTe$_2$, the dipole moment of the lowest-energy exciton branch develops in-plane helical texture in momentum space from the intrinsic Berry curvature of electron and hole. By solving the Bethe-Salpeter equations, we demonstrate that an out-of-plane displacement field induces a Frenkel-to-Wannier exciton transition, accompanied by a reversal of the dipole texture helicity. The resulting attractive exciton dipole-dipole interactions lead to quadrupolar biexcitons that can be probed via two-photon spectroscopy. Our findings establish band topology as a tunable knob to engineer exciton dipole moments and pave the way to manipulate many-body interactions in the terahertz regime.

### [10] [A CMOS-compatible, scalable and compact magnetoelectric spin-torque microwave detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12366)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究展示了一种磁电（ME）自旋转矩微波探测器，该器件单片集成了磁电天线与磁性隧道结（MTJ）。器件直接将无线电磁信号转换为直流输出，其工作原理基于磁性隧道结中直流电流驱动的非相干磁化动力学与磁电天线在入射电磁波下产生的微波电压和应变的非线性耦合效应。

Result: 该器件在亚微瓦功率水平下实现了超过90 kV/W的灵敏度、3 pW*Hz^-0.5的噪声等效功率，以及0.4 mm²的紧凑尺寸。通过将磁电天线与多个磁性隧道结阵列集成，四磁性隧道结探测器的灵敏度超过400 kV/W，证明了设计的可扩展性。

Abstract: The development of compact and highly sensitive microwave detectors compatible with complementary-metal-oxide-semiconductor (CMOS) processes is an active research area but remains a major challenge in microwave technology. Spin-torque diodes (STDs) are emerging nanoscale spintronic devices capable of surpassing the theoretical thermodynamic sensitivity limits of Schottky diodes. However, their practical use in compact systems is limited by the need of external antennas or probes. Here, we demonstrate a magnetoelectric (ME) spin-torque microwave detector that monolithically integrates an ME antenna with a magnetic tunnel junction (MTJ). The device directly converts wireless electromagnetic signals into a DC output at sub-microwatt power levels, achieving a sensitivity greater than 90 kV/W, a noise equivalent power of 3 pW*Hz^-0.5, and a compact footprint of 0.4 mm^2. This performance is due to the nonlinear coupling between incoherent magnetization dynamics, driven by a DC current in the MTJ, and the combined effects of the microwave voltage and strain generated by the ME antenna under incident electromagnetic waves. We further show that this design is scalable, enabling the co-integration of an ME antenna with an array of MTJs. A detector incorporating four MTJs, for example, exhibits a sensitivity exceeding 400 kV/W. This work paves the way for a new generation of highly sensitive, compact and scalable microwave detectors that combine ME antennas and spintronic diodes.

Abstract: We report gate-controlled quantum-dot transport in a trilayer MoSe2 device that combines a graphite back gate beneath the active region, a separate global gate for conductive access regions, and local top finger gates. In the low-backgate regime, bias spectroscopy shows regular Coulomb-blockade diamonds characteristic of single-dot transport. As backgate is increased, additional low-bias structure develops beyond a simple single-dot pattern, indicating that the electrostatic landscape is reshaped and that a second dot becomes active in transport. In the higher-backgate regime, plunger-gate tuning and two-gate measurements establish a gate-reconfigurable double-dot configuration with two non-equivalent dots whose relative alignment and interdot coupling evolve with gate voltage. These results indicate that trilayer MoSe2 supports electrically reconfigurable single- and double-dot transport in the present device architecture.

Method: 采用量子化准正态模式（quantized quasinormal modes, QNMs）框架，通过非玻色子算符描述腔体与行波光子浴的相互作用。系统动力学完全由系统-浴关联函数描述，其中发射延迟效应被纳入考虑。

Abstract: A time-dependent theory for the interactions between spatially separated lossy cavities in a homogeneous background medium using quantized quasinormal modes (QNMs) is presented. The cavities interact via a bath of traveling photons, described by non-bosonic operators that are orthogonal to the open-cavity QNMs. The retarded (i.e., time-delayed) inter-cavity dynamics are fully described by system-bath correlation functions, in which the emission from one cavity appears as the input field for another. Coupling between quantum emitters (described as two-level systems), placed inside a cavity or embedded in an external medium, and the electromagnetic field (cavity modes and bath photons) is included in the theory, which gives rise to both bath-mediated and QNM-mediated interactions between the emitters.

Abstract: Moiré superlattices are generally assumed to act only at the interface where lattice mismatch or twist occurs. Here, we study charge transport in large-angle helical twisted trilayer graphene, where interlayer tunneling is strongly reduced. When only the top monolayer graphene is aligned with hBN, the electronic response reorganizes into a moiré-modulated monolayer and a remaining twisted bilayer graphene subsystem. Despite the absence of any explicit structural moiré in the twisted bilayer, we observe satellite-like features in its electronic response that run parallel to the primary spectrum and are locked to the density scale of the hBN/graphene moiré. These findings indicate that a moiré potential may not be confined to its structural interface and can, through electrostatic coupling, influence a spatially separated Dirac subsystem even in the absence of strong interlayer tunneling.

### [15] [Torsion-induced confinement and tunable nonlinear optical gain in a mesoscopic electron system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12664)

We show that the coupling between longitudinal motion and the geometric background produces an effective in-plane confinement, allowing bound states to emerge without the need for an external radial potential. Exact analytical solutions are obtained for the energy spectrum and radial wave functions, and these results are used to evaluate linear and third-order nonlinear absorption, changes in the refractive index, the photoionization cross section, and the oscillator strength. The combined action of torsion, magnetic field, and topological defect increases the interlevel spacing, compresses the radial electronic distribution, and breaks the dynamical symmetry between opposite angular-momentum channels, leading to strongly asymmetric and state-resolved optical spectra. Under intense optical excitation, the nonlinear contribution can overcome linear absorption, driving the system into a negative-absorption regime and enabling geometry-controlled optical gain. These results establish torsion and defect engineering as effective tools for tuning confinement, resonant energies, and selective amplification in mesoscopic nanophotonic platforms operating in the mid-infrared and terahertz ranges.

Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）作为一类具有零净磁化但呈现自旋劈裂能带结构的新型磁性材料，展现出独特的轨道-自旋锁定（orbital-spin locking）现象，需要建立其光自旋电子响应的微观理论描述。

Method: 从d波交变磁体的最小多轨道紧束缚哈密顿量出发，分析三阶注入电流和位移电流的一般公式；在δ键跳跃V_δ=0的理想情况下推导闭合解析解，在有限V_δ情况下给出V_δ≪V_π极限下的微扰解析解，并通过数值计算验证。

Result: 三阶光电流仅由量子度规和量子联络决定，不受贝里曲率污染；获得了V_δ=0时的闭合解析解和有限V_δ情况下的微扰解析解，建立了d波交变磁体三阶光自旋电子响应的完整理论描述。

Conclusion: 本研究基于微观模型为d波交变磁体的三阶光自旋电子响应提供了全面的理论框架，并为实验观测纯量子几何效应（pure quantum geometric effects）提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Altermagnets represent a novel category of magnetic materials characterized by zero net magnetization yet featuring spin-split band structures, and they demonstrate distinctive orbital-spin locking phenomena. Commencing from the minimal multi-orbital tight-binding Hamiltonian of d-wave altermagnets, we conduct an analysis of the general formulas for the third-order injection and shift currents. These currents are solely determined by the quantum metric and quantum connection, being free from Berry curvature contamination. In the ideal scenario where the $δ$-bond hopping $V_δ$ approaches zero ($V_δ= 0$), we derive closed-form analytical solutions for the third-order photoconductivities. For the general situation with a finite value of $V_δ$, we present a perturbative analytical solution within the limit of $V_δ\ll V_π$, and this solution is verified through numerical calculations. Our research establishes a comprehensive theoretical description of the third-order optospintronic responses in d-wave altermagnets based on a microscopic model. Moreover, it offers a viable approach for the experimental observation of pure quantum geometric effects.

### [18] [Heating Dynamics of Mesoscopic Electron Baths at High Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12810)
*F. Zanichelli,A. Veillon,C. Piquard,A. Aassime,Y. Sato,A. Cavanna,Y. Jin,J. Folk,U. Gennser,A. Anthore,F. Pierre*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验揭示了一种特定于介观尺度的两步热化过程：快速的初始温度跃变后，跟随一个持续数分钟的缓慢升温。这一观测结果可通过电子量子通道、冷声子以及金属岛中核自旋之间的热流平衡得到定量解释。

Conclusion: 所揭示的介观热化现象推动了量子热动力学领域的发展，突显了量子电路核心组件中热现象的独特性质。该研究对纳米器件热工程的意义包括在高磁场下奇异态的热表征。

Abstract: Quantum thermodynamics addresses the dynamics of heat flow in quantum devices driven out of equilibrium. Although mesoscopic circuits at low temperatures provide a flexible platform to explore this dynamics, experimental studies are wanting because thermal timescales in nanodevices are often too fast. Here we engineer and investigate with noise thermometry a mesoscopic thermal circuit where heat flows between electron, phonon and nuclear systems can occur on slower timescales. The central constituent of this device is a micrometer-scale metallic island electrically connected to large cold electron reservoirs through two to four ballistic quantum Hall channels, a component frequently used for exploring stationary thermal currents. We uncover a two-step thermalization process specific to the mesoscopic scale, involving a fast initial temperature step followed by a much slower rise extending over minutes. This observation is quantitatively accounted for by the balance between heat flows through electronic quantum channels, to cold phonons, and to the nuclear spins in the metallic island. The disclosed mesoscopic thermalization takes a step into the field of quantum thermo-\emph{dynamical} phenomena, highlighting their distinctive nature on a central constituent of quantum circuits. The implications for the thermal engineering of nanodevices include the thermal characterization of exotic states at high magnetic field.

### [20] [Dynamical Poles in Non-Hermitian Impurity Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12939)
*Ao Yang,Kai Zhang,Chen Fang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了非厄米（non-Hermitian）杂质散射中晚期指数信号与束缚态（bound states）的对应关系失效，提出了由格林函数（Green's function）解析延拓决定的动力学极点（dynamical poles）概念，这些极点与静态束缚态可能不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在厄米（Hermitian）杂质散射中，每个孤立的晚期指数信号都是束缚态的指纹，但本文旨在探究这种对应关系在非厄米能带中是否成立。

Method: 通过研究非厄米晶格中的单个杂质，分析格林函数在实时动力学中的解析延拓，识别出控制晚期信号的孤立复频率，即动力学极点。

Result: 发现动力学极点与静态束缚态不必重合：可能出现无束缚态对应的动力学极点，而静态束缚态可能在动力学上不可见。其余信号由复连续谱边缘（complex continuum edges）设定的非相干背景决定。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，非厄米杂质散射的组织结构由格林函数的实时解析结构决定，而非仅由静态本征值问题决定，这颠覆了厄米体系中的传统对应关系。

Abstract: In Hermitian impurity scattering, each isolated late-time exponential is the fingerprint of a bound state. We show that this correspondence breaks down in non-Hermitian bands. For a single impurity in a non-Hermitian lattice, the late-time signal is controlled by isolated complex frequencies selected by the analytic continuation of the Green's function relevant to real-time dynamics, which we term dynamical poles (DPs). DPs need not coincide with static bound states: one may appear without any bound-state counterpart, while a static bound state may be dynamically invisible. The remainder of the signal is an incoherent background set by complex continuum edges. Our results establish that the real-time analytic structure of the Green's function, not the static eigenvalue problem alone, organizes non-Hermitian impurity scattering.

</details>

Method: 研究采用微米分辨率光致发光测温技术，在砷化镓（GaAs）流体动力学窄通道（hydrodynamic narrow channel）中探测热电子（hot electrons）的传播行为。

Conclusion: 该工作通过实验观测和理论分析，在流体动力学电子输运体系中验证了维德曼-弗朗兹定律的违反，并揭示了窄缩结构对这一违反现象的关键影响。

Abstract: The Wiedemann--Franz law, which determines the universality of the ratio of thermal conductivity to electrical conductivity, is studied in the hydrodynamic electron transport regime, where electron--electron scattering predominates over scattering by disorder. In this case, the different relaxation of electric and thermal currents can lead to a violation of the Wiedemann--Franz law, which is expected to be even more pronounced in mesoscopic electron systems. This paper reports the propagation of hot electrons in a GaAs hydrodynamic narrow channel, studied using micrometer-resolution photoluminescence thermometry. A temperature dependence of the Lorenz number was obtained, indicating a violation of the Wiedemann--Franz law. The important role of narrow constrictions in this violation was also demonstrated, and theoretical arguments are presented.

### [22] [Sensitive dependence of Poor Man's Majorana modes on the length of superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12950)
*Zhi-Lei Zhang,Xin Yue,Guo-Jian Qiao,C. P. Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过将超导体建模为有限长度一维链，建立了量子点-超导体混合系统中Poor Man's Majorana模式（PMMs）存在的普适条件，发现PMMs数量对超导体长度高度敏感，并在有限长度情况下不存在分别局域于系统两端的PMMs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论常将超导体理想化为体系统或无限长链，或将其视为具有邻近诱导超导性的量子点，而实验中使用的是有限长度的超导段。这种理论与实验之间的差距促使研究者建立更符合实际系统的模型。

Method: 将超导体建模为有限长度的一维链，并将量子点与超导体置于同等地位进行处理。该方法适用于任意超导体长度、任意隧穿强度和磁场强度。

Result: 发现Poor Man's Majorana模式（PMMs）的数量对超导体长度高度敏感：在费米波长（约1Å）设定的周期内，PMMs数量在0到2之间振荡。在长超导体极限下，当两个量子点间的有效耦合变得可忽略时，会出现四个PMMs。在有限长度情况下，不存在分别局域于混合系统两端的PMMs。

Conclusion: 通过建立更符合实验条件的有限长度超导体模型，获得了PMMs存在的普适条件，并发现只有当磁场足够强时才能识别出近局域的PMMs。这种方法能够找到实际系统的广义"甜点"（sweet spot）。

Abstract: In a hybrid system where two quantum dots (QDs) are coupled to a conventional $s$-wave superconductor, Poor Man's Majorana modes (PMMs) have been proposed. Existing theories often idealize the superconductor (SC) as a bulk system or an infinitely long chain, or treat it as another quantum dot with proximity-induced superconductivity, while experiments employ superconducting segments of finite length. Here, we model the SC as a finite-length 1D chain and treat the QDs and SC on equal footing. We obtain the conditions for the existence of PMMs, valid for arbitrary SC length and applicable to arbitrary tunneling strengths and magnetic fields. We find that the number of PMMs is highly sensitive to the SC length: it oscillates between zero and two with a period set by the Fermi wavelength ($\sim1\,\textÅ$), while four PMMs appear in the long-SC limit where the effective coupling between the two QDs becomes negligible. We further demonstrate that the PMMs that are separately localized at the two ends of the hybrid system do not exist in the finite-length case. Consequently, only nearly localized PMMs can be identified when the magnetic field is strong enough. In this way, the generalized `sweet spot' of the practical system can be found.

### [23] [Spin-Momentum Decoupling in Quarkonium Hadronization: Polarization Quenching via Environment-Induced Decoherence in Jets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11847)
*Yi Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种有效的开放量子系统范式，解释高横向动量下重夸克偶素极化的抑制现象。通过将强色电场作为动态退相干环境，并引入有效温度参数，预测了极化和方位各向异性同时淬灭至最大混合态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高横向动量下重夸克偶素极化的抑制是量子色动力学中的一个持久难题。CMS合作组最近观测到的Υ(nS)的"软"碎裂为解释历史上的无极化异常提供了关键相空间权重。

Method: 采用有效的开放量子系统范式，论证重夸克自旋态与其宏观动量在强子化过程中有效解耦。保留短距离非相对论性QCD微扰计算作为运动学基线，使用视界启发的图像作为物理参数化，推导出由软伴随部分子多重数驱动的有效温度Teff(z) ∝ √ln(1/z)。

Result: 通过将有效温度纳入Lindblad耗散框架，预测极化和方位各向异性同时淬灭至最大混合态。识别碎裂分数z = pT^Q/pT^jet作为关键控制变量，提出可测试的预测是在固定夸克偶素和喷注pT区间内λθ、λφ和λ̃的z依赖抑制。

Conclusion: 该框架为解释高pT下重夸克偶素极化抑制提供了自洽的理论解释，将碎裂分数z作为关键变量，并提出了可通过实验验证的预测，为理解强子化过程中的退相干机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: The suppression of heavy quarkonium polarization at high transverse momentum ($p_T$) remains a persistent puzzle in quantum chromodynamics (QCD). We propose an effective open-quantum-system paradigm demonstrating that the heavy quark spin state and its macroscopic momentum effectively decouple during hadronization. By retaining the short-distance non-relativistic QCD (NRQCD) perturbative calculations as a kinematic baseline, we argue that the immense kinematic inertia at high $p_T$ parametrically preserves the power-law momentum spectrum. Concurrently, the intense, stochastic chromo-electric background within a fragmenting jet acts as a dynamic decoherence environment. Using a horizon-inspired picture as a physically motivated parametrization, we derive an effective temperature $T_{\text{eff}}(z) \propto \sqrt{\ln(1/z)}$ driven by the multiplicity of soft accompanying partons. By incorporating this effective temperature into a Lindblad dissipation framework, we predict a simultaneous quenching of the polar and azimuthal anisotropies towards a maximally mixed state. Crucially, the recently observed ``soft'' fragmentation of $Υ(nS)$ by the CMS Collaboration provides a highly consistent phase-space weighting required in our framework to explain the historical inclusive unpolarized anomaly. Identifying the fragmentation fraction $z=p_T^{\mathcal{Q}}/p_T^{\text{jet}}$ as the critical control variable, we propose that a key testable prediction is the simultaneous $z$-dependent suppression of $λ_θ$, $λ_φ$, and $\tildeλ$ in fixed quarkonium and jet $p_T$ bins.

### [24] [Grand Unified Origin of Enhanced Scalar Couplings: Connecting Radiative Electroweak Symmetry Breaking to SO(10) Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11851)
*Farrukh A. Chishtie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出，SO(10)大统一理论（grand unification）自然产生辐射电弱对称性破缺（radiatively broken electroweak symmetry, RBEWS）所需的增强希格斯四次耦合（enhanced Higgs quartic coupling）。通过方案转换和尺度演化，RBEWS预测的耦合增强因子k≈6.0-6.4在Mt处对应紫外朗道极点（UV Landau pole）接近GUT尺度，表明该极点标志着标准模型有效描述必须嵌入完整SO(10)结构的尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解释辐射电弱对称性破缺（RBEWS）所需的增强希格斯四次耦合（enhanced Higgs quartic coupling）如何从SO(10)大统一理论（grand unification）中自然产生。先前研究表明，耦合增强因子k≳1.03会导致绝对真空稳定性，并在GUT尺度附近出现紫外朗道极点（UV Landau pole）。

Method: 通过将Steele和Wang的RBEWS预测e125=7.2从Coleman-Weinberg方案（Coleman-Weinberg scheme）在电弱真空期望值（electroweak VEV）处转换到$\overline{\rm MS}$方案在Mt处，进行方案转换（scheme conversion）和尺度依赖的比值演化（scale-dependent ratio evolution）。推导包含$\mathbf{10}_H$、$\mathbf{\overline{126}}_H$和$\mathbf{45}_H$表示的SO(10)标量场（scalar sectors）的阈值修正（threshold corrections）。

Result: RBEWS预测在Mt处产生k(Mt)≈6.0-6.4的耦合增强因子，对应紫外极点（UV pole）ΛUV∼1.5-2×10¹⁶ GeV，与GUT尺度MGUT∼2×10¹⁶ GeV惊人接近。SO(10)标量场中轻希格斯双重态（light Higgs doublet）与重GUT标量场（heavy GUT scalars）之间的门户耦合（portal couplings）可在匹配尺度（matching scale）产生k∼5-10量级的增强因子。

Conclusion: 紫外极点（UV pole）标志着标准模型有效描述必须嵌入完整SO(10)结构的尺度。在经典尺度不变的GUT标量势（classically scale-invariant GUT scalar potential）中运行的Coleman-Weinberg机制为RBEWS以及GUT尺度与电弱尺度之间的层次结构（hierarchy）提供了动力学起源（dynamical origin）。

Abstract: We propose that the enhanced Higgs quartic coupling required by radiatively broken electroweak symmetry (RBEWS) emerges naturally from SO(10) grand unification. Our previous analysis demonstrated that a coupling enhancement factor $k = λ_{\rm enhanced}/λ_{\rm SM}$ leads to absolute vacuum stability with a UV Landau pole near the GUT scale for $k \gtrsim 1.03$. The RBEWS prediction $e_{125} = 7.2$ of Steele and Wang, when properly translated from the Coleman-Weinberg scheme at the electroweak VEV to the $\overline{\rm MS}$ scheme at $M_t$ via scheme conversion and scale-dependent ratio evolution, yields $k(M_t) \approx 6.0$--$6.4$, corresponding to a UV pole at $Λ_{\rm UV} \sim {1.5\text{--}2} \times 10^{16}$~GeV -- remarkably close to the GUT scale $M_{\rm GUT} \sim 2 \times 10^{16}$~GeV. We argue this coincidence is not accidental: the UV pole signals the scale where the Standard Model effective description must be embedded into the full SO(10) structure. We derive threshold corrections from SO(10) scalar sectors containing $\mathbf{10}_H$, $\mathbf{\overline{126}}_H$, and $\mathbf{45}_H$ representations, showing that portal couplings between the light Higgs doublet and heavy GUT scalars can generate enhancement factors of order $k \sim 5$--$10$ at the matching scale. The Coleman-Weinberg mechanism operating within a classically scale-invariant GUT scalar potential provides a dynamical origin for both RBEWS and the hierarchy between $M_{\rm GUT}$ and the electroweak scale.

### [25] [ALP production in Lepton Flavour Violating meson, tau and gauge boson decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11889)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在轴子样粒子（ALPs）质量超过μ子阈值的区域，奇异μ子衰变μ→ea的强约束不再适用，而衰变通道a→eμ变得运动学可及，这为基于虚拟μ子产生的ALPs研究提供了新机遇。

Result: a→eμ衰变产生显著的LFV信号且标准模型背景可忽略，结合当前低能约束评估了未来高能e⁺e⁻对撞机、Belle II和STCF等味工厂、NA62等固定靶实验以及SHiP等质子束流倾卸装置的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 介子、规范玻色子、夸克偶素和τ衰变（含位移顶点）中的LFV ALPs产生是测试μ子质量阈值以上ALPs与带电轻子相互作用的有前景且尚未充分探索的途径。

Abstract: In this paper we study axion-like particles (ALPs) with lepton-flavour-violating (LFV) couplings in the mass regime above the muon threshold, $m_a>m_μ$, where the strong bound from the exotic muon decay $μ\to ea$ no longer apply and the decay channel $a\to eμ$ becomes kinematically accessible. In this region, the ALP typically decays promptly, motivating new search strategies based on its production in decays involving virtual muons. We analyse charged-meson and $W$ decays, neutral-current processes such as $Z$ and quarkonium decays, and, when couplings to the third generation are present, LFV $τ$ decays. The subsequent decay $a\to eμ$ leads to striking LFV signatures with negligible Standard Model backgrounds. Combining these production modes with current low-energy constraints, we assess the sensitivity of future high-energy $e^+e^-$ colliders, flavour factories such as Belle II and STCF, fixed-target experiments such as NA62, and proton beam-dump facilities such as SHiP. Overall, our results identify LFV ALP production in meson, gauge-boson, quarkonium and $τ$ decays (with displaced vertices) as a promising and largely unexplored avenue to test ALP interactions with charged leptons above the muon mass threshold.

</details>


### [26] [Deciphering the nature of $P^Σ_{ψs}$ pentaquarks in the light of their electromagnetic multipole moments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12533)
*Ulaş Özdem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次计算了Σ型奇异隐粲五夸克态$P^Σ_{ψs}$的电磁多极矩，包括磁偶极矩、电四极矩和磁八极矩，并提供了首个夸克味道分解分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索奇异隐粲五夸克态$P^Σ_{ψs}$的电磁性质，这些态由$Σ^+$、$Σ^0$、$Σ^-$同位旋三重态组成。通过计算电磁多极矩，可以深入了解这些奇特强子的内部结构和夸克组分。

Method: 采用QCD光锥求和规则（QCD light-cone sum rules）方法，构建了六种（自旋-1/2）和七种（自旋-3/2）由双夸克-双夸克-反夸克算符组成的插值流。计算了所有通道的磁偶极矩$μ$，以及自旋-3/2态的电四极矩${\cal Q}$和磁八极矩${\cal O}$。

Result: 标量双夸克流产生粲夸克主导、味道不敏感的矩（自旋-1/2的$μ\in[-1.92,-1.21]μ_N$，自旋-3/2的$|μ|\lesssim1.2μ_N$），符合重夸克自旋对称性。轴矢量双夸克流产生更大、味道敏感的矩，符号反转由$e_u/e_d=-2$控制。电四极矩方面，标量双夸克流给出扁椭球变形（$Q_0\approx-2.0\times10^{-2}{\rm fm}^2$），而双轴矢量双夸克流预测长椭球值高达$Q_0=+8.0\times10^{-2}{\rm fm}^2$。

Conclusion: 研究首次计算了奇异隐粲五夸克态的电磁多极矩，为区分不同理论模型提供了四个判别标准：自旋-1/2态的$|μ|\gtrsim3μ_N$；自旋-3/2态$[su][uc]\bar{c}$的$μ$符号；非零电四极矩${\cal Q}$（在$S$-波分子态中消失）；以及${\cal Q}$-${\cal O}$符号相关性，可用于探测$1/m_q$权重效应。

Abstract: We calculate electromagnetic multipole moments of $Σ$-type strange hidden-charm pentaquarks $P^Σ_{ψs}$ (isospin triplet $Σ^+,Σ^0,Σ^-$) using QCD light-cone sum rules, with six (spin-1/2) and seven (spin-3/2) interpolating currents built from diquark-diquark-antiquark operators. We compute magnetic dipole $μ$ for all channels and, for spin-3/2, electric quadrupole ${\cal Q}$ and magnetic octupole ${\cal O}$ moments (first computation), and give the first quark-flavor decomposition. Scalar diquark currents yield charm-dominated, flavor-insensitive moments ($μ\in[-1.92,-1.21]μ_N$ for spin-1/2, $|μ|\lesssim1.2μ_N$ for spin-3/2), consistent with heavy-quark spin symmetry. Axial-vector diquark currents produce larger, flavor-sensitive moments with sign reversals governed by $e_u/e_d=-2$. For ${\cal Q}$, scalar-diquark currents give oblate deformations ($Q_0\approx-2.0\times10^{-2}{\rm fm}^2$) dominated by charm, while two-axial-vector-diquark currents predict prolate values up to $Q_0=+8.0\times10^{-2}{\rm fm}^2$, with sign reversal for $[su][uc]\bar{c}$ in two currents. Currents with scalar antiquark coupling yield a topology-independent octupole ${\cal O}\approx-0.25\times10^{-3}{\rm fm}^3$, a lattice QCD benchmark. Comparison with constituent quark models identifies four discriminants: $|μ|\gtrsim3μ_N$ in spin-1/2; sign of $μ$ for $[su][uc]\bar{c}$ in spin-3/2; non-zero ${\cal Q}$ (vanishes in $S$-wave molecules); and the ${\cal Q}$-${\cal O}$ sign correlation, probing $1/m_q$ weighting.

</details>


### [27] [Open-flavor threshold effects on quarkonium spectrum in the BOEFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12603)
*Nora Brambilla,Abhishek Mohapatra,Tommaso Scirpa,Antonio Vairo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究使用玻恩-奥本海默有效场论（BOEFT）重新审视了开味阈（open-flavor thresholds）对夸克偶素（quarkonium）谱的影响，通过求解耦合薛定谔方程量化了阈值效应，并与实验数据和传统$^3P_0$模型进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自康奈尔势（Cornell potential）引入以来，开味阈对夸克偶素谱的影响一直是研究课题，主要通过$^3P_0$模型等唯象方法量化。本研究旨在使用从QCD系统推导出的玻恩-奥本海默有效场论（BOEFT）重新审视这一问题。

Method: 采用玻恩-奥本海默有效场论（Born--Oppenheimer effective field theory, BOEFT），该理论通过利用能标和对称性的层次结构从QCD系统推导。在BOEFT框架内，开味阈效应源于具有相同玻恩-奥本海默量子数的夸克偶素和四夸克静态势（tetraquark static potentials）之间的混合。静态势的形状由格点QCD（lattice QCD）计算约束，并考虑了BOEFT四夸克静态势在短距离和长距离的独特行为。

Result: 通过求解BOEFT决定的耦合薛定谔方程（coupled Schrödinger equations）量化阈值效应，唯一自由参数（伴随介子质量）固定为$χ_{c1}(3872)$态的质量。首次在包含物理阈值自旋劈裂（spin splittings）的情况下求解方程，并通过将相同阈值效应计算为夸克偶素传播子的自能修正（self-energy corrections）验证结果。与现有实验数据和先前文献进行了比较。

Conclusion: 研究提供了$^3P_0$模型中出现的对产生常数$γ$的场论解释（field-theoretical interpretation），系统量化了开味阈对夸克偶素谱的影响，为理解阈值效应提供了基于QCD的有效场论框架。

Abstract: The impact of open-flavor thresholds on the quarkonium spectrum has been a subject of study since the introduction of the Cornell potential and has been quantified through various phenomenological approaches, most notably the $^3P_0$ model. We revisit this problem using the Born--Oppenheimer effective field theory (BOEFT), an effective field theory systematically derived from QCD by exploiting hierarchies of energy scales and symmetries. Within the BOEFT, open-flavor threshold effects emerge from the mixing between quarkonium and tetraquark static potentials sharing the same Born--Oppenheimer quantum numbers. The shapes of the static potentials are constrained by lattice QCD calculations. Furthermore, we account for the distinctive behavior of the BOEFT tetraquark static potentials at short and large distances: at short distances they are repulsive, reflecting the color-octet configuration of the heavy quark-antiquark pair, while at large distances they asymptotically approach heavy-light meson-antimeson thresholds. To quantify threshold effects on the quarkonium spectrum below threshold, we solve a set of coupled Schrödinger equations dictated by the BOEFT, whose only free parameter, the adjoint meson mass, is fixed to the mass of the $χ_{c1}(3872)$ state. These coupled equations are solved both in the spin-isospin averaged threshold limit and, for the first time, including the spin splittings of the physical thresholds. We validate our results by computing the same threshold effects as self-energy corrections to the quarkonium propagator. We compare our predictions with existing experimental data and previous literature. Finally, we provide a field-theoretical interpretation of the pair-creation constant $γ$ appearing in the $^3P_0$ model.

</details>


### [28] [Mass creation by the strong interaction: Glueballs -- status and perspectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12895)
*Ulrich Wiedner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 胶球（glueball）作为强相互作用中由多个胶子（gluon）组成的复合粒子，其质量产生机制为研究强相互作用粒子的质量起源提供了独特视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶球代表了自然界强相互作用的一个迷人方面。胶子作为强相互作用的媒介粒子，虽然本身无质量，但具有独特的色荷（color charge）属性，这为研究质量产生机制提供了理想系统。

Method: 本文通过理论分析胶球的基本性质进行研究。重点探讨了色荷相互作用如何使原本无质量的胶子组合形成有质量的胶球，这一过程类比了电磁相互作用中的电荷概念。

Result: 分析表明，胶球的质量源于色荷之间的相互作用。虽然单个胶子无质量，但多个胶子通过色荷相互作用形成的束缚态——胶球——成为有质量物体。

Conclusion: 胶球为研究强相互作用粒子的质量创造（mass creation）提供了独特途径。通过研究胶球的质量产生机制，可以深入理解强相互作用中质量起源的基本物理过程。

Abstract: Glueballs represent a fascinating aspect of the strong interaction in nature. Gluons that serve as the mediators of the strong interaction are massless particles, but they possess a property unique to the strong interaction called color charge, which is analogous to electric charge in the electromagnetic interaction. Glueballs are composed of multiple gluons and would be massless without color charges. The interaction of the color charges, however, makes glueballs becoming massive objects. Glueballs thus offer a unique way to study the mass creation of strongly interacting particles.

</details>

*Hao Chen,Yibei Li*

Main category: hep-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能量关联子为量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics）提供了干净的探针，是严格研究非微扰幂次修正的理想实验室。最近发现的线性修正具有普适反常标度现象，指向了深刻的底层理论结构。

Method: 使用光射线算符（light-ray operators）研究能量-能量关联子（energy-energy correlator）中的现象。通过显式的圈计算（loop calculation），推导了一圈反常维度（one-loop anomalous dimension）。

Result: 揭示了线性修正普适反常标度的量子场论起源，发现双喷注算符（dijet operator）必须与特定的三喷注分量（triple-jet component）结合。这提供了连接算符理论与高精度对撞机现象学的第一性原理框架。

Conclusion: 研究建立了能量关联子中线性修正反常标度现象的理论基础，为理解量子色动力学的非微扰效应提供了新的理论框架，并搭建了算符理论与实验现象学之间的桥梁。

Abstract: Energy correlators offer a clean probe of quantum chromodynamics, serving as an ideal laboratory to rigorously investigate non-perturbative power corrections. The recent discovery that linear corrections exhibit a universal anomalous scaling points to a deep, underlying theoretical structure. We uncover the quantum field-theoretic origin of this phenomenon in the energy-energy correlator using light-ray operators. Through an explicit loop calculation, we derive the one-loop anomalous dimension, revealing that the dijet operator must be combined with a specific triple-jet component. This provides a first-principles framework that connects operator theory with high-precision collider phenomenology.

### [30] [Perspective: Measuring physical entropy out of equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11953)
*Haim Diamant,Gil Ariel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 熵作为反映物质状态变化的关键热力学变量，在非平衡稳态中通过其与信息的关系仍能良好定义。然而，将这一关系应用于物理系统面临挑战，因为需要获取微观高维连续分布的信息，而这通常是无法实现的。

Method: 论文综述了一组测量非平衡稳态或吸收态熵的新方法。这些方法强调物理系统（包括非平衡系统）的熵估计与一般统计熵估计和推断问题存在本质区别。

Result: 这些新方法已成功应用于识别多种系统中的动态结构和相变，包括堵塞堆积（jammed packings）和集群细菌（swarming bacteria）等不同领域。

Conclusion: 作者指出了当前和未来有前景的研究方向，强调非平衡物理系统中熵测量的特殊挑战和应用价值。

Abstract: Entropy is one of the key thermodynamic variables reflecting changes in the state of matter. Unlike other thermodynamic variables, it is well-defined also for nonequilibrium steady states through its relation to information. Applying this relation to physical systems is an ongoing challenge, as it requires knowledge of microscopic high-dimensional continuous distributions which is generally unattainable. A set of new approaches for the measurement of entropy in nonequilibrium steady or absorbing states have been developed and successfully applied to identify dynamic structures and transitions in diverse systems, ranging from jammed packings to swarming bacteria. We briefly review these approaches, emphasizing why applications to physical systems, including those out of equilibrium, is substantially different from the general statistical challenge of entropy estimation and inference. We point at promising current and future directions.

### [31] [Steady-State Equilibrium and Nonequilibrium Noisy Network Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12225)
*Pik-Yin Lai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文理论研究了网络在稳定、无噪声稳态附近的涨落动力学，识别了非平衡动力学的多种成因，推导了噪声网络在平衡态下的等价条件，并建立了与物理布朗动力学和网络重构的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在理论探究网络在稳定、无噪声稳态（noise-free steady state）附近的涨落动力学，识别导致非平衡动力学的各种因素，并建立与物理系统布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）的联系。

Method: 通过分析网络连接特性和噪声协方差矩阵（noise covariance matrices）的对称性，推导噪声网络在平衡态下的等价条件；从线性化涨落噪声网络动力学的视角分析过阻尼布朗动力学（overdamped Brownian dynamics）。

Result: 推导出非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady state, NESS）动力学的分析框架，证明物理系统中的过阻尼布朗动力学是广义噪声有向网络在非平衡稳态下的特例，并建立了广义非平衡噪声网络动力学的涨落耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）。

Conclusion: 该研究为网络涨落动力学提供了理论框架，建立了噪声网络动力学与物理布朗动力学之间的联系，并通过数值模拟验证了理论结果，为从时间序列数据重建网络提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The fluctuating dynamics of a network about its stable, noise-free steady state are theoretically investigated. Various causes of non-equilibrium dynamics are identified in terms of the properties and symmetry of the network connections and the noise covariance matrices. Several equivalent conditions are derived for the dynamics of the noisy network at equilibrium. In particular, non-equilibrium steady state (NESS) dynamics are analyzed in terms of the steady-state probability current and the drift velocity relative to the effective potential surface. Conventional physical Brownian dynamics for overdamped fluctuating dynamics is analyzed from the perspective of the linearized fluctuating noisy network dynamics. Connection with the network reconstruction from time-series data is discussed. It is demonstrated that the overdamped Brownian dynamics in the physical system is a special case of the general noisy directed network in a NESS. Furthermore, a general fluctuation-dissipation relation is derived for the general non-equilibrium noisy network dynamics. These theoretical results are verified by numerical simulations.

</details>


### [32] [Finite temperature correlation functions of the sine--Gordon model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12585)
*M. Tóth,J. H. Pixley,G. Takács,M. Kormos*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究采用随机曲面方法（Method of Random Surfaces, MRS）计算了sine-Gordon模型在有限温度下的两点及高阶关联函数，验证了该方法在传统方法失效的中等参数区间的可靠性，并推导了满足选择规则的任意N点函数的精确结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: sine-Gordon模型作为1+1维量子场论的基础模型，在凝聚态物理中有广泛应用。尽管该模型具有可积性，但其有限温度行为的表征仍是一个重要的理论挑战，传统的形式因子展开和半经典方法在中等参数区间不适用。

Method: 研究采用先前发展的随机曲面方法（Method of Random Surfaces, MRS）来评估两点及高阶关联函数。该方法通过与已知解析极限进行交叉验证，确保其在传统方法失效的中等参数区间提供可靠的非微扰数据。

Result: MRS方法在传统形式因子展开和半经典方法不适用的中间参数区间提供了可靠的关联函数数据。研究推导了满足适当选择规则的任意N点函数的精确结果，为有限温度下复杂多点可观测量提供了直接计算方法。同时，研究表征了关联的非高斯性，结果显示与理论预期一致。

Conclusion: 随机曲面方法为sine-Gordon模型的有限温度关联函数提供了可靠的非微扰计算框架，特别是在传统方法失效的参数区间。该方法不仅适用于两点函数，还可通过推导的精确结果计算任意N点函数，为研究复杂多体关联提供了有效工具。

Abstract: The sine-Gordon model serves as a foundational $1+1$-dimensional quantum field theory with numerous applications in condensed matter physics. Despite its integrability, characterizing its finite-temperature behavior remains a significant theoretical challenge. Here we use the previously developed Method of Random Surfaces (MRS) to evaluate two-point and higher-order correlation functions. We cross-check these results with known analytical limits, demonstrating that the MRS provides reliable, non-perturbative data in intermediate regimes where traditional form-factor expansions and semiclassical methods are inapplicable. Furthermore, we derive an exact result for arbitrary $N$-point functions satisfying an appropriate selection rule, providing a direct computational method for complex multi-point observables at finite temperature. We also characterize the non-Gaussianity of correlations and demonstrate that the results align with intuitive theoretical expectations.

### [33] [Generalized BChS Model with Group Interactions: Shift in the Critical Point and Mean-Field Ising Universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12430)
*Amit Pradhan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了广义化的Biswas-Chatterjee-Sen (BChS)模型，引入q体相互作用，发现高阶相互作用改变了相变位置但不改变普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于扩展原始的BChS模型，从两体相互作用推广到q体相互作用，探索高阶相互作用对系统相变行为的影响。

Method: 在平均场框架下，推导了临界噪声p_c(q)的精确表达式，并通过有限尺寸标度分析Binder累积量、序参量及其涨落来研究临界行为。

Result: 临界噪声p_c(q)随q单调增加，在大q极限下趋近于1/2；临界行为在所有q值下保持不变，序参量标度为(p_c(q)-p)^{1/2}，弛豫时间标度发散为|p-p_c(q)|^{-1}。

Conclusion: 高阶相互作用改变了相变位置但不改变其普适类，系统在所有q值下都属于平均场伊辛（mean-field Ising）普适类。

Abstract: We introduce a generalized version of the Biswas-Chatterjee-Sen (BChS) model \cite{Biswas} with group interactions of size $q$, extending the original pairwise interaction dynamics. Within a mean-field framework, we derive an exact expression for the critical noise $p_c(q)$, showing that it increases monotonically with $q$ and approaches $1/2$ in the large-$q$ limit, consistent with a Gaussian approximation. Despite this shift in the phase boundary, the critical behavior remains unchanged across all $q$: the order parameter scales as $(p_c(q)-p)^{1/2}$, and the relaxation timescale diverges as $|p-p_c(q)|^{-1}$, identical to the original BChS model \cite{Biswas}. Finite-size scaling of the Binder cumulant, order parameter, and its fluctuations confirm that the system belongs to the mean-field Ising universality class for all $q$. Our results demonstrate that higher-order interactions modify the location of the transition without altering its universality class.

</details>

### [34] [Orbit-Level Transfer Matrix for the 3D Fourier-Galerkin Navier-Stokes System on the Periodic Torus: Explicit Orbit-Triad Incidence Bounds and Deterministic Row-Sum Estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12188)
*Oleg Kiriukhin*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程在周期性环面上经完整八面体对称群约化后的立方Fourier-Galerkin截断系统，通过面归一化分解将局部计数问题简化为经典二平方表示函数，获得轨道-三元组关联的阶数估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程在周期性环面上经完整八面体对称群$O_h$约化后的立方Fourier-Galerkin截断系统，旨在分析非线性相互作用在轨道层面的转移机制。

Method: 采用面归一化分解（face-normalized decomposition）将局部计数问题简化为经典二平方表示函数，利用本文发展的壳层计数论证（shell-counting argument）获得关联界估计；同时推导精确的轨道层面熵恒等式和代数分解$M_N(u)=A_N(u)+V_N(u)$。

Result: 获得轨道-三元组关联的阶数估计为$N^{4+\varepsilon}$，推导出精确的轨道层面熵恒等式和代数分解$M_N(u)=A_N(u)+V_N(u)$，并在指定指数范围内得到原始矩阵$M_N(u)$的确定性Sobolev行和界。

Conclusion: 这些结果为截断系统中的非线性转移提供了轨道层面的描述，通过对称约化和组合计数方法建立了三维Navier-Stokes方程截断系统的数学分析框架。

Abstract: I study the cubic Fourier-Galerkin truncation of the three-dimensional (3D) incompressible Navier-Stokes equations on the periodic torus after reduction by the full octahedral symmetry group $O_h$. The nonlinear interaction is encoded by a state-dependent orbit-level transfer matrix $M_N(u)$, and the main discrete problem is to estimate orbit-triad incidences in shell slices of translated cubes. Using a face-normalized decomposition, I reduce the local counting problem to the classical two-squares representation function and obtain an incidence bound of order $N^{4+\varepsilon}$ by the shell-counting argument developed in this manuscript. I also derive the exact orbit-level enstrophy identity, the algebraic decomposition $M_N(u)=A_N(u)+V_N(u)$, and deterministic Sobolev row-sum bounds for the raw matrix $M_N(u)$ in the stated range of exponents. These results give an orbit-level description of nonlinear transfer in the truncated system.

### [35] [Effective Dynamics for the Bose Polaron in the Large-Volume Mean-Field Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11976)
*Jonas Lampart,Peter Pickl,Siegfried Spruck*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了玻色极化子（Bose polaron）系统的动力学，在平均场标度下推导了从微观动力学到平移不变Bogoliubov-Fröhlich哈密顿量的有效描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究玻色极化子系统的动力学行为，该系统由N个玻色子在杂质粒子存在下演化组成。关注高密度ρ和大体积Λ的极限情况，其中几乎所有玻色子初始都处于玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚态（Bose-Einstein condensate）。

Method: 采用平均场标度（mean-field scaling）分析，在初始高密度和大体积条件下，从微观动力学出发推导有效描述。考虑联合极限：密度ρ和体积Λ同时趋于无穷大，但满足约束条件Λ³ ≪ ρ。

Result: 在密度和体积的联合极限下，推导出平移不变的Bogoliubov-Fröhlich哈密顿量（translation-invariant Bogoliubov-Fröhlich Hamiltonian）作为有效描述。该哈密顿量将激发量子场与杂质粒子线性耦合。

Conclusion: 成功建立了玻色极化子系统从微观动力学到有效场论描述的数学框架，为研究杂质与玻色子凝聚体相互作用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We consider the dynamics of the Bose polaron system, a dense quantum gas consisting of $N$ bosons evolving in $\mathbb{R}^3$ in the presence of an impurity particle. The system is studied in the mean-field scaling with initially high density $ρ$ and large volume $Λ$ of the gas. In the initial state, almost all bosons are in the Bose-Einstein condensate, with a few excitations. We derive from the microscopic dynamics, in the joint limit of large densities and volumes, with the constraint $Λ^3 \ll ρ$, the effective description by the translation-invariant Bogoliubov-Fröhlich Hamiltonian, which couples the quantum field of excitations linearly to the impurity particle.

### [36] [Quantum mechanical model for charge excitation: Surface binding and dispersion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12111)
*Dionisios Margetis*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 通过理想化量子力学模型，本文精确描述了三维空间中固定平面附近非延迟电磁表面波的色散关系，揭示了表面等离子体激元（surface plasmon）形成中微观尺度（包括约束长度）的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在通过理想化量子力学模型，正式描述三维空间中固定平面附近非延迟电磁表面波的色散关系，以捕捉表面等离子体激元（surface plasmon）这一集体低能电荷激发形成过程中微观尺度（包括约束长度）的相互作用。

Method: 从三维时间相关Hartree型方程出发，该模型考虑了粒子与平面的束缚以及相对于基态的诱导电荷密度产生的排斥库仑相互作用。通过线性化运动方程，建立了垂直平面方向（z坐标）粒子波函数散射振幅的齐次积分方程。对于与负δ函数成正比的束缚势和z对称波函数，应用正z方向的拉普拉斯变换，将积分方程转换为包含变换解多个值的函数方程。

Result: 通过Mittag-Leffler定理，以快速收敛级数的形式精确导出了散射振幅和色散关系。在半经典区域，结果提供了能量激发谱的渐近展开，其主导项与基于投影欧拉-泊松系统的经典流体动力学模型预测一致。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了描述表面等离子体激元色散关系的精确量子力学模型，在半经典极限下与经典流体动力学模型预测相符，为理解微观尺度在表面等离子体形成中的作用提供了理论框架。

Abstract: By an idealized quantum mechanical model, we formally describe the dispersion of nonretarded electromagnetic surface waves that express charge density oscillations near a fixed plane in three spatial dimensions (3D) at zero temperature. Our goal is to capture the interplay of microscopic scales that include a confinement length in the emergence of the surface plasmon, a collective low-energy charge excitation in the vicinity of the plane. We start with a time-dependent Hartree-type equation in 3D. This model accounts for particle binding to the plane and the repulsive Coulomb interaction associated with the induced charge density relative to the ground state. By linearizing the equation of motion, we formulate a homogeneous integral equation for the scattering amplitude of the particle wave function in the (z-) coordinate vertical to the plane. For a binding potential proportional to a negative delta function and symmetric-in-z wave function, we apply the Laplace transform with respect to positive z and convert the integral equation into a functional equation that involves several values of the transformed solution. The scattering amplitude and dispersion relation are derived exactly in terms of rapidly convergent series via the Mittag-Leffler theorem. In the semiclassical regime, our result furnishes an asymptotic expansion for the energy excitation spectrum. The leading-order term is found in agreement with the prediction of a classical hydrodynamic model based on a projected-Euler-Poisson system.

### [37] [The parity operator for parafermions and parabosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12393)
*N. I. Stoilova,J. Van der Jeugt*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入宇称算符P重新审视了parafermions和parabosons的定义，并揭示了其代数结构分别对应正交李代数so(2n+2)和正交超李代数osp(2|2n)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在通过格林三重关系（Green's triple relations）重新审视parafermions和parabosons的定义，并通过引入宇称算符P扩展这些代数关系，从而探索新的代数结构。

Method: 采用格林三重关系定义parafermions和parabosons，并引入宇称算符P扩展这些关系。通过代数分析揭示其对应的李代数结构，并研究福克空间（Fock spaces）的表示理论。

Result: 研究发现：n个parafermions与P构成的代数结构对应正交李代数so(2n+2)，其福克空间对应so(2n+2)的特定不可约表示；n个parabosons与P构成的代数结构对应正交超李代数osp(2|2n)，其福克空间对应osp(2|2n)的无限维不可约表示。P的谱与格林引入的统计阶数p密切相关。

Conclusion: 通过引入宇称算符P扩展格林三重关系，本文建立了parafermions和parabosons与特定李代数结构的对应关系，揭示了其福克空间的表示特性，并建立了P的谱与统计阶数p的联系。

Abstract: In this paper we reexamine the definition of parafermions and parabosons by means of Green's triple relations, and extend these relations by including a parity operator $P$ which is also determined by means of triple relations. As a consequence, we are dealing with new algebraic structures. It is shown that the algebra underlying a set of $n$ parafermions together with $P$ is the orthogonal Lie algebra $so(2n+2)$. The Fock spaces correspond to particular irreducible representations of $so(2n+2)$, and the action of $P$ in these spaces leads to interesting observations. Next, we show that the algebra underlying a set of $n$ parabosons together with $P$ is the orthosymplectic Lie superalgebra $osp(2|2n)$. In this case, the Fock spaces correspond to certain irreducible infinite-dimensional representations of $osp(2|2n)$. Both for parafermions and parabosons the spectrum of $P$ is closely related to the so-called order of statistics $p$, introduced by Green.

</details>


### [38] [Contact Geometry of Relativistic Particle Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12402)
*Begum Atesli,Ogul Esen,Michal Pavelka*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于接触几何（contact geometry）的几何框架，用于处理相对论性粒子动力学，特别适用于粒子衰变等耗散过程。该框架将演化表述为接触向量场，并将固有时（proper time）提升为独立变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相对论性粒子动力学框架在处理耗散过程（如粒子衰变）时存在局限性。传统方法需要将固有时视为世界线参数，这导致质量为零的粒子（如光子）演化定义不明确，需要重新参数化。

Method: 建立了一个九维扩展相空间，包含四个位置坐标、四个动量坐标和一个附加变量（作为固有时的几何变体）。动力学由接触哈密顿量（contact Hamiltonian）编码质量壳条件的演化接触向量场（evolution contact vector field）生成。通过将固有时提升为独立变量，相对论哈密顿正则方程被重写为完全几何形式。

Result: 该框架使质量为零粒子（光子）的演化定义明确，无需重新参数化。应用于衰变粒子时，能够几何化描述其演化。此外，建立了协变动理学理论（covariant kinetic theory），展示了衰变粒子在该框架中的几何描述如何改变熵。

Conclusion: 提出的基于接触几何的几何框架为相对论性粒子动力学提供了新的表述，特别适用于处理耗散过程。该框架通过将固有时独立化，避免了传统参数化方法的局限性，并为衰变粒子的几何描述和熵变分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We introduce a new geometric framework for relativistic particle dynamics based on contact geometry and suitable for treating dissipative processes like particle decay. The dynamics is formulated on a nine--dimensional extended phase space consisting of four position coordinates, four momenta, and an additional variable (functioning as a geometric variant of the particle's proper time). In this setting, the evolution is generated by an evolution contact vector field with a contact Hamiltonian encoding the mass shell. By promoting the proper time to an independent variable, the relativistic Hamilton canonical equations are rewritten in a fully geometric form without having to identify the proper time with a parameter along the worldlines. This makes for instance the evolution of massless particles (photons) well-defined without the need of reparametrization. The framework is then applied to decaying particles. Finally, we formulate a covariant kinetic theory and show how decaying particles can be described geometrically in this framework, changing the entropy.

</details>

### [42] [A variationally consistent mesoscopic Cosserat theory with distributed defects and configurational forces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12984)
*Lev Steinberg*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Cosserat弹性理论在相容性破坏时不再闭合，这促使研究者发展一个变分一致的细观扩展理论，以处理缺陷动力学和微结构演化问题。

Method: 采用Palatini型变分方法，将标架（coframe）和联络（connection）作为独立场变量，构建理论框架，通过变分原理导出Euler-Lagrange方程。

Result: 理论同时给出了标准平衡定律和与缺陷相关的激发场，材料不变性产生了构型力和力矩，这些作为Noether流出现并与由Bianchi恒等式支配的缺陷输运直接相关。

Abstract: We develop a variationally consistent mesoscopic extension of Cosserat elasticity motivated by the breakdown of compatibility in classical formulations. By admitting compatibility-breaking perturbations, the classical theory ceases to remain closed under admissible variations, necessitating an enlargement of the constitutive framework. This leads naturally to a formulation in which torsion and curvature are treated as independent distributed measures of defects. The theory is constructed using a Palatini-type variational approach, with the coframe and connection as independent fields. The resulting Euler--Lagrange equations yield both the standard balance laws and defect-related excitation fields. Material invariance gives rise to configurational forces and moments, which emerge as Noether currents and are directly linked to defect transport governed by the Bianchi identities. The framework provides a unified description of defect kinematics, configurational mechanics, and microstructural evolution. Illustrative examples and numerical evaluations demonstrate how defect transport generates configurational forces and highlight the underlying Maxwell-type structure of the theory. The proposed formulation offers a consistent geometric foundation for the analysis of structured solids with evolving internal geometry and provides a basis for future developments in defect dynamics and dissipative processes.

The clean $e^+e^-$ environment, free of pileup and characterized by simple event topologies, provides a well-controlled benchmark for evaluating the generative model's fidelity. Our results demonstrate that modern neural-network-based generative simulation approaches, developed primarily for LHC experiments, generalize naturally to historical collider experiments with distinct detector geometries and physics environments. This work shows that Parnassus can be applied beyond the LHC context and serves as an important tool for legacy data analysis where archival software tools are challenging to resurrect.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为探测反应堆中微子诱导的相干弹性中微子-原子核散射（Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering, CEνNS）产生的亚keV核反冲信号，必须维持探测器内足够低的杂质浓度以最小化信号衰减。因此需要建立准确的纯度演化模型来描述杂质在探测器内部的迁移行为。

Method: 本研究开发了一个全面的纯度演化模型，以实测的材料出气率（outgassing rates）作为输入参数。该模型包含了杂质在探测器内的非均匀传输机制，包括循环（circulation）、汽化（vaporization）和冷凝（condensation）等过程。模型通过专用原型探测器（prototype detector）的实验数据进行验证。

Result: 建立的纯度演化模型成功通过原型探测器数据的验证，表明模型能够准确描述杂质在双相液氙时间投影室（dual-phase liquid xenon time projection chamber）内的迁移行为。基于这一验证模型，研究提供了对即将建设的RELICS-10和RELICS-50探测器纯化性能的预测。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发并验证了一个描述RELICS实验探测器内杂质迁移的纯度演化模型，该模型能够准确预测杂质浓度变化。基于此模型对RELICS-10和RELICS-50探测器纯化性能的预测，为未来实验的探测器设计和运行提供了重要参考依据。

Abstract: The RELICS (REactor neutrino LIquid xenon Coherent elastic Scattering) experiment employs a dual-phase liquid xenon time projection chamber to search for Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering (CE$ν$NS) induced by reactor neutrinos. To detect these sub-keV nuclear recoils and minimize signal attenuation, it is critical to maintain a sufficiently low impurity concentration in the detector. This work presents a comprehensive purity evolution model developed to describe impurity migration inside the detector. Utilizing measured material outgassing rates as input parameters, the model incorporates non-uniform transport mechanisms of the impurities, including circulation, vaporization, and condensation. The model is validated using data from a dedicated prototype detector. Based on this validated model, projections for the purification performance of the upcoming RELICS-10 and RELICS-50 detectors are provided.

</details>

### [45] [Information-Geometric Decomposition of Generalization Error in Unsupervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12340)
*Gilhan Kim*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 该论文将无监督学习中Kullback-Leibler泛化误差精确分解为三个非负分量：模型误差、数据偏差和方差，并应用于ε-PCA模型，揭示了最优秩选择机制和相图结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在深入理解无监督学习中的泛化误差（generalization error）结构，特别是Kullback-Leibler泛化误差的组成成分及其在具体模型中的表现。

Method: 采用信息几何（information geometry）方法，基于广义勾股定理（generalized Pythagorean theorem）和对偶e-混合方差恒等式（dual e-mixture variance identity），对e-平坦（e-flat）模型类的KL泛化误差进行精确分解。将框架应用于ε-PCA（ε-正则化主成分分析）模型，通过技术性重构分析各分量。

Result: 对于各向同性高斯数据（isotropic Gaussian data），ε-PCA的最优秩选择对应截断值λ_cut* = ε，即保留超过噪声基底的经验特征值。相图呈现三个区域：全保留（retain-all）、内部（interior）和塌缩（collapse），由下界Marchenko-Pastur边和可解析计算的塌缩阈值ε_*(α)分隔。

Conclusion: 该分解框架为无监督学习泛化误差提供了精确的几何解释，最优秩选择反映了模型误差增益与数据偏差成本之间的边际率平衡，所有理论结果均通过数值模拟验证。

Abstract: We decompose the Kullback--Leibler generalization error (GE) -- the expected KL divergence from the data distribution to the trained model -- of unsupervised learning into three non-negative components: model error, data bias, and variance. The decomposition is exact for any e-flat model class and follows from two identities of information geometry: the generalized Pythagorean theorem and a dual e-mixture variance identity. As an analytically tractable demonstration, we apply the framework to $ε$-PCA, a regularized principal component analysis in which the empirical covariance is truncated at rank $N_K$ and discarded directions are pinned at a fixed noise floor $ε$. Although rank-constrained $ε$-PCA is not itself e-flat, it admits a technical reformulation with the same total GE on isotropic Gaussian data, under which each component of the decomposition takes closed form. The optimal rank emerges as the cutoff $λ_{\mathrm{cut}}^{*} = ε$ -- the model retains exactly those empirical eigenvalues exceeding the noise floor -- with the cutoff reflecting a marginal-rate balance between model-error gain and data-bias cost. A boundary comparison further yields a three-regime phase diagram -- retain-all, interior, and collapse -- separated by the lower Marchenko--Pastur edge and an analytically computable collapse threshold $ε_{*}(α)$, where $α$ is the dimension-to-sample-size ratio. All claims are verified numerically.

### [46] [Fixation probabilities for multi-allele Moran dynamics with weak selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12004)
*Ian Braga,Lucas Wardil,Ricardo Martinez-Garcia*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个微扰框架（perturbative framework），用于计算弱选择（weak selection）条件下多等位基因（multi-allele）Moran过程的固定概率（fixation probabilities）。该框架将固定概率围绕其中性解（neutral solution）进行系统展开，并应用于三个生物学实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固定概率对于刻画随机进化动力学（stochastic evolutionary dynamics）至关重要，但现有分析结果主要局限于两种竞争类型的系统。需要扩展分析理解至超越成对相互作用（pairwise interactions）的多等位基因情形。

Method: 研究者开发了一个微扰框架，利用弱选择条件下后向Fokker-Planck算符（backward Fokker-Planck operator）的一般结构。该框架首先在具有M个竞争等位基因和任意适应度函数（fitness functions）的一般情况下引入，然后将固定概率围绕其中性解进行系统展开。

Result: 该框架应用于三个生物学实例：具有恒定适应度函数的三等位基因竞争模型、等位基因适应度随其群体频率增加而增加的协调博弈（coordination game），以及互惠等位基因（mutualistic alleles）之间克隆干扰（clonal interference）的模型。这些结果扩展了固定概率的分析理解。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个用于研究多策略随机进化动力学（multi-strategy stochastic evolutionary dynamics）的框架，将固定概率的分析理解扩展到超越成对相互作用的多等位基因系统。

Abstract: Fixation probabilities are essential for characterizing stochastic evolutionary dynamics, but analytical results remain limited mainly to systems with two competing types. We develop a perturbative framework to compute fixation probabilities in multi-allele Moran processes under weak selection. Exploiting the general structure of the backward Fokker-Planck operator in this regime, we show that fixation probabilities admit a systematic expansion around their neutral solution. We first introduce the framework in a general case with $M$ competing alleles and arbitrary fitness functions, and then apply it to three biologically motivated examples: a simple model of three competing alleles with a constant fitness function, a coordination game in which allele fitness increases with its frequency in the population, and a model of clonal interference between mutualistic alleles. These results extend the analytical understanding of fixation probabilities beyond pairwise interactions, establishing a framework for investigating multi-strategy stochastic evolutionary dynamics.

</details>


### [47] [Predicting success of cooperators across arbitrary heterogeneous environmental landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12546)
*Amir Kargaran,Kamran Kaveh,Krishnendu Chatterjee*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个研究异质环境中合作演化的通用框架，发现环境异质性对合作的影响主要取决于环境状态的空间组织方式。空间相关性指数（SCI）能够预测合作者的固定概率，分离环境促进合作而交错环境抑制合作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大多数理论模型假设同质环境，但现实中种群栖息于空间异质景观中，合作收益随空间位置变化。需要建立通用框架来研究复杂异质环境中合作如何演化，特别是环境质量如何影响合作效益。

Method: 引入一个通用框架研究复杂异质环境中的合作演化，其中合作效益取决于局部环境质量。采用空间相关性指数（spatial correlation index, SCI）作为关键指标，分析不同空间组织方式下合作者的固定概率。

Result: 环境异质性对合作的影响主要取决于环境状态的空间组织：分离环境增强合作，而高度交错环境抑制合作。空间相关性指数（SCI）能够预测合作者的固定概率。在弱选择下，环境组织还控制演化时间尺度：分离景观产生长期亚稳态共存，交错景观导致合作者更快但成功率较低的固定。

Conclusion: 研究提供了关于空间环境异质性如何塑造合作演化的统一描述，并提出了生物和社会环境中合作成功的可测量预测指标。环境的空间组织是决定合作演化的关键因素，分离环境促进合作而交错环境抑制合作。

Abstract: Cooperation is central to the organization of complex biological and social systems. Most theoretical models assume homogeneous environments; in reality, populations inhabit spatially varying landscapes in which the payoffs of cooperation differ across space. Here, we introduce a general framework for the evolution of cooperation in complex, heterogeneous environments where the benefit of cooperation depends on local environmental quality. Cooperators in environmentally rich sites confer greater benefits than those on poor sites. We show that whether heterogeneity promotes or suppresses cooperation is determined primarily by the spatial organization of environmental states. Across arbitrary environmental landscapes, a single quantity, the spatial correlation index (SCI), predicts the fixation probability of cooperators. Under weak selection, segregated environments enhance cooperation, whereas highly intermixed, checkerboard-like landscapes suppress it. Beyond fixation probabilities, environmental organization also controls evolutionary timescales: segregated landscapes generate long-lived metastable coexistence, whereas intermixed landscapes lead to faster but less successful fixation of cooperators. Together, these results provide a unifying description of how spatial environmental heterogeneity shapes the evolution of cooperation and suggest measurable predictors of cooperative success in biological and social settings.

### [48] [Towards grounded autonomous research: an end-to-end LLM mini research loop on published computational physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12198)
*Haonan Huang*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 该研究开发了能够自主执行"阅读-计划-计算-比较"循环的LLM智能体，在计算物理领域测试了两种互补的研究范式：规模化分析111篇论文，以及深度分析一篇Nature Communications论文，展示了智能体在物理科学研究中的批判性评估和扩展能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的物理科学研究比机器学习研究更为复杂，需要受物理真理约束的深度推理，并且几乎总是建立在现有文献基础上。研究旨在探索LLM智能体在物理科学最小研究单元——"迷你研究循环"中的能力。

Method: 研究采用两种互补的测试范式：规模化测试中，智能体对111篇开放获取的计算物理论文自主执行"阅读-计划-计算-比较"循环；深度测试中，针对一篇关于二维材料MOSFET多尺度模拟的Nature Communications论文，智能体运行原始论文缺失的新计算。

Result: 规模化测试中，智能体在未受要求批判的情况下，对约42%的论文提出了实质性关切，其中97.7%的问题需要通过执行才能发现。深度测试中，智能体自主生成了可发表的评论文章，包含撰写、配图、排版和PDF迭代，修订了原始论文的主要结论。

Conclusion: 研究表明LLM智能体能够在物理科学研究中执行有意义的迷你研究循环，不仅能够规模化地识别文献中的问题，还能深度扩展研究内容并生成学术评论，展示了自主智能体在科学发现过程中的潜力。

Abstract: Recent autonomous LLM agents have demonstrated end-to-end automation of machine-learning research. Real-world physical science is intrinsically harder, requiring deep reasoning bounded by physical truth and, because real systems are too complex to study in isolation, almost always built on existing literature. We focus on the smallest meaningful unit of such research, a mini research loop in which an agent reads a paper, reproduces it, critiques it, and extends it. We test this loop in two complementary regimes: scale and depth. At scale, across 111 open-access computational physics papers, an agent autonomously runs the read-plan-compute-compare loop and, without being asked to critique, raises substantive concerns on ~42% of papers - 97.7% of which require execution to surface. In depth, for one Nature Communications paper on multiscale simulation of a 2D-material MOSFET, the agent runs new calculations missing from the original and produces, unsupervised, a publishable Comment -- composed, figured, typeset, and PDF-iterated -- that revises the paper's headline conclusion.

### [49] [Gravitational Gertsenshtein-Zeldovich mechanism for the Association between GW190425 and FRB 20190425A](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12775)
*Shao-Qin Wu,Jing-Rui Zhang,Rong-Gen Cai,Bing Zhang,Yun-Long Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新机制来解释GW190425引力波事件与FRB 20190425A快速射电暴事件的时空关联：通过磁星附近的Gertsenshtein-Zeldovich效应将千赫兹引力波转换为千赫兹电磁辐射，再通过相对论粒子的逆康普顿散射产生观测到的千兆赫兹快速射电暴。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW190425引力波事件与FRB 20190425A快速射电暴事件的时空巧合引发了二者可能存在物理关联的推测。先前讨论的超大质量中子星坍缩模型存在预测与系统测量倾角不一致的问题，需要新的物理解释。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的物理机制：假设在双中子星并合地点约2.5光时距离处存在一颗磁星（magnetar）。并合产生的千赫兹引力波通过磁星附近的Gertsenshtein-Zeldovich效应转换为千赫兹电磁辐射，随后相对论粒子通过逆康普顿散射（inverse Compton scattering）将千赫兹电磁波转换为观测到的千兆赫兹快速射电暴发射。

Result: 计算表明，在适当的参数选择下，该机制能够重现FRB 20190425A的观测特性，为引力波与快速射电暴的关联提供了新的物理解释框架。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种通过Gertsenshtein-Zeldovich效应和逆康普顿散射将引力波转换为快速射电暴的新机制，为解释GW190425与FRB 20190425A的时空关联提供了可行的理论方案，避免了先前模型与观测倾角的不一致问题。

Abstract: The temporal and spatial coincidence between the gravitational wave (GW) event GW190425 and the fast radio burst (FRB) event FRB 20190425A raises the intriguing possibility of a physical connection between the two. The widely discussed possibility invoking the collapse of a supermassive neutron star as the merger product suffers the inconsistency between the model prediction and the measured inclination angle of the system. Here, we propose a novel physical mechanism to account for the association. We envisage a magnetar located at about 2.5 light hours away from the binary neutron star merger site. The kiloherz GWs generated by the merger are converted into kiloherz electromagnetic (EM) radiation via the Gertsenshtein-Zeldovich (GZ) effect near the magnetar. Subsequent inverse Compton scattering off the kilohertz EM waves by relativistic particles generates the observed gigahertz FRB emission. Our calculation reveals that, with appropriate parameter choices, the properties of FRB 20190425A can be reproduced.

### [50] [Effective field theory of a single scalar pion field for large scale structure in the Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12009)
*Lara Celik,Bart Horn,Bhavya Mishra,David Muqattash*
