Method: 采用高分辨率角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）直接观测拓扑表面态，这些表面态源于体相狄拉克节线（bulk Dirac nodal lines）。

Result: 直接观测到源于体相狄拉克节线的拓扑表面态，这些表面态对多种扰动（包括2×1表面重构、晶体表面终止的化学变化以及螺旋反铁磁序）表现出异常鲁棒性。在尼尔温度以下观察到由磁有序驱动的复制能带，并展示了这种磁拓扑耦合对表面终止的明显依赖性。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了Eu(Ga₁₋ₓAlₓ)₄作为双重拓扑材料，为探索和控制两个基本拓扑领域之间的相互作用提供了一个稀有平台。

Abstract: The interplay between real-space topology such as magnetic skyrmions and momentum-space topology characterized by topological surface states (TSSs) is predicted to realize novel phenomena and functionalities, yet materials hosting both topologies are scarce. Skyrmion-hosting helimagnet family EuGa$_2$Al$_2$ and EuAl$_4$ has been a prime candidate for such a dual-topology system, but conclusive evidence for its momentum-space topology has remained elusive. We provide this evidence by directly observing TSSs that stem from bulk Dirac nodal lines using high-resolution angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy. These TSSs are exceptionally robust against various perturbations such as a 2$\times$1 surface reconstruction, a chemical change in the termination of the crystal surface, and the onset of helical antiferromagnetic order. Crucially, below the Neel temperature, we observe replica bands driven by the magnetic ordering. Moreover, we demonstrate clear surface-termination dependence of this magneto-topological coupling. Our findings establish Eu(Ga$_{1-x}$Al$_x$)$_4$ as a dual-topology material and offer a rare platform to explore and control the interaction between the two fundamental topological realms.

### [97] [Unconventional entanglement scaling and quantum criticality in the long-range spin-one Heisenberg chain with single-ion anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12754)
*Patrick Adelhardt,Sean R. Muleady,Kai P. Schmidt,Alexey V. Gorshkov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过矩阵乘积态计算和高阶级数展开，分析了具有单离子各向异性和交错反铁磁幂律相互作用的spin-1海森堡链的基态相图与临界性质。长程相互作用绕过了Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner定理，稳定了连续对称破缺相与Haldane相的竞争，揭示了非传统的量子临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程相互作用能重塑低维量子物质的低能性质，影响连续对称破缺和拓扑现象，但其对量子临界性的影响尚不清楚。研究旨在理解长程相互作用如何影响分离不同物相的量子临界行为。

Method: 采用矩阵乘积态计算（matrix-product state, MPS）结合高阶级数展开（pCUT+MC）方法，研究具有单离子各向异性和交错反铁磁幂律相互作用的spin-1海森堡链。通过分析纠缠熵标度行为和有限尺寸标度来表征相变边界。

Result: 确定了包含连续对称破缺相与Haldane相竞争的相图。在U(1)和SU(2)连续对称破缺相中，纠缠熵标度显示出超越短程预期的对数修正。大D到U(1)-CSB相变表现出随长程衰减指数连续变化的临界指数，Haldane到U(1)-CSB相变同样显示非传统量子临界性。

Conclusion: 该模型为具有可调长程耦合和天然单离子各向异性的原子平台提供了研究目标，为探索长程相互作用、连续对称破缺和拓扑之间的相互作用提供了最小化研究平台。

Abstract: Long-range interactions can fundamentally reshape the low-energy properties of low-dimensional quantum matter, altering both continuous symmetry breaking and topological phenomena. However, their impact on the quantum criticality separating these regimes remains poorly understood. We determine the ground-state phase diagram and critical properties of the spin-one Heisenberg chain with single-ion anisotropy and staggered antiferromagnetic power-law interactions, using matrix-product state (MPS) calculations complemented by high-order series expansions (pCUT+MC). Such long-range, non-frustrated interactions circumvent the Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner theorem, thereby stabilizing continuous symmetry breaking (CSB) phases in direct competition with the Haldane phase. We map out the resulting phase diagram and analyze the entanglement entropy scaling behavior in the U(1) and SU(2) CSB phases, finding logarithmic corrections beyond the short-range, universal contributions expected from linearly dispersed Goldstone modes. We further characterize all critical boundaries through finite-size scaling of either the entanglement entropy or the staggered magnetization. In particular, the large-D-to-U(1)-CSB transition exhibits unconventional, continuously varying critical exponents as a function of the long-range decay exponent with a strong dependence on the imposed boundary conditions leading to distinct finite-size scalings for sufficiently long-range potentials. Remarkably, the Haldane-to-U(1)-CSB transition likewise displays unconventional quantum criticality with distinct continuously varying critical exponents. Our work positions this model as a target for near-term atomic platforms with tunable long-range couplings and exhibiting natural single-ion anisotropy, offering a minimal playground for exploring the interplay between long-range interactions, continuous symmetry breaking, and topology.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用理论模型研究包含质量差异显著的两类费米子的重费米子d-f杂化体系，其中重费米子与轻费米子在色散交叉点发生杂化，但该杂化不产生完整的绝缘隙。

Conclusion: 所研究的重费米子d-f杂化模型成功解释了SmB₆低温相的实验观测特征，表明该理论框架能够有效描述此类重费米子杂化体系的物理性质。

Abstract: In this Letter we theoretically study physical properties of a model of heavy fermion $d-f$ hybrid. In the studied model two species of fermions have dispersions with different masses, one being much heavier than the other. Hybridization between the fermions at the crossing point of their dispersions doesn't open a true insulating gap leaving a heavy fermion $d-f$ hybrid at the Fermi level. As a result, our theoretical model qualitatively explains experiments on the low-temperature phase of the SmB$_6$. These are the saturation of the resistance, linear in temperature specific heat, and frequency dependence of the optical conductivity. Calculated optical conductivity shows a broadened peak at the twice the hybridization value as well as a low frequency tail.

### [100] [Momentum-dependent charge-density-wave gap formation in ZrTe_{2.98}Se_{0.02}](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12326)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用激光光电子显微镜（laser photoemission microscopy）技术，在布里渊区（Brillouin zone, BZ）内解析了CDW转变温度上下费米面的强度差异，并绘制了能量CDW间隙的动量分布图。

Result: 研究发现：1）在布里渊区中心观测到一个椭圆形费米面，边界处有两个准一维费米面；2）能量CDW间隙形成仅限于动量区域0.25 Å^{-1} < ky < 0.8 Å^{-1}（沿\bar{B}-\bar{D}线），该区域与一个准一维费米面位置重合。

Conclusion: 能量CDW间隙的特征性动量依赖性表明，要理解ZrTe_{3}体系中的CDW态，必须同时考虑费米面嵌套（FS nesting）和能带依赖的电子-声子耦合（band-dependent electron-phonon coupling）的重要性。

Abstract: We investigated the energy gap formation across the charge density wave (CDW) transition inof ZrTe_{2.98}Se_{0.02}. By employing a laser photoemission microscopy, we clearly resolved one elliptical Fermi surface (FS) around the Brillouin zone (BZ) center, and two quasi-one-dimensional FSs along the BZ boundary. We further mapped the intensity difference between the FSs below and above the CDW transition temperature. We found that the energy CDW gap formation is limited to the momentum region 0.25 Å^{-1} < ky < 0.8 Å^{-1} along \bar{B}-\bar{D} line, which coincides with the location of one of the quasi-one-dimensional FSs. Characteristic momentum dependence in the energy CDW gap suggests the importance of both FS nesting and band-dependent electron-phonon coupling for understanding the CDW state in ZrTe_{3} system.

### [101] [Spintronic THz emitters based on NiCu alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12722)
*E. A. Karashtin,I. Yu. Pashen'kin,A. V. Gorbatova,E. D. Lebedeva,P. Yu. Avdeev,N. V. Bezvikonnyi,A. M. Buryakov*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究通过使用不同镍含量的NiCu合金作为铁磁层或非磁层，构建了基于自旋电子学的太赫兹发射纳米结构。研究发现NiCu合金在特定成分下既能作为有效的自旋源，又能作为有效的自旋-电荷转换器，并展示了基于热效应的太赫兹辐射发射控制能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索基于铁磁/非磁材料（FM/NM）自旋电子纳米结构的太赫兹发射特性，特别关注NiCu合金在不同成分下的功能表现。通过设计特定化学计量组成的合金，使其在室温下分别呈现铁磁性或顺磁性，以研究边界匹配在自旋电子太赫兹源中的重要性。

Method: 采用不同镍含量（x）的NiCu合金构建FM/NM纳米结构，其中合金的化学计量组成被设计为两种类型：[FM]型在室温下呈铁磁性，[PM]型在室温下呈顺磁性。两种合金的镍含量差异仅为10%，用于分别作为铁磁层、非磁层或同时作为两层。

Result: 研究发现，尽管NiCu[PM]合金不含重金属，但在结构中作为自旋电流向电荷电流的有效转换器，效率仅比Pt低2.8倍。NiCu[FM]合金尽管居里温度较低（约65°C），但作为有效自旋源，效率仅比类似结构中的Co低2倍。这凸显了边界匹配在自旋电子太赫兹源中的重要性。

Conclusion: 基于NiCu的太赫兹源展示了通过热效应有效控制太赫兹辐射发射的可能性，这得益于高发射率和相对较低居里温度的独特组合。该研究为自旋电子太赫兹源的设计提供了新的材料选择和调控途径。

Abstract: We study THz emission from ferromagnet / nonmagnetic material (FM/NM) spintronic nanostructures in which the $Ni_xCu_{1-x}$ alloy with different $x$ is used as an FM, an NM, or both layers. The stoichiometric composition of the NiCu alloys standing at two positions (we denote it as [FM] or [PM]) is chosen so that it is ferromagnetic at room temperature in the case it is used as the FM layer, and is paramagnetic at room temperature for the NM layer. Besides, we choose the nickel ratio $x$ close to each other for both [FM] and [PM] types of the alloy (the difference is only $10\%$). We show that although NiCu[PM] does not contain heavy metal it acts as an effective converter of spin current into the electric one in our structure showing only 2.8 times smaller efficiency than Pt. Besides, the NiCu[FM] alloy, despite having quite small Curie temperature (approximately $65 ^\circ C$), acts as an effective spin source having the efficiency only 2 times smaller than Co in similar structures. This shows up the importance of boundary matching in the spintronic THz sources. Our NiCu-based THz sources reveal a possibility of effective thermally induced control of emission of THz radiation due to a unique combination of high emission rate and relatively small Curie temperature.

</details>

### [102] [Atomically-Thin Tsumoite (BiTe) based All-Photonic-Isolator, Information Converter, and Logic-Gate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12003)
*Saswata Goswami,Caique Campos de Oliveira,Abhijith M. B.,Varinder Pal,Vidya Kochat,Pulickel M. Ajayan,Samit K. Ray,Pedro A. S. Autreto,Chandra Sekhar Tiwary*

Method: 采用空间自相位调制（spatial self-phase modulation, SSPM）光谱技术分析BiTe分散体的非线性光学响应，通过衍射环图案定量推导非线性折射率（n2）和三阶非线性磁化率。利用风铃模型（wind-chime model）研究SSPM环的时间演化和畸变，并通过第一性原理电子能带结构计算揭示非线性磁化率增强的物理机制。

Result: BiTe的三阶非线性磁化率与先进二维材料相当甚至更优，其增强源于能带色散特性。研究建立了载流子输运与三阶非线性磁化率之间的直接关联，并基于这些特性设计了基于BiTe-hBN异质结的光子隔离器、光子信息转换器和逻辑门等全光器件，展示了非对称传播功能。

Conclusion: 二维BiTe纳米结构展现出卓越的非线性光学性能，为先进光子信号处理和集成光子应用提供了强大的非线性光学平台。研究不仅定量表征了其非线性响应，还成功展示了多种功能性光子器件的设计实现。

Abstract: Two-dimensional tsumoite (BiTe), a polymorph of Bi2Te3, has emerged as a promising candidate for nonlinear photonic devices owing to its strong spin-orbit coupling, tunable bandgap, and high carrier mobility characteristics. This work presents a thorough examination of the third-order nonlinear optical response of BiTe dispersions using spatial self-phase modulation (SSPM) spectroscopy. The nonlinear refractive index (n2) and third-order nonlinear susceptibility are quantitatively derived from the diffraction ring patterns, demonstrating third-order nonlinear susceptibility values, similar to or surpassing those of advanced 2D materials. The temporal development and distortion of the SSPM rings are examined using the wind-chime model, and thermal factors influencing the SSPM pattern are analyzed. First-principles electronic band structure studies reveal that the elevated nonlinear susceptibility arises from band dispersion. Direct correlation between carrier transport and third-order nonlinear susceptibility is established. Utilizing these qualities, all photonic devices, including a photonic isolator based on a 2D BiTe-2D hBN heterostructure, are depicted to show asymmetric propagation. A photonic information converter and a logic gate are designed using the cross-phase modulation technique. These findings establish 2D BiTe nanostructure as a formidable nonlinear optical platform for advanced photonic signal processing and integrated photonic applications.

</details>


### [103] [Tunable Polariton Canalization in Natural van der Waals Oxide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12174)
*H. Shiravi,W. Zheng,D. A. Rhodes,L. Balicas,H. D. Zhou,G. X. Ni*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双曲声子极化激元（HPPs）虽已在多种层状材料中被发现，但实现高级控制（特别是用于单向能量流的极化激元渠化）通常需要复杂的器件制备或晶体改性。本研究旨在探索α-V2O5中无需额外处理即可实现极化激元控制的潜力。

Method: 采用红外纳米成像（infrared nano-imaging）技术对α-V2O5中的面内双曲性进行可视化表征，并结合理论建模分析极化激元特性。通过理论计算构建了用于调控极化激元波前的介电常数相图（permittivity phase diagram）。

Result: 在α-V2O5中观察到了无需额外处理的单向坡印廷矢量（Poynting-vector）传播，揭示了极化激元渠化的新形式，其色散轮廓可通过入射光频率连续调谐。理论相图为定制极化激元波前提供了设计指导。

Conclusion: 金属氧化物α-V2O5在按需纳米尺度光渠化（light canalization）和控制方面具有巨大潜力，为简化极化激元器件设计提供了新途径。

Abstract: Hyperbolic phonon polaritons (HPPs) are coupled oscillations of anisotropic lattice vibrations and electromagnetic fields that confine the latter to the nanoscale, enabling novel nano-polaritonic devices. While HPPs have been identified in multiple layered materials, achieving advanced control and manipulation - particularly polariton canalization for unidirectional energy flow - often necessitates complex device fabrications or crystal modifications. Here we visualize and elucidate the properties of in-plane hyperbolicity in alpha-V2O5, a layered compound with a highly anisotropic permittivity tensor. We show unidirectional Poynting-vector propagation of polaritons in alpha-V2O5 without additional treatments. Combined with theoretical modeling, our infrared nano-imaging studies unveil a novel form of polariton canalization, with its dispersion contour continuously tunable by the incident light frequency. Additionally, we provide a theoretically calculated permittivity phase diagram for tailoring polaritonic wavefronts. These findings suggest that the metal-oxide alpha-V2O5 holds great promise for on-demand light canalization and control at the nanoscale.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性声子极化激元态对于手性依赖的光-物质相互作用具有重要意义，但其实现和磁控制仍具挑战性，且声子极化激元介质的直接磁光可调性有限。

Method: 提出混合平台，使六方氮化硼（hBN）声子极化激元与磁光光子晶体支持的连续谱束缚态（bound state in the continuum）耦合，实现强选择性光子耦合，并通过声子比例分析和耦合理论量化模态组成。

Result: 相互作用导致显著的模分裂和杂化态形成，其模态组成可通过磁偏置通过光子组分的磁光响应进行控制，从而调控模态组成和光谱响应；杂化态在圆偏振激发下表现出手性选择性吸收。

Conclusion: 该工作为磁可调手性声子极化激元器件和杂化极化激元功能提供了可行路径，实现了通过磁控制调节杂化过程，为手性依赖的光-物质相互作用提供了新平台。

Abstract: Chiral phonon-polaritonic states are of interest for handedness-dependent light-matter interactions, yet their realization and magnetic control remain challenging, while direct magneto-optical tunability of phonon-polaritonic media is limited. Here, we propose a hybrid platform in which an hBN phonon polariton couples to a chiral bound state in the continuum supported by a magneto-optical photonic crystal, enabling strong and selective photonic coupling. The interaction gives rise to pronounced mode splitting and the formation of hybrid states, and their modal composition is quantified by phonon-proportion analysis and described by a coupling theory. Importantly, the hybridization can be controlled by magnetic bias through the magneto-optical response of the photonic component, providing control over the modal composition and spectral response. In addition, the hybrid states exhibit handedness-selective absorption under circularly polarized excitation. This work offers a feasible route toward magnetically tunable chiral phonon-polaritonic devices and hybrid polaritonic functionalities

### [105] [Engineering strong coupling in ultra-compact photonic crystal/2D material platforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12779)
*Eleonora P. Kraus,Jamie M. Fitzgerald,Carlos Maciel-Escudero,Ermin Malic*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了亚波长厚度的光子晶体（PhC）平板与二维激子材料（如过渡金属硫族化合物）耦合系统，揭示了其中弱耦合与强耦合区域共存的现象，为设计无金属、超紧凑的极化激元器件提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚波长厚度的光子晶体平板与二维激子材料耦合系统是高度可调谐、室温工作、片上光电器件的理想平台。与传统法布里-珀罗微腔不同，这些紧凑型开放腔体展现出非平凡的电场分布，导致在光子晶体晶胞内存在空间上不同的弱耦合和强耦合区域。

Method: 研究采用耦合模理论（coupled mode theory）和麦克斯韦方程的严格解，分析光子晶体几何结构如何控制共存的激子/极化激元贡献并调控光学光谱。对于大填充因子（即小空气间隙），光子晶体极化激元可建模为通过光子晶体平板周期性而"变亮"的暗波导模式。

Result: 通过基于局部场强对过渡金属硫族化合物单层进行空间图案化，研究揭示了激子在弱耦合和强耦合机制中同时存在的现象。光子晶体几何结构能够有效调控这些共存的激子/极化激元贡献，从而定制光学响应特性。

Conclusion: 该工作为结构化光子环境中的强光-物质耦合机制提供了基础性见解，为设计和优化无金属、超紧凑的极化激元器件开辟了途径。研究展示了通过光子晶体几何调控实现弱/强耦合区域共存的可能性。

Abstract: Sub-wavelength thick photonic crystal (PhC) slabs coupled to 2D excitonic materials, such as transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs), are a promising platform for highly tunable, room-temperature, on-chip optoelectronic devices. Unlike conventional Fabry-Perot microcavities, these compact open cavities exhibit non-trivial electric field profiles, leading to spatially distinct regions of weak and strong coupling with excitons within the PhC unit cell. Using coupled mode theory and rigorous solutions to Maxwell's equations, we investigate how the PhC geometry can be used to control these coexisting exciton/polariton contributions and tailor the resulting optical spectra. For large filling factors, i.e., small air gaps, we show that PhC polaritons can be modeled as dark waveguide modes brightened via the periodicity of the PhC slab. Furthermore, by spatially patterning the TMD monolayer based on the local field intensity, we reveal the simultaneous presence of excitons in both the weak and strong coupling regimes. Overall, this work provides fundamental insights into the strong light-matter coupling regime in structured photonic environments, offering a pathway to design and optimize metal-free, ultra-compact polaritonic devices.

### [106] [Correctness criteria for complex Langevin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12388)
*Michael Mandl*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究系统比较了复杂朗之万（complex Langevin）方法中用于评估模拟结果正确性的主要诊断标准，通过四个简单但非平凡的模型测试这些标准的适用性、易用性和预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂朗之万方法是处理具有符号问题（sign problem）系统的有前景数值方法，但该方法可能在某些情况下无法收敛或在其他情况下收敛到错误极限。多年来开发了各种诊断工具来评估模拟结果的正确性，但需要对这些标准进行系统比较。

Method: 研究采用系统比较方法，考虑四个简单但非平凡的模型，并将各种正确性标准应用于每个模型。重点对比这些标准的适用性、易用性和预测能力。

Result: 通过对四个模型应用不同诊断标准，获得了关于各标准性能的具体结论。这些结论预计可以推广到更现实的理论中。

Conclusion: 该研究为复杂朗之万方法中诊断工具的选择提供了系统比较框架，通过模型测试揭示了各标准的相对优势和局限性，为更广泛的理论应用提供了指导。

Abstract: The complex Langevin approach is a promising method for the numerical treatment of systems with a sign problem, for which conventional lattice field theory techniques based on importance sampling cannot be applied. However, complex Langevin dynamics may fail to converge in some cases and converge to a wrong limit in others, motivating the development of various diagnostic tools over the years to assess the correctness of given simulation results. This work aims at providing a systematic comparison between the most prominent such correctness criteria. In particular, the main goal is to contrast their applicability, ease of use, and - most importantly - their predictive power. To this end, four simple but nontrivial models are considered and the criteria applied to each of them. The obtained conclusions are expected to carry over to more realistic theories as well.

</details>


### [107] [Hilbert Space Fragmentation from Generalized Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12907)
*Thea Budde,Marina Kristć Marinković,Joao C. Pinto Barros*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该论文证明广义对称性（generalized symmetries）可以导致希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert space fragmentation），而指数增长的Krylov子空间数量本身并不必然意味着遍历性破缺（ergodicity breaking）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为希尔伯特空间碎片化是指数增长的Krylov子空间数量，通常被视为遍历性破缺的证据，因为传统对称性最多只能产生多项式数量的子空间。然而，需要重新审视这种关联性。

Method: 通过分析具有高阶形式对称性（higher-form symmetries）、子系统对称性（subsystem symmetries）和规范对称性（gauge symmetries）的模型，证明这些广义对称性可以产生指数数量的对称性子空间。进一步证明非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）可以在单个对称性子空间内引发额外碎片化。

Result: 多个已知模型中的碎片化现象源于广义对称性，因此指数数量的Krylov子空间本身并不必然意味着遍历性破缺。当子空间缺乏平移不变性时，Krylov受限热化（Krylov-restricted thermalization）自然导致无序自由局域化（disorder free localization）。

Conclusion: 希尔伯特空间碎片化可以由广义对称性引起，指数增长的Krylov子空间数量不能单独作为遍历性破缺的证据。无序自由局域化可以在不需要遍历性破缺或规范对称性的情况下，通过Krylov受限热化自然产生。

Abstract: Hilbert space fragmentation refers to exponential growth in the number of dynamically disconnected Krylov sectors with system size. It is taken as evidence of ergodicity breaking, since conventional symmetries generate at most a polynomial number of sectors. However, we demonstrate that generalized symmetries can fragment the Hilbert space. Models with higher-form, subsystem, and gauge symmetries can have exponentially many symmetry sectors. We further prove that non-invertible symmetries can induce additional fragmentation within individual symmetry sectors. Fragmentation in several known models arises from generalized symmetries, and the presence of exponentially many Krylov sectors therefore does not by itself imply ergodicity breaking. Finally, we show that disorder free localization arises naturally from Krylov-restricted thermalization when sectors lack translation invariance, requiring neither ergodicity breaking nor gauge symmetry.

</details>

### [108] [Inverse Design of Inorganic Compounds with Generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11827)

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该综述分析了生成式人工智能（generative AI）在无机化合物领域的应用现状、挑战及未来方向，重点关注如何通过数据-表示-模型（data-representation-model）流程处理无机化合物的复杂性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然机器学习（machine learning）正在革新化学领域，特别是生成式人工智能在有机化学和药物发现中已有丰富工具箱，但其在无机化合物中的应用仍受限于无机化合物固有的复杂性挑战。

Method: 该综述通过分析广泛多样的无机系统（从分子到晶体，包括过渡金属配合物（transition metal complexes）和微孔材料（microporous materials）），考察生成式人工智能方法如何演化为处理完整复杂性的数据-表示-模型（data-representation-model）流程。

Result: 分析表明，生成式人工智能方法已发展出能够处理无机化合物化学组成、几何结构、对称性和电子结构（electronic structure）等完整复杂性的综合解决方案，但该领域仍面临标准化不足等挑战。

Conclusion: 未来发展方向包括基准标准化（benchmark standardization）和可合成性度量（synthesizability metrics）的开发，这些将推动生成式人工智能在无机化学领域的更广泛应用。

Abstract: Machine learning is revolutionizing chemistry. Beyond the value of predictive models accelerating virtual screening, generative AI aims at enabling inverse design, reversing the compound-to-property prediction paradigm into property-to-compound generation. Chemists now have access to a rich AI toolbox for organic chemistry, including drug discovery. However, the application of these methods to inorganic compounds remains limited by the challenges posed by their intrinsic nature. This Review analyzes how these challenges have been addressed, considering widely diverse systems ranging from molecules to crystals, including transition metal complexes and microporous materials. The analysis focuses on how generative AI methods have evolved towards data-representation-model pipelines that address the full complexity of inorganic compounds, including their chemical composition, geometry, symmetry, and electronic structure. Future directions, like benchmark standardization and the development of synthesizability metrics, are also discussed.

</details>


### [109] [Surface Plasmons in the Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12008)
*Mohit Chaudhary,Hans-Christian Weissker,Daniele Toffoli,Mauro Stener,Victor Despré,Franck Rabilloud,Jean Lermé,Rajarshi Sinha-Roy*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent density-functional theory）时间演化形式的方法，用于计算金属团簇连续谱中的表面等离激元共振（surface plasmon resonance），特别适用于铝和铟等非常规等离激元材料在紫外区域的等离子体应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推动紫外区域等离子体应用的需求促使了对铝和铟等非常规等离激元材料团簇的研究。这些材料的表面等离激元共振出现在电离势以上，量子力学描述需要包含电离过程，这使得从头计算（ab initio calculations）具有挑战性。

Method: 提出了一种基于含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent density-functional theory）时间演化形式（time-evolution formalism）的稳健方法，用于计算金属团簇连续谱中的表面等离激元共振。该方法能够准确描述连续谱和团簇的电离过程。

Result: 以Al₁₃⁻为参考系统，研究表明对连续谱和团簇电离的准确描述能够捕捉到紫外区域的宽表面等离激元。该方法应用于铝团簇显示了从Al₆的离散光谱特征到更大团簇在深紫外区域表面等离激元的尺寸依赖性演化。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法能够有效计算非常规等离激元材料团簇在紫外区域的表面等离激元共振，为理解铝等材料团簇中等离激元行为的尺寸依赖性演化提供了有力工具。

Abstract: The interest to foster plasmonic applications at energies in the ultra-violet, has escalated research initiatives in clusters of unconventional plasmonic materials like aluminum and indium,for which the surface-plasmon resonance appears above the ionization potential. Naturally, the quantum mechanical description calls for the incorporation of the ionization process, thereby making the ab initio calculations challenging. We present a robust approach within the time-evolution formalism of the time-dependent density-functional theory to calculate surface plasmon resonance in the continuum of metal clusters. Using the much studied Al$_{13}^-$ as a system of reference, we show that accurate description of the continuum and of the ionization of the cluster allow to capture a broad surface-plasmon in the UV. Application of this approach in aluminum clusters has given the size-dependent evolution from discrete spectral features in Al$_{6}$ to the surface-plasmon in larger clusters in the deep ultra-violet.

</details>

### [110] [Cross-Domain Transfer with Particle Physics Foundation Models: From Jets to Neutrino Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12364)
*Gregor Krzmanc,Vinicius Mikuni,Benjamin Nachman,Callum Wilkinson*

TL;DR: 该研究探索了粒子物理基础模型（foundation model）的跨实验迁移能力，验证了在高能碰撞数据上预训练的OmniLearned模型在低能固定靶中微子实验中的有效性，展示了基础模型在能量尺度、探测器技术和物理过程差异下的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子物理领域未来AI研究将基于基础模型（foundation model）以加速训练并提升灵敏度。本研究旨在探索为粒子物理构建通用基础模型的可能性，具体验证在高能碰撞数据上预训练的模型能否有效迁移到低能固定靶中微子实验。

Method: 研究处理了MINERvA中微子-核散射事件，评估了在高能$pp$和$ep$碰撞模拟与真实数据上预训练的OmniLearned基础模型。评估任务包括可用能量的回归（regression）和带电流π介子末态（charged-current pion final states）的二元分类（binary classification），具体涉及$\mathrm{CC1π^{\pm}}$、$\mathrm{CCNπ^{\pm}}$和$\mathrm{CC1π^{0}}$等过程。

Result: 预训练的OmniLearned模型在相同计算预算（compute budget）下始终优于从头训练的类似规模模型，整体性能更优。在相同训练步数（training steps）下也能获得更好的性能，表明粒子级基础模型获得的归纳偏置（inductive biases）能够跨越能量尺度、探测器技术和基础物理过程的巨大差异。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明粒子物理基础模型具有广泛的跨实验泛化能力，指向了粒子物理中探测器无关推断（detector-agnostic inference）的新范式，为构建通用粒子物理基础模型提供了重要支持。

Abstract: Future AI-based studies in particle physics will likely start from a foundation model to accelerate training and enhance sensitivity. As a step towards a general-purpose foundation model for particle physics, we investigate whether the OmniLearned foundation model pre-trained on diverse high-$Q^2$ simulated and real $pp$ and $ep$ collisions can be effectively transferred to a few-GeV fixed-target neutrino experiment. We process MINERvA neutrino--nucleus scattering events and evaluate pre-trained models on two types of tasks: regression of available energy and binary classification of charged-current pion final states ($\mathrm{CC1π^{\pm}}$, $\mathrm{CCNπ^{\pm}}$, and $\mathrm{CC1π^{0}}$). Pre-trained OmniLearned models consistently outperform similarly sized models trained from scratch, achieving better overall performance at the same compute budget, as well as achieving better performance at the same number of training steps. These results suggest that particle-level foundation models acquire inductive biases that generalize across large differences in energy scale, detector technology, and underlying physics processes, pointing toward a paradigm of detector-agnostic inference in particle physics.

</details>

J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII合作组利用2712.4×10⁶个ψ(2S)事例，首次在χc1→π⁺π⁻η′衰变中观测到具有奇特量子数Jᴾᶜ=1⁻⁺的π₁(1600)态，统计显著性超过21σ，并测量了其质量和宽度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过ψ(2S)→γχc1, χc1→π⁺π⁻η′过程的偏波分析（partial wave analysis），寻找具有奇特量子数（exotic quantum numbers）Jᴾᶜ=1⁻⁺的强子态，这类态无法由传统的夸克模型解释。

Method: 研究采用BESIII探测器收集的(2712.4±14.3)×10⁶个ψ(2S)事例，对衰变链ψ(2S)→γχc1, χc1→π⁺π⁻η′进行偏波分析，并使用质量依赖宽度的相对论性Breit-Wigner函数进行参数提取。

Result: 首次在χc1→π₁±(1600)π∓, π₁±(1600)→π±η′衰变中观测到同位旋矢量态π₁(1600)，统计显著性超过21σ；测得质量1828±8(stat)+11-33(syst) MeV/c²，宽度638±26(stat)+35-86(syst) MeV；分支比乘积为(4.30±0.14(stat)+1.04-1.03(syst))×10⁻⁴。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在粲偶素衰变中明确观测到具有奇特量子数Jᴾᶜ=1⁻⁺的π₁(1600)态，为理解超出传统夸克模型的强子态提供了重要实验证据。

Abstract: A partial wave analysis of the process $ψ(2S)\rightarrowγχ_{c1}, χ_{c1}\rightarrowπ^+π^-η^{\prime}$ is performed using $(2712.4\pm14.3)\times10^{6}$ $ψ(2S)$ events collected with the BESIII detector. An isovector state with exotic quantum numbers $J^{PC}=1^{-+}$, denoted as $π_{1}(1600)$, is observed for the first time in the charmonium decay of $χ_{c1}\rightarrowπ_{1}^{\pm}(1600)π^{\mp}$, $π_{1}^{\pm}(1600)\rightarrowπ^{\pm}η^{\prime}$ with a statistical significance over $21σ$. Its mass and width are determined to be $1828 \pm 8 ({\rm stat})^{+11}_{-33}({\rm syst})~\mathrm{MeV}/c^2$ and $638 \pm 26 ({\rm stat})^{+35}_{-86}({\rm syst})~\mathrm{MeV}$, respectively, using a relativistic Breit-Wigner function with a mass-dependent width. The corresponding product of branching fractions is determined to be $\mathcal{B}\left[χ_{c1}\rightarrowπ_{1}(1600)^{\pm}π^{\mp} \right] \times \mathcal{B}\left[π_{1}(1600)^{\pm}\rightarrowπ^{\pm}η^{\prime}\right] = \left( 4.30 \pm 0.14 ({\rm stat})^{+1.04}_{-1.03}({\rm syst})~ \right) \times 10^{-4}$.

</details>

Witek,L. Witola,T. Wolf,E. Wood,G. Wormser,S. A. Wotton,H. Wu,J. Wu,X. Wu,Y. Wu,Z. Wu,K. Wyllie,S. Xian,Z. Xiang,Y. Xie,T. X. Xing,A. Xu,L. Xu,M. Xu,R. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文报告了在质子-质子碰撞中W玻色子衰变产生的μ子电荷不对称性的精确测量，这是目前前向区域最精确的测量结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量μ子电荷不对称性对于检验微扰量子色动力学（perturbative quantum chromodynamics）的预测具有重要意义，特别是在前向区域的高精度测量能够提供对标准模型的重要验证。

Method: 分析使用了LHCb探测器在2016-2018年记录的5.1 fb⁻¹积分亮度数据，测量了横向动量在25-55 GeV、赝快度在2.0-4.5范围内的μ子的电荷不对称性。

Result: 该测量代表了目前前向区域μ子电荷不对称性最精确的测定结果，与微扰量子色动力学的次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading-order）预测表现出极好的一致性。

Conclusion: 该精确测量为检验标准模型提供了重要数据，特别是在前向区域的测量结果与理论预测的高度一致性增强了我们对微扰量子色动力学计算可靠性的信心。

Abstract: A precision measurement of the muon charge asymmetry from $W$-boson decays in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV is presented. The analysis utilizes data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 5.1 $fb^{-1}$, recorded by the LHCb detector during 2016, 2017 and 2018. The asymmetry is measured for muons with transverse momentum between 25 and 55 GeV and pseudorapidity between 2.0 and 4.5. This result represents the most precise determination of the muon charge asymmetry in the forward region to date, exhibiting excellent agreement with next-to-next-to-leading-order predictions in perturbative quantum chromodynamics.

</details>


### [113] [New measurement of $K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$ branching ratio at the NA62 experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12649)
*Xiafei Chang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: NA62实验利用2016-2024年数据测量了超稀有衰变K⁺→π⁺νν̄的分支比，结果为(9.6±1.9)×10⁻¹¹，与标准模型预言相符，精度优于20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: K⁺→π⁺νν̄衰变是味物理（flavor physics）中的黄金模式（golden mode），其标准模型预言的分支比低于10⁻¹⁰。该衰变模式对质量尺度高达O(100 TeV)的新物理模型高度敏感，NA62实验旨在精确测量这一衰变。

Method: NA62实验位于CERN SPS，专门设计用于测量K⁺→π⁺νν̄衰变。研究使用了2016-2024年收集的数据，其中2023-2024年的新数据集使信号样本翻倍，同时按比例降低了本底。

Result: 结合2016-2024年数据，测得分支比B(K⁺→π⁺νν̄) = (9.6⁺¹·⁹₋₁·₈)×10⁻¹¹。该结果与标准模型预言兼容，测量精度优于20%。

Conclusion: NA62实验成功测量了超稀有衰变K⁺→π⁺νν̄的分支比，结果为(9.6±1.9)×10⁻¹¹，与标准模型预言一致，为检验新物理模型提供了重要约束。

Abstract: The ultra-rare decay $K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$ is a golden mode in flavor physics. The Standard Model prediction for its branching ratio is below $10^{-10}$. This decay mode is highly sensitive to new physics models at mass scales up to $\mathcal{O}(100\,\mathrm{TeV})$. The NA62 experiment at CERN SPS is designed to measure this decay mode. A preliminary result of the branching ratio measurement using data collected in 2023--2024 is presented. With the new dataset, the NA62 experiment doubled its signal sample while reducing the background in proportion. Combining the data collected in 2016--2024, the branching ratio is measured to be $\mathcal{B}(K^+\toπ^+ν\barν) = \left(9.6^{+1.9}_{-1.8}\right)\times10^{-11}$. The result is compatible with the Standard Model prediction with a precision better than $20\%$.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: No AI summary available.

Result: No AI summary available.

Conclusion: No AI summary available.

Abstract: A precision measurement of the $W$-boson production cross-section is performed using the $W \to μν$ decay channel, based on a sample of proton-proton collision data collected by the LHCb experiment at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 5.1 $fb^{-1}$. The cross-section is measured for muons with transverse momentum between 25 and 55 GeV and pseudorapidity between 2.0 and 4.5. The integrated production cross-sections of $W$ bosons are measured to be $$ \begin{array}{lcl} σ_{W^+ \to μ^+ν} &=& 1754.2 \pm 1.5 \pm 11.9 \pm 35.1\text{ pb} \\ σ_{W^- \to μ^-\barν} &=& 1178.1 \pm 1.3 \pm 9.7 \pm 23.6\text{ pb} \end{array} $$ where uncertainties are statistical, systematic, and due to the luminosity determination, respectively. Results are in good agreement with theoretical predictions at next-to-next-to-leading order in perturbative quantum chromodynamics. This measurement is significantly more precise than previous results in this kinematic regime.

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [115] [XANE(3): An E(3)-Equivariant Graph Neural Network for Accurate Prediction of XANES Spectra from Atomic Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12140)
*Vitor F. Grizzi,Luke N. Pretzie,Jiayi Xu,Cong Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: XANE(3)是一种基于物理的E(3)-等变图神经网络，可直接从原子结构预测X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）光谱。该模型在铁氧化物表面数据集上实现了1.0×10⁻³的均方误差，准确再现了主要边缘结构、相对峰强度、前边缘特征和后边缘振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在开发一种能够直接从原子结构预测X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）光谱的准确且高效的替代模型，以加速光谱预测、实现机器学习辅助光谱学并推动数据驱动的材料发现。

Method: XANE(3)结合了张量积消息传递（tensor-product message passing）与球谐边特征（spherical harmonic edge features）、吸收体查询注意力池化（absorber-query attention pooling）、自定义等变层归一化（custom equivariant layer normalization）、自适应门控残差连接（adaptive gated residual connections），以及基于多尺度高斯基（multi-scale Gaussian basis）和可选S型背景项（sigmoidal background term）的光谱读出机制。

Result: 在5,941个铁氧化物表面刻面的FDMNES模拟数据集上，模型在测试集上获得了1.0×10⁻³的光谱均方误差，准确再现了主要边缘结构、相对峰强度、前边缘特征和后边缘振荡。消融研究表明，导数感知目标、自定义等变归一化、吸收体条件注意力池化、自适应门控残差混合和全局背景项均能提升性能。

Conclusion: XANE(3)被确立为XANES模拟的准确高效替代模型，为加速光谱预测、机器学习辅助光谱学和数据驱动的材料发现提供了有前景的途径。有趣的是，容量匹配的纯标量变体实现了可比的逐点重建误差，但导数级保真度降低，表明显式张量通道对于此数据集上的低强度误差并非严格必需，尽管它们对捕捉更精细的光谱结构仍有益处。

Abstract: We present XANE(3), a physics-based E(3)-equivariant graph neural network for predicting X-ray absorption near-edge structure (XANES) spectra directly from atomic structures. The model combines tensor-product message passing with spherical harmonic edge features, absorber-query attention pooling, custom equivariant layer normalization, adaptive gated residual connections, and a spectral readout based on a multi-scale Gaussian basis with an optional sigmoidal background term. To improve line-shape fidelity, training is performed with a composite objective that includes pointwise spectral reconstruction together with first- and second-derivative matching terms. We evaluate the model on a dataset of 5,941 FDMNES simulations of iron oxide surface facets and obtain a spectrum mean squared error of $1.0 \times 10^{-3}$ on the test set. The model accurately reproduces the main edge structure, relative peak intensities, pre-edge features, and post-edge oscillations. Ablation studies show that the derivative-aware objective, custom equivariant normalization, absorber-conditioned attention pooling, adaptive gated residual mixing, and global background term each improve performance. Interestingly, a capacity-matched scalar-only variant achieves comparable pointwise reconstruction error but reduced derivative-level fidelity, indicating that explicit tensorial channels are not strictly required for low intensity error on this dataset, although they remain beneficial for capturing finer spectral structure. These results establish XANE(3) as an accurate and efficient surrogate for XANES simulation and offer a promising route toward accelerated spectral prediction, ML-assisted spectroscopy, and data-driven materials discovery.

</details>


### [116] [Distinct mechanisms underlying in-context learning in transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12151)
*Cole Gibson,Wenping Cui,Gautam Reddy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究对在离散马尔可夫链数据集上训练的transformer进行了完整的机制性表征，揭示了其实现上下文学习（in-context learning）的四种算法相（algorithmic phases）和两种不同的计算机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代分布式网络（特别是transformer）展现出显著的上下文学习能力，能够根据输入统计特性自适应调整计算，使得固定网络可应用于广泛系统的数据。研究旨在完整表征这一行为的机制。

Method: 研究在离散马尔可夫链（discrete Markov chains）的有限集合S上训练transformer，通过机制性分析揭示其算法相。采用对称约束理论（symmetry-constrained theory）解释训练动态，并使用最小模型（minimal models）分离关键特征。

Result: Transformer展现出四种算法相，分别由网络是否记忆（memorize）和泛化（generalize），以及使用1点统计（1-point statistics）还是2点统计（2-point statistics）来表征。这些相通过多层子电路（multi-layer subcircuits）实现，体现了两种不同的上下文自适应计算机制。记忆和泛化相由两个依赖于数据多样性K的边界划分。

Conclusion: Transformer发展出不同的子电路来实现上下文学习，研究确定了有利于特定机制的条件。对称约束理论解释了从1点泛化到2点泛化的尖锐转变，并识别了允许网络泛化的损失景观（loss landscape）关键特征。

Abstract: Modern distributed networks, notably transformers, acquire a remarkable ability (termed `in-context learning') to adapt their computation to input statistics, such that a fixed network can be applied to data from a broad range of systems. Here, we provide a complete mechanistic characterization of this behavior in transformers trained on a finite set $S$ of discrete Markov chains. The transformer displays four algorithmic phases, characterized by whether the network memorizes and generalizes, and whether it uses 1-point or 2-point statistics. We show that the four phases are implemented by multi-layer subcircuits that exemplify two qualitatively distinct mechanisms for implementing context-adaptive computations. Minimal models isolate the key features of both motifs. Memorization and generalization phases are delineated by two boundaries that depend on data diversity, $K = |S|$. The first ($K_1^\ast$) is set by a kinetic competition between subcircuits and the second ($K_2^\ast$) is set by a representational bottleneck. A symmetry-constrained theory of a transformer's training dynamics explains the sharp transition from 1-point to 2-point generalization and identifies key features of the loss landscape that allow the network to generalize. Put together, we show that transformers develop distinct subcircuits to implement in-context learning and identify conditions that favor certain mechanisms over others.

</details>

### [117] [Wavelength-dependent photo-creep in halide perovskite single crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11848)
*Ruitian Chen,Jincong Pang,Lizhong Lang,Jiaze Wu,Mingyu Xie,Shuo Yang,Kaiqi Qiu,Tobin Filleter,Kai Huang,Guangda Niu,Jiang Tang,Yu Zou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了卤化物钙钛矿（halide perovskites）中波长依赖的光致蠕变（photo-creep）现象，发现离子迁移促进位错攀移和蠕变，而载流子俘获抑制位错滑移和相关蠕变，这种竞争关系由波长调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卤化物钙钛矿是极具前景的光电材料，但其在光照下的时间依赖性永久变形（即光致蠕变）机制尚不明确，这限制了材料的机械稳定性。理解这一现象对于提高器件可靠性至关重要。

Method: 采用恒定载荷纳米压痕（constant-load nanoindentation）技术在受控波长光照下研究CsPbBr3和FAPbBr3单晶的光致蠕变现象。结合光致发光（photoluminescence）和光电流（photocurrent）测量分析内在机制。

Result: 相比暗态蠕变，连续绿光（近带隙）使CsPbBr3和FAPbBr3的蠕变分别抑制19%和10%，而紫光（远高于带隙）则分别增强16%和8%。当在蠕变过程中开启光照时，蓝光增强效应最显著，绿光影响最小。光致发光和光电流测量表明，离子迁移促进位错攀移（dislocation climb）和蠕变，而载流子俘获抑制位错滑移（dislocation glide）和相关蠕变。

Conclusion: 卤化物钙钛矿中的光致蠕变行为与传统半导体的光塑性现象不同，由载流子俘获和离子迁移之间的竞争关系调控，这一竞争受波长影响。该研究揭示了卤化物钙钛矿中的光机械效应，阐明了光照下载流子和离子耦合动力学如何影响器件可靠性。

Abstract: Halide perovskites are promising optoelectronic materials, but their time-dependent permanent deformation under illumination (i.e., photo-creep) is poorly understood, limiting their mechanical stability. Here we report wavelength-dependent photo-creep phenomena in CsPbBr3 and FAPbBr3 single crystals, studied by constant-load nanoindentation under controlled light with various wavelengths. Compared with creep in dark, continuous green light (near-bandgap) suppresses creep by 19% in CsPbBr3 and 10% in FAPbBr3, whereas violet (far above-bandgap) light enhances creep by 16% in CsPbBr3 and 8% in FAPbBr3. In contrast, when light is onset during creep, blue light enhances creep most prominently, whereas green light exhibits minimal influence. Such photo-creep behavior in halide perovskites are distinct with photo-plasticity phenomenon in conventional semiconductors. By combining the photoluminescence and photocurrent measurements, we unveil that ion migration promotes dislocation climb and creep, while carrier trapping suppresses dislocation glide and related creep in halide perovskites. Such competition between carrier trapping and ion migration tuned by wavelength governs the photo-creep response. Our findings uncover a photomechanical effect in halide perovskites and highlight how coupled carrier and ion dynamics under illumination affect their device reliability.

</details>


### [118] [Surface-enhanced Raman scattering and density functional theory study of selected-lanthanide-citrate complexes (lanthanide: Tb, Dy, Ho, Er, Tm, Yb and Lu)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11850)
*Hao Jin,Yuko S. Yamamoto*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合表面增强拉曼散射（SERS）和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，分析了镧系元素-柠檬酸盐配合物在488和532 nm激发下的SERS光谱，揭示了相对峰强度随镧系元素变化的规律及其与Ln-O相互作用的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过结合实验与理论方法，深入理解镧系元素-柠檬酸盐配合物的表面增强拉曼散射光谱特征，特别是相对峰强度随镧系元素变化的趋势及其物理化学机制。

Method: 采用表面增强拉曼散射（SERS）实验与密度泛函理论（DFT）计算相结合的方法，使用大核有效核势优化的DFT方法计算模拟SERS光谱，对主要谱带进行归属分析。

Result: 主要谱带935、1060、1315和1485 cm⁻¹分别归属于(C-COO⁻)+(CH₂)、(CH₂)+(C-O--Ln)、sym(COO⁻)+(CH₂)和asym(COO⁻)+(CH₂)振动模式。相对峰强度比值I_935/I_1315和I_1485/I_1315从Dy到Lu逐渐增加，而I_1060/I_1315比值则逐渐减小。

Conclusion: 1060 cm⁻¹谱带相对SERS峰强度的降低归因于更强的Ln-O相互作用和极化率变化的减小，而935和1485 cm⁻¹谱带的增强可能与局部电子分布变化和有效对称敏感性有关。

Abstract: In this study, surface-enhanced Raman scattering (SERS) and density functional theory (DFT) calculations were combined to investigate the SERS spectra of Ln-citrate complexes (Ln: Tb, Dy, Ho, Er, Tm, Yb, and Lu) under 488 and 532 nm excitation. Peak assignment was supported by simulated SERS spectra calculated with an optimized DFT method using large-core effective core potentials. The main bands near 935, 1060, 1315, and 1485 cm-1 were assigned to (C-COO-) + (CH2), (CH2) + (C-O -- Ln), sym(COO-) + (CH2), and asym(COO-) + (CH2), respectively. Relative peak intensities were evaluated by normalizing the bands near 935, 1060, and 1485 cm-1 to that near 1315 cm-1. The ratios I_935/I_1315 and I_1485/I_1315 generally increased from Dy-citrate to Lu-citrate, whereas the I_1060/I_1315 ratio decreased. These trends were observed under both excitation wavelengths. The decrease in relative SERS peak intensity of the 1060 cm-1 band is attributed to stronger Ln-O interaction and reduced polarizability change, whereas the increases of the 935 and 1485 cm-1 bands are likely related to changes in local electronic distribution and effective symmetry sensitivity.

</details>

Abstract: Strongly bound excitons dominate the optical response in many van der Waals semiconductors, yet distinguishing between the different microscopic processes governing exciton dissociation remains challenging. Using time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (TR-ARPES), we independently track exciton and band-edge carrier populations in bulk ReSe$_{\text{2}}$ under resonant excitation. ### [120] [Agentic LLM Reasoning in a Self-Driving Laboratory for Air-Sensitive Lithium Halide Spinel Conductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11957)
*Yuxing Fei,Bernardus Rendy,Xiaochen Yang,Junhee Woo,Xu Huang,Chang Li,Shilong Wang,David Milsted,Yan Zeng,Gerbrand Ceder*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了A-Lab GPSS机器人平台，集成智能AI框架，通过溯因推理（abductive reasoning）和归纳推理（inductive reasoning）实现自主实验设计。平台在手套箱环境中运行，能够合成和表征空气敏感无机材料。

Result: 在包含352个样品的合成实验中，系统探索了广阔的化学空间，实现了19种金属中171种可能成对组合的72%。具有良好离子电导率（> 0.05 mS/cm）和高卤化物尖晶石相纯度的组合比例从最初75个AI提议样品的1.33%增加到最终75个样品的5.33%。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个可扩展的平台，用于复杂空气敏感固态材料的自主发现。通过分析AI的推理过程，揭示了溯因推理和归纳推理在材料发现中的互补策略：前者深入探索已研究区域，后者扩展至新的化学空间。

Abstract: Self-driving laboratories promise to accelerate materials discovery. Yet current automated solid-state synthesis platforms are limited to ambient conditions, thereby precluding their use for air-sensitive materials. Here, we present A-Lab for Glovebox Powder Solid-state Synthesis (A-Lab GPSS), a robotic platform capable of synthesizing and characterizing air-sensitive inorganic materials under strict air-free conditions. By integrating an agentic AI framework into the A-Lab GPSS platform, we structure autonomous experimental design through abductive and inductive reasoning. We deploy this platform to explore the vast compositional space of lithium halide spinel solid-state ionic conductors. Across a synthesis campaign comprising 352 samples with diverse compositions, the system explores a broad chemical space, experimentally realizing 72% of the 171 possible pairwise combinations among the 19 metals considered in this study. Over the course of the campaign, the fraction of compositions exhibiting both good ionic conductivity (> 0.05 mS/cm) and high halide spinel phase purity increases from 1.33% in the first 75 agent-proposed samples to 5.33% in the final 75. Furthermore, by inspecting the AI's reasoning processes, we reveal distinct yet complementary discovery strategies: abductive reasoning interrogates abnormal observations within already explored regions, whereas inductive reasoning expands the search into broader, previously unvisited chemical space. This work establishes a scalable platform for the autonomous discovery of complex, air-sensitive solid-state materials.

### [121] [Fe-H melting curve below 3 GPa: Implications for hydrogen in the lunar core](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12222)
*Jun Takeshita,Kei Hirose,Suyu Fu,Fumiya Sakai,Koutaro Hikosaka*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过高压熔融实验发现氢在低于1 GPa的低压下即可显著溶解于液态铁中，且溶解度随压力增加而增强。在月球核心条件下（5 GPa），氢溶解度可达1.2 wt%，导致密度降低9%，这或许能完全解释月球核心相对于纯铁的密度赤字。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为在约3 GPa以下压力时，氢在核心形成金属中的掺入可忽略不计，因此未考虑氢存在于月球等小型类地天体铁核中的可能性。本研究旨在重新评估氢在低压条件下对铁核密度的影响。

Method: 采用高压熔融实验研究Fe-H体系在H₂饱和条件下的行为，并结合同步辐射X射线衍射（XRD）测量。通过XRD数据中的漫散射信号推导液态Fe-H的密度。

Result: 实验结果表明，Fe-H的熔融曲线在1.0-3.3 GPa压力范围内相比纯铁显著降低，证明氢在低于1 GPa的低压下即可掺入液态铁，且溶解度随压力增加而增强。液态铁中氢的溶解度在3.6 GPa时约为0.9 wt%，在月球核心条件（5 GPa）下可能增至1.2 wt%。

Conclusion: 1.2 wt%的氢含量会导致9%的密度降低，这或许能完全解释月球核心相对于纯铁的观测密度赤字，具体取决于地震学数据对密度的估算。研究挑战了传统关于氢在低压铁核中可忽略不计的假设。

Abstract: It has been assumed that hydrogen is negligibly incorporated into core-forming metals below $\sim$3 GPa, and therefore the presence of hydrogen in iron cores of small terrestrial bodies including the moon has not been considered. Here we performed high-pressure melting experiments on the Fe-H system under H$_2$-saturated conditions, combined with synchrotron X-ray diffraction (XRD) measurements. Results demonstrate substantial depression of the Fe-H melting curve compared to that for Fe at 1.0-3.3 GPa, indicating that hydrogen is incorporated into liquid iron even at low pressures less than 1 GPa and the solubility is enhanced with increasing pressure. Based on the density of liquid Fe-H derived from diffuse scattering signal in XRD data, we found that the solubility of hydrogen in liquid iron is about 0.9 wt% at 3.6 GPa and likely enhanced to 1.2 wt% at 5 GPa corresponding to lunar core conditions. The 1.2 wt% H causes 9 % density reduction, which might fully explain the observed density deficit of the lunar core with respect to iron, depending on the density estimate from seismological data.

</details>


### [122] [Enhancing Laser Surface Texturing through Advanced Machine Learning Techniques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12451)
*Christoph Zwahr,Frederic Schell,Tobias Steege,Andrés Fabián Lasagni*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本章展示了机器学习在激光表面纹理化（Laser Surface Texturing）技术中的应用，通过神经网络和随机森林等算法，基于激光参数和材料数据预测表面粗糙度，实现快速工艺优化并减少实验成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光材料加工中，激光与表面的相互作用受众多因素影响，包括激光脉冲持续时间、波长、脉冲形态以及材料表面粗糙度、热容和导热性等。传统优化方法依赖专家经验且耗时，而复杂非线性关系难以解析建模，需要大量参数变化实验进行经验建模。

Method: 采用机器学习方法，特别是神经网络（neural networks）和随机森林（random forests）等算法，基于激光参数和材料数据来预测表面粗糙度。该方法能够处理工艺参数间的复杂非线性关系。

Result: 机器学习实现了有效的工艺优化、表面性能预测和自动化监控任务，这些任务以往需要专家知识。该方法促进了更快的工艺优化，减少了实验工作量，并实现了预测性可视化，同时保持高精度。

Conclusion: 机器学习为激光表面纹理化技术提供了有前景的解决方案，特别是在工艺参数间相互关系不明确的情况下，能够克服传统方法的挑战，实现高效的过程优化和预测能力。

Abstract: Laser material processing has emerged as a versatile and indispensable tool in various industries, including manufacturing, healthcare, and materials science. However, the interaction of a lasers with surfaces is highly dependent on a large number of factors, including properties of the laser source such as pulse duration, wavelength and pulse form, as well as properties of the material such as surface roughness, heat capacity and thermal conductivity. Therefore, the optimization of laser texturing processes in regards to specific target geometries while maintaining texture quality and process efficiency is a time consuming task that requires experienced operators with expert knowledge of the process and its components. The complex and nonlinear relationships between the various process, laser and material parameters and the resulting surface topography or functionality are challenging to model analytically. Therefore, the fabrication of large numbers of different parameter variations are typically required to enable empirical modeling and process optimization. Machine learning offers a promising approach to overcoming these challenges, particularly when the interrelations between process parameters are not well understood. It enables effective process optimization, surface property prediction, and automated monitoring-tasks that previously required expert knowledge. This chapter demonstrates the application of machine learning to Laser Surface Texturing techniques. Using algorithms such as neural networks and random forests, surface roughness can be predicted based on laser parameters and material data. This facilitates faster process optimization, reduces experimental effort, and enables predictive visualization - all while maintaining high accuracy.

</details>


### [123] [Depth-Resolved Thermal Conductivity of HFCVD Diamond Films via Square-Pulsed Thermometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12522)
*Kexin Zhang,Xiaosong Han,Ershuai Yin,Xin Qian,Junjun Wei,Puqing Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究采用方波脉冲源热测量技术，定量分析了热丝化学气相沉积法制备的~5 μm厚金刚石薄膜在SiC衬底上的深度依赖热导率分布，揭示了从成核界面到薄膜表面的热导率显著增加与晶粒粗化微结构演化的直接关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将高热导率的金刚石薄膜集成到碳化硅（SiC）衬底上，为高功率电子器件热管理提供了有前景的技术路径。然而，需要深入理解金刚石薄膜内部深度依赖的热传输特性，以优化其热管理性能。

Method: 采用热丝化学气相沉积（HFCVD）在SiC衬底上生长~5 μm厚金刚石薄膜，使用方波脉冲源（SPS）热测量技术进行热导率分析。结合电子背散射衍射（EBSD）和透射电子显微镜（TEM）表征微结构演化，并通过频率相关热渗透与深度分辨热传输模型相结合的方法，定量重建热导率分布剖面。

Result: 热导率从成核区域附近的~60 W m^(-1) K^(-1)急剧增加到薄膜表面的~200 W m^(-1) K^(-1)，直接反映了从成核界面到薄膜表面的显著晶粒粗化（grain coarsening）微结构演化。EBSD和TEM分析证实了这种微结构梯度变化。

Conclusion: 研究结果为HFCVD金刚石中梯度热传输提供了物理基础理解，并为下一代功率器件金刚石基热管理层的工程设计提供了实用指导。热导率剖面与微结构演化的直接关联为优化薄膜生长工艺以提高热管理性能指明了方向。

Abstract: The integration of high-thermal-conductivity diamond films onto silicon carbide (SiC) substrates offers a promising pathway for thermal management in high-power electronic devices. Here, we investigate the depth-dependent thermal conductivity of a ~5 μm-thick diamond film grown on SiC by hot-filament chemical vapor deposition (HFCVD) using square-pulsed source (SPS) thermometry. Electron backscatter diffraction (EBSD) and transmission electron microscopy (TEM) reveal pronounced grain coarsening from the nucleation interface to the film surface. By combining frequency-dependent thermal penetration with a depth-resolved thermal transport model, we quantitatively reconstruct the thermal conductivity profile. The thermal conductivity increases sharply from ~60 W m^(-1) K^(-1) near the nucleation region to ~200 W m^(-1) K^(-1) at the surface, directly reflecting the underlying microstructural evolution. These results provide a physically grounded understanding of graded heat transport in HFCVD diamond and offer practical guidance for engineering diamond-based thermal management layers for next-generation power devices.

</details>


### [124] [Kinetic Arrest of a First Order Phase Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12531)
*Sindhunil Barman Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种描述一级相变动力学阻滞（kinetic arrest）的现象学理论，以V₂O₃中的Mott金属-绝缘体相变为研究对象。通过将时间依赖的Ginzburg-Landau动力学映射到受无序影响的Imry-Wortis势能面上，推导出动力学阻滞机制的普适超越条件。研究表明，外延衬底诱导的夹持效应提升了弹性激活势垒，将高对称性的刚玉相捕获至4.2 K，从而结构性地抑制了绝缘态，解释了观察到的忆阻性V-I开关迟滞现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立一级相变动力学阻滞（kinetic arrest）的现象学理论框架，以V₂O₃中的Mott金属-绝缘体相变（Mott metal-insulator transition）作为测试案例。研究动机源于理解应变薄膜中相变动力学阻滞机制及其对忆阻性（memristive）行为的结构调控作用。

Method: 通过定义与高温金属相单斜畸变（monoclinic distortion）相关的序参数φ，并将其时间依赖的Ginzburg-Landau（TDGL）动力学映射到受无序影响的Imry-Wortis势能面上。该方法推导出动力学阻滞机制的普适超越条件（universal transcendental condition），特别关注(001)取向V₂O₃薄膜中外延衬底诱导的夹持效应（epitaxial substrate-induced clamping）。

Result: 研究表明，外延衬底诱导的夹持效应显著提升了弹性激活势垒（elastic activation barriers），将高对称性的刚玉相（corundum phase）捕获至4.2 K。这种对绝缘态的结构性抑制（structural suppression）稳健地解释了观察到的V-I开关迟滞现象（hysteretic V-I switching），这是忆阻性行为（memristive behaviour）的标志性特征。研究识别出"Mott-Glass"作为V₂O₃应变薄膜中结构阻滞的非平衡态。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个预测性框架，用于工程化应变调控的神经形态突触（strain-tuned neuromorphic synapses）。研究识别出"莫特玻璃（Mott-Glass）"作为V₂O₃应变薄膜中结构阻滞的非平衡态（structurally arrested non-equilibrium state），为理解一级相变的动力学阻滞机制及其在神经形态计算中的应用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We report a phenomenological theory for the kinetic arrest (KA) of a first-order phase transition, taking the Mott metal-insulator transition in $V_2O_3$ as a test case. By defining a order parameter $φ$ related to the monoclinic distortion of the high temperature metallic and mapping its Time-Dependent Ginzburg-Landau (TDGL) dynamics onto a disorder-influenced Imry-Wortis landscape, we derive a universal transcendental condition for the mechanism of the kinetic arrest. We demonstrate that epitaxial substrate-induced clamping in (001)-oriented $V_2O_3$ thin films elevates the elastic activation barriers, trapping the high-symmetry corundum phase down to 4.2~K. This structural suppression of the insulating state robustly explains the observed hysteretic $V$-$I$ switching a hallmark of memristive behaviour. Our work identifies a "Mott-Glass" as a structurally arrested non-equilibrium state in the strained thin-film of V$_2$O$_3$. Our work provides a predictive framework for engineering strain-tuned neuromorphic synapses.

</details>


### [125] [Tuning Structure and Magnetism in Large-Scale 2D Ferromagnet Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ through Ni Doping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12571)
*Kacho Imtiyaz Ali Khan,Tauqir Shinwari,Soheil Ershadrad,Majid Ahmadi,Weiben Li,Hua Lv,Frans Munnik,Adriana I. Figueroa,Manuel Valvidares,Sandra Ruiz-Gómez,Lucia Aballe,Jens Herfort,Michael Hanke,Bart Kooi,Biplab Sanyal,João Marcelo J. Lopes*

Conclusion: 分子束外延技术成功实现了对FGT薄膜中Ni掺杂的精确控制，Ni掺杂通过取代和插层机制显著改变了材料的磁性能，特别是抑制了垂直磁各向异性并大幅降低了居里温度。该研究为理解掺杂对二维铁磁体磁性能的影响机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Two-dimensional ferromagnets with strong perpendicular magnetic anisotropy exhibit magnetic order down to the monolayer thickness, beneficial for energy-efficient spintronic devices. In this work, molecular beam epitaxy has been employed to realize controlled Ni-doping in Fe$_{3}$GeTe$_{2}$ (FGT) epitaxial films. MBE not only enables a large-scale growth of 2D films, but also allows a precise control over thickness and doping. X-ray diffraction and scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) reveal the formation of high-quality epitaxial films of pristine and Ni-doped FGT on graphene via van der Waals (vdW) epitaxy. Integrated differential phase contrast STEM images further provide in-depth information on Ni substitution and intercalation into the vdW gaps. Ni incorporation in doped films results in the shrinking of both in-plane and out-of-plane lattice parameters. Superconducting Quantum Interference Device, Hall, and X-ray magnetic circular dichroism measurements were utilized to probe the ferromagnetic properties of the films. Due to both Ni substitution and intercalation into the vdW gaps for Ni-doped FGT films, we observed a suppression of PMA and a drastic reduction in the Curie temperature down to 50 K. Rather than focusing on thermodynamics transition levels, as in earlier work, this present paper focuses on the vertical transitions in a defect configuration diagram of defects in different charge states, representing absorption and emission processes involving carrier capture/emission from/to band edges. ### [128] [Damage dose dependence of deuterium retention in high-temperature self-ion irradiated tungsten](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12612)
*Mikhail Zibrov,Thomas Schwarz-Selinger,Michael Klimenkov,Ute Jäntsch*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 再结晶钨样品在1350 K下接受20 MeV自离子辐照（0.001-2.3 dpa），随后在370 K下用温和氘等离子体（<5 eV/D）进行氘装饰。氘深度分布测量显示，与290 K和800 K辐照相比，最大俘获氘浓度随损伤剂量呈现不同演化规律。透射电镜观察到1350 K辐照样品的纳米空洞，热脱附谱表明主要俘获位点与前两者不同，反应扩散模拟证实氘以D₂气体形式存在于空洞体积中并以D原子形式吸附于空洞表面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用20 MeV自离子在1350 K下辐照再结晶钨样品，损伤剂量范围为0.001-2.3 dpa。随后在370 K下使用温和氘等离子体（<5 eV/D，通量5.6×10¹⁹ D/(m²·s)）进行氘装饰。通过D(³He,p)α核反应分析测量氘深度分布，利用透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy, TEM）观察微观结构，并采用热脱附谱（thermal desorption spectroscopy, TDS）分析氘脱附行为。

Result: 在损伤剂量低于0.1 dpa时，1350 K辐照样品的氘浓度低于800 K辐照样品；但在更高损伤剂量下，氘浓度超过800 K辐照值，在2.3 dpa时达到1.7 at.%，且未显示明显饱和趋势。TEM观察发现1350 K辐照样品中存在纳米空洞，而290 K和800 K辐照样品中未观察到类似结构。TDS分析表明主要氘俘获位点与290 K和800 K辐照不同，反应扩散模拟证实氘以D₂气体形式存在于空洞体积中，并以D原子形式吸附于空洞表面。

Conclusion: 高温（1350 K）辐照在钨中产生独特的纳米空洞缺陷结构，导致氘俘获机制与低温辐照显著不同。氘主要以D₂气体形式储存在空洞体积中，同时以原子形式吸附于空洞表面，这种双重俘获机制解释了观察到的氘浓度演化规律和热脱附行为。

Abstract: Recrystallized tungsten (W) samples were irradiated by 20 MeV self-ions at 1350 K to peak damage doses in the range of 0.001-2.3 dpa. The irradiation-induced defects were then decorated with deuterium (D) by a gentle D plasma exposure ($<5$ eV/D, $5.6 \times 10^{19}$ $\text{D} / (\text{m}^2 \text{s})$) at 370 K. The D depth profiles in the samples were measured using $\rm D(^{3}He,p)α$ nuclear reaction analysis. The maximum trapped D concentration evolves differently with the damage dose compared with the previously studied irradiations at 290 K and 800 K. At the damage doses below 0.1 dpa, the D concentrations are lower than those after the irradiation at 800 K. At higher damage doses, the D concentrations exceed the 800 K values and reach 1.7 at.% at 2.3 dpa, showing no clear tendency towards saturation. Transmission electron microscopy revealed the presence of nm-sized voids in the samples irradiated at 1350 K, in contrast to the ones irradiated at 290 K and 800 K. Thermal desorption spectroscopy (TDS) indicates that the dominant D trapping sites are different compared to the irradiations at 290 K and 800 K. Reaction-diffusion simulations show that the TDS spectra can be described by assuming that D is trapped as $\rm D_2$ gas in the void volume and as D atoms at the void surface.

### [129] [Nonmonotonic Scaling of the Anomalous Hall Effect in a Bicollinear Antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12636)
*Ruifeng Wang,Chi Fang,Ilya Kostanovski,Ke Xiao,Felix Küster,Jenny Davern,Naoto Nagaosa,Stuart S. P. Parkin*

Conclusion: FeTe中的异常霍尔效应响应源于其拓扑能带结构产生的贝里曲率（Berry curvature），突显了拓扑、磁性和电子输运之间复杂的相互作用机制。

Abstract: An anomalous Hall effect (AHE) in antiferromagnetic (AF) systems with no net magnetization is of considerable interest for both fundamental physics and spintronic applications. Of particular interest is the two-dimensional van der Waals antiferromagnet FeTe that has an unusual fully magnetically compensated bicollinear AF structure and exhibits pronounced Kondo interaction leading to strong band renormalization. Here, we investigate the AHE in epitaxial FeTe thin films grown by molecular beam epitaxy. A large anomalous Hall conductivity is exhibited below the Neel temperature (T_N ~ 60 K) and, strikingly, becomes nonlinear at high fields within a narrow temperature window around 49 K, deviating from conventional AHE scaling behavior versus its longitudinal conductivity. Linear fits reveal a pronounced negative peak in the intercept, accompanied by a field-induced canted magnetic moment. The AHE responses are related to the Berry curvature derived from FeTe's topological band structure, highlighting the intricate interplay between topology, magnetism, and electronic transport.

### [130] [Role of diffusion-induced grain boundary migration during molten salt corrosion of a Ni-30Cr alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12670)
*Konnor Walter,Jagadeesh Sure,Adrien Couet,Emmanuelle A. Marquis*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比不同表面处理的Ni-30Cr合金在熔盐中的腐蚀行为，明确证实扩散诱导晶界迁移（DIGM）是合金熔盐腐蚀的关键机制，且微观结构对腐蚀响应具有决定性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ni-Cr合金在熔融氯化物和氟化物盐中的腐蚀通常表现为Cr脱合金化，形成Cr贫化的双连续多孔亚表层，但仅靠晶格扩散无法解释Cr在长距离上的损失机制，这一机制仍存在争议。

Method: 采用两种不同表面处理（电抛光和砂纸打磨）的Ni-30Cr合金，在500°C下暴露于LiCl-KCl-2wt% EuCl3共晶盐中96小时，对比分析其腐蚀行为差异。

Result: 电抛光样品在无快速扩散通道时呈现逐层溶解，动力学受Ni溶解控制；晶界发生扩散诱导晶界迁移（DIGM），形成纯Ni岛。砂纸打磨表面则产生数微米深的互连孔隙和完全Cr贫化，其再结晶形成的致密晶界的DIGM导致了观察到的亚表层微观结构。

Conclusion: 该工作明确证实扩散诱导晶界迁移（DIGM）是合金熔盐腐蚀的关键机制，且微观结构是决定合金腐蚀响应的决定性因素。

Abstract: The response of Ni-Cr alloys to exposure to molten chloride and fluoride salts is typically characterized by Cr dealloying with the formation of a Cr-depleted bi-continuous porous subsurface layer. The exact mechanism behind the loss of Cr over distances unattainable by lattice diffusion alone is still debated. To address this question, two different surface finishes, namely electropolished and sanded, of a Ni-30Cr alloy were exposed to LiCl-KCl-2wt% EuCl3 eutectic salt at 500 °C for 96 hours. In the absence of fast diffusion pathways, dissolution occurred layer by layer and was kinetically controlled by Ni dissolution, as observed over the grain interiors of the electropolished sample. Grain boundaries were subject to diffusion-induced grain boundary migration (DIGM), leading to the formation of pure Ni islands above grain boundaries. This overall behavior contrasted with the sanded surface response that was characterized by several micrometer deep interconnected porosity and complete Cr depletion. DIGM of the dense grain boundaries created by recrystallization of the sanded surface was responsible for the observed sub-surface microstructure. This work unequivocally establishes DIGM as a key mechanism in alloy molten salt corrosion, and microstructure as a decisive contributor to an alloy's corrosion response.

### [131] [Cs$_4$Cr$_7$Te$_{10}$: Interwoven Reconstructed Archimedean and Kagome Lattices with a Possible Phase Transition near 130 K](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12680)
*Zhen Zhao,Ruwen Wang,Hua Zhang,Tong Liu,Haisen Liu,Guojing Hu,Ke Zhu,Senhao Lv,Gang Cao,Chenyu Bai,Hui Guo,Xiaoli Dong,Wu Zhou,Haitao Yang,Hong-Jun Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文报道了一种新型铬基化合物Cs₄Cr₇Te₁₀，其具有由阿基米德3.4.6.4铺砌和Kagome晶格衍生的复杂晶格几何结构，表现出半导体性质和约130 K的相变，为探索关联电子和磁性态提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有复杂晶格几何的铬基材料为研究关联电子和磁性态提供了重要平台，但具有非常规晶体几何的铬基化合物仍鲜有报道。本研究旨在发现新型铬基化合物并探索其物理性质。

Method: 通过合成新型化合物Cs₄Cr₇Te₁₀，采用输运测量（transport measurements）表征其半导体性质，磁化测量（magnetization measurements）分析各向异性，以及比热测量（specific-heat measurements）确认相变的热力学性质。

Result: Cs₄Cr₇Te₁₀具有由阿基米德3.4.6.4铺砌（Archimedean 3.4.6.4 tiling）和Kagome晶格衍生的交织Cr和Te亚晶格。输运测量显示其为半导体，磁化测量发现H//b和H//ac平面间的弱各向异性，并在约130 K处观察到对磁场不敏感的异常。比热测量确认了该相变，熵变仅为0.41 J mol⁻¹ K⁻¹，排除了结构相变，指向可能的电子和/或磁性相变。

Conclusion: Cs₄Cr₇Te₁₀的发现为设计复杂晶体几何结构及其关联的涌现现象（emergent phenomena）提供了新途径，该化合物在约130 K处的相变可能源于电子和/或磁性转变。

Abstract: Chromium-based materials with complex lattice geometries provide an important platform for investigating correlated electronic and magnetic states. However, Cr-based compounds with unusual crystal geometries are still rarely reported. Here, we report a new Cr-based compound, Cs$_4$Cr$_7$Te$_{10}$, featuring interwoven Cr and Te sublattices that can be viewed as reconstructed networks derived from Archimedean 3.4.6.4 tiling and the kagome lattice, respectively. Transport measurements reveal the semiconducting nature in Cs$_4$Cr$_7$Te$_{10}$. Magnetization measurements show a weak anisotropy between H//b and H//ac planes, and uncover an anomaly near 130 K that is insensitive to the applied magnetic fields. Specific-heat measurements further confirm this transition, indicating its bulk thermodynamic nature. The associated entropy change is as small as 0.41 J mol^-1 K^-1, ruling out a structural phase transition and pointing to a possible electronic and/or magnetic phase transition. These results provide a new route for designing complex crystal geometries and exploring their associated emergent phenomena.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维系统中磁相控制对于理解低维涌现磁态至关重要，其中厚度依赖的磁输运能够探测可逆输运或体磁化单独无法捕获的不可逆磁过程。

Method: 对层状反铁磁体MnBi2Te4单晶纳米薄片进行广泛的磁滞磁阻研究，分析其多步磁滞对厚度的非单调依赖关系和非平凡的角度各向异性。

Result: 磁输运特征排除了表面主导磁性和简单体相变磁转变作为主要起源，表明磁不可逆性可能由空间非均匀磁景观中的畴壁钉扎（domain wall pinning）与脱钉过程控制。

Abstract: Controlling magnetic phases in two-dimensional systems, where charge transport is highly sensitive to real-space spin inhomogeneities, is central to understanding emergent magnetic states in reduced dimensions. In this context, thickness-dependent magnetotransport provides access to irreversible magnetic processes that are not captured by reversible transport or bulk magnetization alone. Here we report an extensive study of hysteretic magnetoresistance in single-crystalline nanoscale thin flakes of the layered antiferromagnet MnBi2Te4. The multi-step hysteresis exhibits a pronounced non-monotonic dependence on thickness and displays nontrivial angular anisotropy. The transport signatures rule out surface-dominated magnetism and simple bulk metamagnetic transitions as the primary origin. We argue that the magnetic irreversibility is possibly governed by domain wall pinning and de-pinning processes within a spatially non-uniform magnetic landscape. These results suggest that reduced dimensionality is a key driver of magnetic irreversibility in MnBi2Te4.

### [133] [Topographic patterning in perovskite oxide membranes for local control of strain, nanomechanics and electronic structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12728)
*Marti Ramis,Markos Paradinas,Jose M. Caicedo,Claudio Cazorla,Roger Guzman,Mariona Coll*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单晶钙钛矿氧化物薄膜为探索块体晶体和衬底约束薄膜中无法获得的物理性质提供了强大平台。通过精心设计的褶皱形貌，可以施加局部曲率，实现对功能性质的确定性调控。

Method: 研究采用(00l)取向的La$_{0.7}$Sr$_{0.3}$MnO$_3$ (LSMO)薄膜，厚度范围从4到100纳米，使其自发形成具有厚度依赖周期性和振幅的正弦褶皱（sinusoidal wrinkles）。

Result: 褶皱形貌直接调控薄膜刚度，在最薄的薄膜中产生超过5%的极大局部应变，应变梯度接近$\sim$ 2.5 x 10$^{7}$ m$^{-1}$。这些极端形变抑制了反铁畸变八面体旋转（antiferrodistortive octahedral rotations），稳定了极性畸变，证明了曲率驱动的对称性转变（curvature-driven symmetry transformation）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，不同厚度氧化物薄膜中褶皱诱导的应变梯度可以驱动结构、纳米力学和电子性质的耦合转变，为下一代电子器件提供了独特的功能态工程途径。

Abstract: Single-crystalline perovskite oxide membranes provide a powerful platform to access physical properties that are inaccessible in bulk crystals and substrate-clamped thin films. Within this context, the deliberate fabrication of tailored corrugations provides a reliable mean to impose local curvature enabling deterministic modulation of functional properties. Here, we demonstrate controlled topographic patterning in (00l)-oriented La$_{0.7}$Sr$_{0.3}$MnO$_3$ (LSMO) membranes with thicknesses ranging from 4 to 100 nm where they spontaneously form sinusoidal wrinkles with thickness-dependent periodicity and amplitude. The wrinkle morphology directly modulates membrane stiffness and generates exceptionally large local strains exceeding 5\% with strain gradients approaching $\sim$ 2.5 x 10$^{7}$ m$^{-1}$ in the thinnest membranes. These extreme deformations suppress antiferrodistortive octahedral rotations and stabilize polar distortions, evidencing a curvature-driven symmetry transformation. The surface potential variation reinforces the formation of wrinkled-induced polar patterns being strongly modulated with thickness. The variation of Mn oxidation state from $\sim$ 3.2+ to $\sim$ 2.85+ provides a direct chemical signature of a thickness-controlled electronic transition. These results demonstrate that corrugation-induced strain gradients in oxide membranes with different thicknesses can drive coupled structural, nanomechanical and electronic transformations, offering a singular route to engineer their functional states for next-generation electronic devices.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）研究Al-Cu和Ni-Al面心立方（face-centered cubic）合金中的线性复合体，分析纳米粒子阵列（nanoparticle array）和片状阵列（platelet array）两种复合体形态的塑性机制。

Result: 两种复合体形态均表现出显著的强化效果；除了与粒子的直接相互作用外，附近区域的应力场改变也能限制位错运动；位错-粒子相对取向对强化效果影响显著，当位错应力场与复合体成核条件对齐时观察到最强的阻力。

Abstract: Linear complexions are stable defect states that form along dislocations and recent experiments have demonstrated strengthening effects exceeding classical precipitation hardening predictions, motivating a detailed study of nanoscale strengthening mechanisms. Here, molecular dynamics simulations in Al-Cu and Ni-Al face-centered cubic alloys are used to demonstrate distinct plasticity mechanisms associated with linear complexions. Both nanoparticle array and platelet array complexions exhibit appreciable strengthening. In addition to direct interactions with the particles, stress field modification in nearby regions can restrict dislocation motion as well. Finally, the relative particle-dislocation orientation is found to have a large effect, with the strongest resistance observed when the dislocation stress field aligns with the original complexion nucleation condition. As a whole, these findings provide mechanistic insight into the strengthening observed experimentally and establish design principles for linear complexion-induced strengthening in structural alloys.

*Yuan Fang,Yang Liu,Dmitry V. Averyanov,Ivan S. Sokolov,Alexander N. Taldenkov,Oleg E. Parfenov,Oleg A. Kondratev,Andrey M. Tokmachev,Vyacheslav G. Storchak*

MnSi is a prominent silicide hosting magnetic phases with unconventional properties; however, little is known about magnetic states of MnSi at the 2D limit. Here, we explore the magnetism of ultrathin films of MnSi on silicon, down to a single monolayer. Angle-resolved photoemission spectra suggest exchange splitting of MnSi bands. Magnetization measurements confirm that the ferromagnetic state in MnSi is rather robust with respect to the number of monolayers. Most importantly, the ferromagnetism of ultrathin MnSi films acquires a 2D character, as its effective Curie temperature depends on weak magnetic fields. The present study establishes MnSi monolayers as 2D ferromagnets that can find potential applications in silicon-based spintronics.

Abstract: Prospective spintronic memory and logic devices will benefit from the negligible stray field and ultrafast magnetic dynamics inherent to antiferromagnets [1]. Our findings highlight the potential of piezomagnetic effects in designing advanced spintronic devices, providing an efficient pathway for manipulating antiferromagnetic states and developing energy-efficient memory technology.

### [138] [All optical ultrafast pure spin current in the altermagnet Cr$_2$SO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12824)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维d波交变磁体（如Cr₂SO）作为理想的自旋电子学（spintronics）材料，因其极低的自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）而备受关注。然而，其磁性点群（magnetic point group）和高各向异性谷流形（valley manifolds）似乎阻碍了纯自旋电流的生成，限制了其在超快自旋电流产生中的应用。

Method: 该方法结合了红外谷激发（infrared valley excitation）与太赫兹脉冲包络（THz pulse envelope）。基于谷选择规则（valley selection rule），线性偏振光耦合到自旋相反的谷，同时伴随的太赫兹脉冲赋予谷自旋激发固有的动量位移（momentum shift）。

Result: 在交变磁体Cr₂SO中实现了大且近乎100%纯的自旋电流生成。该方法为在d波二维交变磁体中产生纯自旋电流提供了一条实用且全光学的途径。

Conclusion: 该研究为在极低固有自旋混合的环境中实现自旋的光波控制（lightwave control of spin）开辟了新途径，解决了交变磁体材料在超快纯自旋电流生成方面的限制。

Abstract: All-optical generation of pure spin current -- the flow of spin in the absence of a corresponding charge flow -- relies on a symmetry based compensation of valley charge. The 2d $d$-wave altermagnets, ideal spintronics materials due to a very low spin-orbit coupling, possess a magnetic point group and highly anisotropic valley manifolds that would appear to preclude such current compensation, excluding them as materials for the ultrafast generation of pure spin current. Here we show that infra-red valley excitation combined with a THz pulse envelope allows the generation of large and nearly 100\% pure spin currents in the altermagnet Cr$_2$SO. Our approach is based on a valley selection rule coupling linearly polarized light to spin opposite valleys, along with the intrinsic momentum shift that a co-occurring THz pulse imbues a valley spin excitation with. These results thus provide a practical and all-optical route to the generation of pure spin current in $d$-wave 2d altermagnets, opening a route to lightwave control of spin in an environment with very low intrinsic spin mixing.

### [139] [Order-disorder transition and Na-ion redistribution in NASICON-type Na$_3$FeCr(PO$_4$)$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12828)

Method: 采用温度依赖的同步辐射X射线衍射分析（synchrotron-based X-ray diffraction）和量热测量（calorimetric measurements），通过超结构强度温度依赖性和相分数模型（phase-fraction model）研究结构演化。

Result: 材料在约350K发生从单斜相（C2/c）到菱方相（R3c）的对称性降低转变，伴随c轴和晶胞体积的不连续增加；超结构强度偏离平均场临界行为，符合S型相分数模型；350K转变的焓变显著大于445K异常，表明钠离子构型重排主要发生在较低温度区间。

Conclusion: 衍射和量热结果表明钠有序化通过涉及中间钠构型和有限共存区域的序-无序转变进行，钠空位有序化、晶格应变和对称性降低之间的定量关联揭示了钠传导通道中构型相互作用对NASICON型材料相稳定性的核心调控作用。

Abstract: We report the temperature-dependent synchrotron based X-ray diffraction analysis of NASICON type Na$_3$FeCr(PO$_4$)$_3$ sample, which undergoes a symmetry-lowering structural transition from a monoclinic ($C2/c$) phase with long-range Na-vacancy order to a rhombohedral ($R\bar{3}c$) phase with statistical disordered Na ions. The [FeCr(PO$_4$)$_3$] polyanionic framework remains essentially unchanged, confirming that the transition is governed by redistribution of the Na sublattice rather than by reconstruction of the host framework. The structural evolution is accompanied by a discontinuous increase in the $c$-axis and the unit-cell volume, reflecting the progressive depopulation of the Na(1) sites and transfer of Na ions toward the Na(2) sublattice. The temperature dependence of superstructure intensity found to deviate from mean-field critical behavior, instead, the experimental evolution is accurately captured by a sigmoidal phase-fraction model. The calorimetric measurements show that the enthalpy change for the first transition around 350~K is significantly larger than that of the anomaly around 445 K, indicating the dominant configurational rearrangement of Na ions occurs within the lower-temperature interval. Overall, the diffraction and calorimetric results demonstrate that Na ordering proceeds through an order-disorder transition involving intermediate Na configurations and a finite coexisting regime. The quantitative correlation between Na-vacancy ordering, lattice strain, and symmetry lowering reveals the central role of configurational interactions within the Na conduction channels in governing the phase stability of NASICON-type materials.

</details>


### [140] [Evidence for Umklapp electron scattering emission from metal photocathodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12979)
*I-J. Shan,L. A. Angeloni,W. Andreas Schroeder*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过比较单晶Cu(001)和W(111)光阴极的光谱发射特性与现有光发射理论，发现了一种额外的单光子发射过程，主要影响光发射阈值附近及以下的电子发射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释单晶金属光阴极中观察到的光谱发射特性与现有光发射理论之间的差异，特别是在光发射阈值附近及以下区域的电子发射行为。

Method: 通过比较单晶Cu(001)和W(111)光阴极的测量光谱发射特性与已建立的光发射理论，并采用第一性原理模拟（first-principles simulation）结合直接一步带发射模型（direct one-step band emission model）进行分析。

Result: 研究发现存在一种额外的单光子发射过程，推测由动量共振弗兰克-康登机制（momentum-resonant Franck-Condon mechanism）介导，该机制通过非弹性Umklapp电子散射（inelastic Umklapp electron scattering）实现。模拟结果与两种单晶金属光阴极的量子效率和平均横向能量的测量光谱依赖性一致。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种新的光发射机制，能够解释单晶金属光阴极中观察到的光谱发射特性，为理解光发射阈值附近及以下的电子发射过程提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Comparison of the measured spectral emission properties of single-crystal Cu(001) and W(111) photocathodes to established photoemission theories reveal evidence for an additional one photon emission process predominantly affecting electron emission near and below the photoemission threshold. This additional photoemission process is postulated to be due to a momentum-resonant Franck-Condon mechanism mediated by inelastic Umklapp electron scattering. An initial first-principles simulation of this emission process (involving the electron thermal effective mass, the inelastic electron mean free path at the vacuum level, and the number of Fermi surfaces in the metal), when combined with a direct one-step band emission model, is consistent with the measured spectral dependencies of both the quantum efficiency and mean transverse energy of electron photoemission from the two single-crystal metal photocathodes.

</details>
