### [141] [Polytropic $f(Q)$ cosmology and its implications for the $H_0$ tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11821)
*Raja Solanki*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究采用多态（polytropic）状态方程结合f(Q)引力理论，通过贝叶斯统计方法分析晚期宇宙的暗能量问题，并探讨了哈勃常数（H_0）张力的状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解晚期宇宙现象中的暗能量问题，这是理论和观测宇宙学领域的一个突出张力。工作试图分析宇宙缺失流体的本质，而不直接假设特定的流体形式。

Method: 采用包含自由参数的多态状态方程（polytropic equation of state），并结合基于幂律假设的f(Q)宇宙学背景几何。通过精确宇宙学解和贝叶斯统计方法（Bayesian statistics approach）及emcee集成采样器进行严格数据分析，以获得参数约束。

Result: 研究获得了精确宇宙学解，并通过参数约束解释了减速参数（deceleration parameter）和状态探测器参数（statefinder parameter）等物理兴趣参数。同时展示了多态f(Q)宇宙学模型预测的哈勃常数（H_0）张力状态。

Conclusion: 该工作通过多态状态方程与f(Q)引力理论的结合，为晚期宇宙暗能量问题提供了新的分析框架，并评估了模型对哈勃常数张力的预测能力。

Abstract: Understanding the late-time cosmic phenomenon of the universe commonly referred to as the dark energy problem, which is one of the prominent tension in the field of theoretical as well as observational cosmology. In this work, we attempt to analyze the nature of the missing fluid of the universe. In order to do so, we employ a poly tropic equation of state consisting of free parameters rather assuming directly a particular form of the fluid. In addition, for the background geometry we consider a $f(Q)$ cosmology exhibiting power-law assumption, which is recently proposed and found to be attractive in the study of late-time cosmology. We find exact cosmological solution along with a rigorous data analysis, utilizing the Bayesian statistics approach and the emcee ensemble sampler, to find the parameter constraints and then we interpret the parameters of physical interests such as deceleration and statefinder parameter. Also, we present status of the $H_0$ tension predicted by our polytropic $f(Q)$ cosmological model.

</details>


### [142] [Shadow of rotating black hole surrounded by dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11822)
*Haiyuan Feng,Ziqiang Cai,Rong-Jia Yang,Jinjun Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究将暗物质（DM）环绕的史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild BH）推广到轴对称克尔黑洞（Kerr BH），分析了暗物质质量对黑洞阴影、事件视界和能层结构的影响。研究发现暗物质在临界质量以下影响可忽略，超过阈值则显著扩张黑洞结构，并有助于保持阴影近圆形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质（DM）作为基本宇宙成分，其影响对黑洞（BH）阴影的研究具有重要意义，特别是对于事件视界望远镜（EHT）观测证实的旋转黑洞。研究旨在将暗物质环绕的史瓦西黑洞推广到更一般的轴对称克尔黑洞情形。

Method: 采用纽曼-詹尼斯算法（Newman-Janis Algorithm, NJA）将暗物质环绕的史瓦西黑洞推广到轴对称克尔黑洞，研究由此产生的事件视界和能层结构。通过零测地线（null geodesics）分析暗物质质量对黑洞阴影半径、畸变及相关能量发射率的影响。

Result: 分析表明暗物质在临界质量以下影响可忽略，一旦超过该阈值，所有黑洞结构均显著扩张。暗物质能有效维持阴影的近圆形，即使对于高速旋转的黑洞也是如此。高暗物质质量下的显著结构扩张可能超出当前观测约束。

Conclusion: 暗物质要么在黑洞邻近区域不存在，要么其局域质量必须低于临界值，才能与天体物理观测保持一致。暗物质对维持黑洞阴影的圆形特征具有稳健贡献。

Abstract: Dark matter (DM), a fundamental cosmic component, motivates the study of its influence on black hole (BH) shadows, especially for spinning BHs confirmed by EHT observations. This work generalizes the Schwarzschild BH surrounded by DM to an axisymmetric Kerr BH using the Newman-Janis Algorithm (NJA), investigating the resulting event horizon and ergosphere structures. Employing null geodesics, we examine the effects of DM mass ($Δ$M) on BH shadow, including its radius, distortion, and the associated energy emission rate. Our analysis reveals that DM has a negligible effect below a critical mass, once this threshold is surpassed, all BH structures expand significantly. Furthermore, DM robustly contributes to the shadow maintaining a near circular shape, even for highly spinning BHs. This pronounced structural expansion under high DM mass may potentially exceed current observational constraints, suggesting that DM must either be absent in the immediate vicinity of the BH or its localized mass must remain below this critical value to be consistent with astrophysical observations.

</details>


### [143] [Astrophysical Signatures of Einstein-Skyrme Anti-de Sitter Black Holes: Epicyclic Frequencies and QPO Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11844)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦-斯凯姆（Einstein-Skyrme）理论在反德西特（Anti-de Sitter）时空中静态球对称黑洞周围大质量测试粒子的测地线运动和本轮振荡，通过相对论进动（relativistic precession）模型分析准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillations）数据，发现该黑洞模型能够解释观测到的频率对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索爱因斯坦-斯凯姆（Einstein-Skyrme）理论在反德西特（Anti-de Sitter）时空中黑洞解的性质，特别是测试粒子在该时空背景下的运动特征，以及该理论模型能否解释观测到的准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillations）现象。

Method: 研究方法包括：首先分析黑洞视界结构，识别非极端黑洞（non-extremal BH）、极端黑洞（extremal BH）和裸黑洞（naked BH）三种状态；然后推导有效势能（effective potential），确定最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit）；最后采用相对论进动（relativistic precession）模型，使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov chain Monte Carlo）方法分析来自多个天体的准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillations）数据。

Result: 研究结果显示：在反德西特（Anti-de Sitter）时空中，修正的径向本轮频率（radial epicyclic frequency）呈现独特特征——在大半径处增长并超过轨道频率，导致近星点进动频率改变符号；通过准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillations）数据分析，所有源的后验分布收敛于Q≈0.6，轨道半径接近r≈4.2M，质量与独立估计一致，表明爱因斯坦-斯凯姆-反德西特（ES-AdS）黑洞能够在物理合理的参数范围内容纳观测到的频率对。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，爱因斯坦-斯凯姆（Einstein-Skyrme）理论在反德西特（Anti-de Sitter）时空中的黑洞解能够成功解释观测到的准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillations）现象，参数Q≈0.6具有普适性，且该模型预测的反德西特（AdS）特征——径向频率在大半径处超过轨道频率——是区别于渐近平坦时空的独特信号。

Abstract: We study the geodesic motion and epicyclic oscillations of massive test particles around a static, spherically symmetric black hole (BH) solution of the Einstein--Skyrme (ES) theory in Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime. The lapse function of this BH depends on the Skyrme coupling $η$, a charge-like parameter $Q$ inherited from the Skyrme term, and the cosmological constant $Λ<0$. We first map out the horizon structure and identify three regimes-non-extremal BH (NEBH), extremal BH (EBH), and naked BH (NBH)-showing that the NEBH $\to$ EBH $\to$ NBH transition is governed by $Q$ rather than $η$, which enters $f(r)$ only as a constant shift. We then derive the effective potential (EP), locate the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), and compute the radiative efficiency, finding that $\mathcal{E}_{\rm ISCO}>1$ in AdS renders the standard Novikov-Thorne formula negative. The corrected radial epicyclic frequency $Ω_r$ reveals a distinctive AdS signature: $ν_r$ grows at large $r$ and overtakes the orbital frequency $ν_φ$, causing the periastron precession frequency $ν_p = ν_\varphi - ν_r$ to change sign-a feature absent in asymptotically flat geometries. Adopting the relativistic precession (RP) model for quasi-periodic oscillations (QPOs), we perform a Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis using twin-peak QPO data from XTE~J1550-564, GRO~J1655-40, Sgr~A$^*$, and M82~X-1. The posteriors converge to $Q\approx 0.6$ across all sources, with orbital radii near $r\approx 4.2\,M$ and masses consistent with independent estimates, demonstrating that the ES-AdS BH accommodates the observed frequency pairs within physically motivated parameter ranges.

</details>


### [144] [Quasi-resonances in the vicinity of Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11845)
*S. V. Bolokhov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究结合高阶WKB-Padé计算与时域演化方法，分析了带电爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子黑洞中大质量标量场的准正规模谱，发现标量场质量增加会显著抑制多个分支的阻尼，导致接近准共振的长寿命振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索带电爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton）黑洞中大质量标量场的准正规模（quasinormal modes）谱特性，特别关注标量场质量对振荡阻尼的影响以及伸缩子耦合引起的物理效应。

Method: 采用两种互补方法：高阶WKB-Padé计算和时域演化（time-domain evolution）分析，通过对比验证结果的可靠性，并追踪不同电荷和伸缩子耦合参数下的谱趋势。

Result: 两种方法在可靠范围内高度一致，标量场质量增加会强烈抑制多个分支的阻尼，导致接近准共振（quasi-resonant）的长寿命振荡；伸缩子引起的频移显著大于数值不确定性，表明准共振是标量扩展引力理论中环降光谱学（ringdown spectroscopy）的稳健物理特征。

Conclusion: 研究证实准共振现象是标量扩展引力理论中的稳健物理特征，伸缩子耦合对谱特性的影响显著，这些发现对黑洞环降光谱学具有重要意义，特别是在探测标量场存在和参数约束方面。

Abstract: We study massive scalar quasinormal spectra of charged Einstein--Maxwell--dilaton black holes by combining high-order WKB--Padé calculations with time-domain evolution. The two approaches show close agreement in the regime where both methods are reliable, allowing controlled tracking of spectral trends across different charges and dilaton couplings. We find that increasing scalar-field mass can strongly suppress damping for several branches, signaling an approach to quasi-resonant, very long-lived oscillations. Although WKB is not expected to determine modes extremely close to the real-frequency axis with high precision, the onset of this regime is clear and appears for multiple dilaton couplings, with additional near-resonant behavior in lower-multipole sectors. The dilaton-induced shifts are substantially larger than the estimated numerical uncertainty, indicating that quasi-resonances are a robust physical signature relevant for ringdown spectroscopy in scalar-extended gravity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括计算无质量粒子在克尔-森黑洞周围的引力透镜效应，考虑均匀（homogeneous）和非均匀（inhomogeneous）两种等离子体分布，并详细分析黑洞旋转和电荷对光偏折的影响。

Result: 研究计算了光偏折角（light deflection angle），分析了黑洞旋转和电荷对光弯曲的影响，并检验了两种等离子体配置下的圆形光子轨道（circular photon orbits）条件。与真空情况的比较突显了等离子体在改变光传播中的作用。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了对等离子体效应的更深入理解，有助于改善对旋转带电黑洞观测特征的认识，强调了等离子体介质在引力透镜效应中的重要作用。

Abstract: We investigate the gravitational lensing of massless particles around a Kerr-Sen black hole immersed in a magnetized, cold, pressureless plasma medium. Both homogeneous and inhomogeneous plasma distributions are considered in this study to mimic realistic astrophysical environments. The light deflection angle is computed, and the effects of the black hole's rotation and charge on light bending are analyzed in detail. The conditions for the circular photon orbits are also examined in both plasma configurations. A comparison with the vacuum case (i.e. zero plasma frequency) highlights the role of plasma in modifying the light propagation, and the results obtained provide a deeper insight into plasma effects which improve our understanding of observational signatures of rotating charged black holes.

### [146] [Gravitational wave signatures and periodic orbits of a charged black hole in a Hernquist dark matter halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11863)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this work, we study the motion of massive test particles and the gravitational--wave emission associated with periodic trajectories around a magnetically charged black hole immersed in a \textit{Hernquist} dark matter halo. We begin by analyzing the effective potential and the conditions for stable motion, with particular attention to the marginally bound radius and the innermost stable circular orbit. Our results show that the dark matter parameters, namely the halo density and scale radius, enlarge the allowed region and generally shift the relevant characteristic radii and angular momenta toward larger values. In contrast, the magnetic charge partially counterbalances this behavior. We then examine periodic trajectories through the rational number $q$, which characterizes the relation between the azimuthal and radial frequencies, and construct representative zoom--whirl configurations together with their precessing counterparts. Finally, we investigate the imprints of dark matter and magnetic monopole charge on the gravitational--wave polarizations in the extreme mass--ratio regime.

### [147] [Beyond the Cosmological Constant: Breaking the Geometric Degeneracy of $ f(Q) $ cosmology via Redshift-Space Distortions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11865)
*Ameya Kolhatkar,P. K. Sahoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究对包含晚期修正项1/Q的混合f(Q)模型进行了严格的理论与观测分析，发现该模型在保持早期宇宙结构形成的前提下，其线性耦合参数必须精确为1，导致背景演化与ΛCDM模型存在几何简并性，但在扰动层面展现出引力常数有效抑制的新物理效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索混合f(Q)引力模型，特别是包含晚期修正项1/Q的版本，为ΛCDM模型提供物理上有界且可证伪的替代方案，其独特特征可直接通过下一代星系巡天进行检验。

Method: 采用严格的理论与观测分析方法，首先从解析膨胀历史推导严格的可行性条件，然后使用最新的仅背景观测数据进行马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）分析，最后结合红移空间畸变（RSD）数据研究扰动效应。

Result: 分析表明，保持早期宇宙结构形成要求线性耦合参数精确为1，这导致混合模型的背景演化与ΛCDM模型存在几何简并性。在扰动层面，几何耦合打破了背景简并性，导致有效引力常数G_eff < G_N的晚期抑制，RSD数据的纳入揭示了振幅补偿机制，使得在较弱引力下聚类振幅σ_8膨胀以匹配观测的fσ_8特征。

Conclusion: 通过AIC/DIC统计模型比较显示，纳入增长数据后对混合模型存在中度到弱偏好，同时保持背景宇宙学不变。这为ΛCDM提供了一个物理上有界的替代方案，其在大尺度结构中的可证伪特征可直接通过下一代星系巡天进行检验。

Abstract: We present a rigorous theoretical and observational analysis of the Hybrid $ f(Q) $ class of models by including the late-time modifying $ 1/Q $ term. After deriving strict viability conditions from the analytical expansion history, we show that preserving early-universe structure formation dictates that the linear coupling be exactly unity. This fixes the background of the Hybrid model into a geometric degeneracy with $ Λ$CDM which is confirmed explicitly through MCMC analysis with the latest background-only probes. The physical novelty of this model is manifest in the perturbation sector, where the geometric coupling breaks the background degeneracy and induces a late-time suppression of the effective gravitational constant $ G_{eff} < G_N $. Consequently, the inclusion of RSD data reveals an amplitude compensation mechanism, by which the matching of the signature $ fσ_8 $ of the data causes the clustering amplitude $ σ_8 $ to inflate under weaker gravity. Statistical model comparison through AIC/DIC demonstrates that incorporating growth data yields a moderate to weak preference for the Hybrid model keeping the background cosmology intact. This provides a physically bounded alternative to $ Λ$CDM with a falsifiable signature in the large scale structure, directly testable by the next generation of galaxy surveys.

### [148] [Asymptotic Theorems and Averaging in Scalar Field Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11987)
*Genly Leon,Aleksander Kozak,Claudio Michea*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在整合标量场宇宙学（scalar-field cosmology）的综述性内容与新的解析发展，特别关注振荡场（oscillatory fields）的平均化约简问题，以改进对宇宙模型晚期行为的分析。

Method: 研究方法包括：为振荡场推导平均化约简（averaging reduction）得到有效慢系统；引入均匀导数界（uniform derivative bounds）、Barbalat/LaSalle论证和有限维中心/稳定流形约简（center/stable manifold reduction）；应用动力系统技术（dynamical-systems techniques）进行晚期分析。

Result: 研究结果证明：平衡点的持久性（persistence of equilibria）、衰减估计（decay estimates）以及在小$C^k$扰动下的局部不变流形（local invariant manifolds）；量化了平均耗散如何以$\mathcal{O}(H)$误差提升到完整振荡动力学；获得了广义相对论、各向异性和膜世界（brane-world）场景下$t(a)$、$φ(a)$和$H(a)$的精确积分解（exact quadrature solutions）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功整合了平均化约简与动力系统技术，为振荡标量场宇宙学提供了系统的晚期分析框架，同时获得的精确解使得暴胀可观测量（inflationary observables）的解析计算成为可能。

Abstract: We present a hybrid study that combines a concise review of scalar-field cosmology with new analytic developments that integrate averaging reductions for oscillatory regimes with dynamical-systems techniques. For oscillatory fields, we derive an averaging reduction that yields an effective slow system whose time averages control dissipation; introducing uniform derivative bounds, Barbalat/LaSalle arguments, and a finite-dimensional center/stable manifold reduction, we carry out late-time analysis of the models. We prove persistence of equilibria, decay estimates, and local invariant manifolds under small $C^k$ perturbations of $χ(φ)$ and $G(a)$, quantify how averaged dissipation lifts to the full oscillatory dynamics with an $\mathcal{O}(H)$ error, and provide numerical examples. In addition to asymptotic reductions, we obtain exact quadrature solutions in general relativistic, anisotropic, and brane-world settings, yielding closed-form expressions for $t(a)$, $φ(a)$, and $H(a)$ and enabling analytic computation of inflationary observables.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索量子电动力学修正（通过Euler-Heisenberg黑洞体现）与完美流体暗物质在强引力场中的联合效应，特别是它们对粒子轨道动力学和引力波辐射的影响。

Method: 采用有效度规方法结合量子电动力学修正和暗物质效应，利用有效势形式分析类时测地线动力学；通过有理参数和拓扑指数分类周期轨道，并使用数值kludge方法计算周期轨道产生的引力波信号。

Result: 研究发现完美流体暗物质系统性地改变了稳定性阈值并抑制了波形振幅，而量子电动力学修正增强了视界附近产生的高频分量；识别出强场区域丰富的zoom-whirl运动层次结构，并揭示了与whirl阶段相关的特征性爆发式引力波信号。

Conclusion: EH-PFDM时空中的周期轨道为探测强引力场中的量子修正和暗物质效应提供了灵敏探针，展示了这些物理效应在轨道动力学和引力波特征中的可观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate equatorial periodic orbits and their gravitational wave radiation in the spacetime of an Euler--Heisenberg (EH) black hole surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM). The combined effects of quantum electrodynamic corrections and dark matter are incorporated through an effective metric, and the dynamics of timelike geodesics are analyzed using the effective potential formalism. We derive the conditions for marginally bound and innermost stable circular orbits, classify periodic trajectories using the rational parameter and topological indices, and identify a rich hierarchy of zoom--whirl motions in the strong-field regime. Gravitational wave signals from periodic orbits are computed using the numerical kludge method, revealing characteristic burst-like features associated with whirl phases. Our results show that perfect fluid dark matter systematically modifies the stability thresholds and suppresses the waveform amplitude, while QED corrections enhance high-frequency components generated near the horizon. These findings demonstrate that periodic orbits in the EH--PFDM spacetime provide a sensitive probe of quantum corrections and dark matter effects in strong gravitational fields.

### [150] [Weakly turbulent dynamics on Schwarzschild-AdS black hole spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12118)
*Christoph Kehle,Georgios Moschidis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞外部，对于质量参数的通用值，拟线性三次波动方程的小数据解会出现高阶Sobolev范数的任意膨胀，这反映了从低频到高频的前向能量转移机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于探讨Schwarzschild-AdS作为爱因斯坦真空方程解的非线性稳定性或不稳定性问题。在约束条件下，非线性色散方程的小数据解可能表现出从低频到高频的渐进能量转移，这是驱动弱湍流动力学出现的机制。

Method: 研究方法聚焦于分析Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞外部具有无穷远处Dirichlet边界条件的拟线性三次波动方程。证明策略适用于更广泛的一类背景时空，这些背景表现出零测地线的稳定俘获（stable trapping of null geodesics）。

Result: 主要结果表明，对于质量参数的通用值，该方程的小数据解会出现高阶Sobolev范数的任意膨胀（arbitrary inflation of higher order Sobolev norms），这体现了前向能量转移机制。作为应用，在半球$\mathbb S^3_+$上对保持边界俘获结构的圆形度量的通用扰动，在$\mathbb R \times \mathbb S^3_+$上获得了类似的范数膨胀结论。

Conclusion: 研究证实了在具有稳定零测地线俘获的背景时空上，拟线性波动方程的小数据解能够发生显著的前向能量转移，表现为高阶Sobolev范数的任意膨胀。这一发现为理解Schwarzschild-AdS时空的非线性稳定性问题提供了重要见解。

Abstract: In the presence of confinement, small-data solutions to nonlinear dispersive equations can exhibit a gradual energy transfer from low to high frequencies, a mechanism driving the emergence of weakly turbulent dynamics. We show that such a forward energy transfer, manifested as arbitrary inflation of higher order Sobolev norms, occurs for small-data solutions of a quasilinear cubic wave equation on the Schwarzschild-AdS black hole exterior with Dirichlet conditions at infinity, for generic values of the mass parameter. This result is motivated by the question of nonlinear stability or instability of Schwarzschild-AdS as a solution to the Einstein vacuum equations, but the strategy of proof applies to a broader class of backgrounds exhibiting stable trapping of null geodesics. As an application, we obtain the analogous norm inflation statement on $\mathbb R \times \mathbb S^3_+$ for generic perturbations of the round metric on the hemisphere $\mathbb S^3_+$ preserving the trapping structure at the boundary.

### [151] [Not too close! Evaluating the impact of the baseline on the localization of binary black holes by next-generation gravitational-wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11871)
*Francesco Iacovelli,Luca Reali,Emanuele Berti,Alessandra Corsi,B. S. Sathyaprakash,Digvijay Wadekar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了下一代引力波探测器网络基线长度对双黑洞源定位能力的影响，发现8-11毫秒光行时（约2300-3300公里）的基线长度在定位精度和模态分布上提供了合理折衷，而增加第三台探测器能显著改善定位性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究分析了基线长度对两台Cosmic Explorer探测器网络定位能力的影响，采用了固定参数注入和与最新GWTC-4结果一致的真实双黑洞种群进行分析。重点考察了探测器框架总质量高达约100太阳质量的情况。

Result: 研究发现，对应光行时8-11毫秒（约2300-3300公里）的基线长度提供了合理折衷，能产生主要呈单峰或双峰的天区定位，适合电磁后续观测、统计宿主星系识别和星系互相关研究。较短基线会显著降低定位能力，特别是对高信噪比事件。增加第三台探测器能消除大部分源的定位多峰性。

Conclusion: 两台Cosmic Explorer加LIGO-India网络能为相当比例的事件提供单峰后验分布，而两台Cosmic Explorer加Einstein Telescope网络则能为几乎所有事件提供单峰后验。这些考虑因素应为下一代探测器网络的发展提供有用信息。

Abstract: Next-generation (XG) gravitational-wave detectors, such as Cosmic Explorer (CE) and the Einstein Telescope (ET), will observe compact binary coalescences at unprecedented rates and signal-to-noise ratios (SNRs). Accurate sky localization of these sources is crucial for several aspects of the science case of CE and ET. The localization of most binary black hole (BBH) signals, which will spend at most a few minutes within the XG detector's effective sensitivity band, will continue to rely primarily on timing triangulation across a network of detectors. A key design choice for triangulation is the baseline between instruments. We investigate how the baseline affects the localization capabilities of a two-detector CE network, analyzing both fixed-parameter injections and a realistic BBH population consistent with the latest GWTC-4 results. For detector-frame total masses up to $\sim\!100\,{\rm M}_\odot$, we find that baselines corresponding to light travel times of $8-11$ ms ($\sim\!2300-3300$ km) offer a reasonable compromise, producing predominantly unimodal or bimodal sky localizations suitable for electromagnetic follow-up and statistical host galaxy identification and galaxy cross-correlation studies. Shorter baselines significantly degrade localization, particularly for high SNR events. Crucially, we find that adding a third detector to the network eliminates localization multimodality for a substantial fraction of sources. A network with two CEs and LIGO-India provides unimodal posteriors for a good fraction of events, whereas two CEs plus ET would provide unimodal posteriors for essentially all of them. These considerations should be useful to inform the development of the XG detector network.

### [152] [Rotating Thin Shells in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11888)
*João D. Álvares,Tiago V. Fernandes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity）中构造了连接两个旋转时空的薄壳（thin shell）模型，使用戴维斯连接条件（Davis junction conditions）。研究发现薄壳要么是真空薄壳，要么在一个切向具有非零压力，并分析了真空薄壳的运动轨迹和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于最近在陈-西蒙斯点（Chern-Simons point）发现的具有负宇宙学常数的爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力中的旋转度规解。本文旨在构造连接两个旋转时空的薄壳模型，探索其在爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力理论中的性质。

Method: 采用戴维斯连接条件（Davis junction conditions）构造旋转薄壳，连接两个具有相同旋转度规但不同质量和角动量值的时空。通过分析薄壳的应力-能量张量（stress tensor）和运动方程，研究其物理性质。

Result: 研究发现薄壳要么是真空薄壳，要么在一个切向具有非零压力而其他应力张量分量为零。薄壳运动方程类似于广义相对论（General Relativity）中的连续性方程，但类似GR中壳内禀质量的量与其应力张量无关。真空薄壳在某些情况下会坍缩形成裸奇点（naked singularity）。

Conclusion: 存在两种静态真空薄壳解：一种是稳定的，发生在内外时空均为超极端（overextremal）时；另一种是不稳定的，发生在内外时空视界相互接近且接近极端性（extremality）时。在某些情况下，解会失效，真空薄壳会坍缩形成裸奇点。

Abstract: A rotating metric solution in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity with a negative cosmological constant was recently found in the Chern-Simons point. We construct a rotating thin shell gluing two spacetimes in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity, using the Davis junction conditions. We take the inner and outer spacetimes as replicas of the same rotating metric, with different values of mass and angular momentum. We show that the only possible thin shells either are vacuum thin shells or have a non-zero pressure in one tangential direction while the remaining stress tensor components vanish. We obtain the equation of motion for the shell, which resembles the continuity equation for a shell in General Relativity (GR), even though the quantity analogous to the intrinsic mass of the shell in GR is not connected to its stress tensor. We study the special case of vacuum thin shells connecting two spacetimes with zero hair. We obtain analytically the possible trajectories of the shell, and in certain situations we observe that the solution ceases to be valid. We find cases where the vacuum shell collapses and a naked singularity is formed. There two types of static vacuum thin shell solutions, one being stable occurring when both inner and outer spacetimes are overextremal, and the other unstable occurring when the horizons of inner and outer spacetimes approach each other, and are close to extremality.

</details>


### [153] [Relativistic signatures of scalar dark matter in extreme-mass-ratio inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11893)
*Robrecht Keijzer,Simon Maenaut,Henri Inchauspé,Thomas Hertog*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究开发了计算方法，用于表征这种全新的完全相对论性标量云特征。通过分析标量场质量参数 $Mμ$ 的不同范围，系统研究了极向分量修正的主导效应。

Conclusion: 在大 $Mμ$ 情况下，极向修正项和标量辐射项都高度不可忽略。因此，研究结果支持在超越真空的极端质量比双星（EMRI）波形模板中纳入这些相对论性特征。

Abstract: We study gravitational wave emission by circular extreme-mass-ratio systems in a spherically symmetric scalar environment. Previous studies have focused on the impact of scalar radiation channels, revealing a rich structure of resonances, sharp features and floating orbits. Through the backreaction of the cloud on the metric, corrections to the gravitational sector come in at the same order. We develop the computational methods, and provide a characterization of this new, fully relativistic cloud signature. Remarkably, corrections to the polar sector can dominate all other dissipative corrections. We identify scalar field masses $Mμ\lesssim 0.12$ as the regime where polar can overtake axial and scalar channels at small separation. For small $Mμ$, vacuum dephasing is dominated mostly by conservative and polar cloud corrections, with scalar radiation acting as only a minor correction. At large $Mμ$, both terms terms are shown to be highly non-negligible. Our results therefore motivate including these relativistic signatures in beyond-vacuum EMRI templates.

### [154] [Novel ringdown tests of general relativity with black hole greybody factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11895)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: GreyRing模型在主导(ℓ,m)=(2,2)模式上实现了约${\cal O}(10^{-6})$的失配度，通常优于最先进的时域模型。应用于GW250114事件时，从GreyRing推断的残骸质量和自旋与全信号测量结果一致，且测量精度与标准黑洞光谱学相当或略优。

Conclusion: 基于灰体因子的波形模型为使用铃荡信号进行新的精密强引力检验提供了可能，该模型结合了螺旋-合并-铃荡一致性检验和传统黑洞光谱学的优势，且不依赖于泛音或早期铃荡起始时间的选择。

Abstract: We present GreyRing, a new model for the post-merger signal in black-hole binary coalescences based on the greybody factor of the remnant. The model accurately reproduces the full frequency-domain ringdown signal of a large set of comparable-mass, aligned-spin numerical relativity waveforms, achieving mismatches of order ${\cal O}(10^{-6})$ for the dominant $(\ell,m)=(2,2)$ mode, and typically outperforming state-of-the-art time-domain models. Building on this model, we introduce a novel consistency test of strong gravity based on the greybody factor: the remnant mass and spin inferred from GreyRing can be compared with those obtained through standard black hole spectroscopy. This agnostic test relies exclusively on the post-merger signal and does not require the inclusion of overtones or the choice of very early ringdown starting times, combining the advantages of inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency tests and traditional black hole spectroscopy. We apply the test to GW250114 and find that the remnant mass and spin inferred from GreyRing are consistent with those measured from the full signal. Remarkably, the inferred parameters can be measured with a precision comparable to, or slightly better than, that achieved with standard black-hole spectroscopy. Our greybody-factor waveform model allows for new precision tests of strong gravity using the ringdown signal.

### [155] [Post-Newtonian inspiral waveform model for eccentric precessing binaries with higher-order modes and matter effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11903)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确高效的波形模型对于探索致密双星形成通道和利用当前及未来引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）观测至关重要。现有模型需要扩展以包含偏心、自旋进动、高阶模和物质效应等物理内容。

Method: 模型扩展了pyEFPE，在2.5PN阶以上将准圆轨道贡献作为轨道相位主导项，并纳入所有可用的高阶准圆PN相位修正，包括绝热潮汐效应。同时推广了自旋进程方程的多尺度分析解至高PN阶，并在波形振幅中加入了高达1PN阶的偏心修正，涵盖多个引力波多极矩。

Result: 模型在解析波形模型和数值相对论模拟验证中表现稳健，计算高效，在广泛参数空间内直至接近并合时均能良好吻合。但在质量比极不对称、自旋与轨道角动量高度对齐以及高偏心率等PN展开预期失效的晚期旋进阶段，精度会下降。

Conclusion: pyEFPEHM代表了偏心与进动双星物理完备且高效波形建模的重要进展，为未来纳入更高阶修正、数值相对论校准以及并合-铃荡建模等扩展奠定了基础。

Abstract: We introduce pyEFPEHM, a post-Newtonian (PN) inspiral waveform model for eccentric and spin-precessing compact binaries that includes higher-order modes and matter effects. Accurate and efficient waveform models capturing these effects are essential for probing compact-binary formation channels and exploiting current and future gravitational-wave (GW) observations. pyEFPEHM extends pyEFPE, significantly improving its physical content and accuracy. In particular, we show that above 2.5PN order the quasi-circular contributions to the orbital phasing dominate at each PN order, and incorporate all available higher-order quasi-circular PN corrections to the phasing, including adiabatic tidal effects. We generalize the multiple-scale analysis solution of the spin-precession equations, extending it to higher PN orders and including all available quasi-circular corrections. Finally, we add eccentric corrections up to 1PN order in the waveform amplitudes, including the GW multipoles $(l,|m|)=(2,2),(2,1),(2,0),(3,3),(3,2),(3,1),(3,0),(4,4),(4,2),(4,0)$. We validate pyEFPEHM against analytical waveform models and numerical relativity simulations, showing that it provides a robust and computationally efficient description of the inspiral, with good agreement across a broad region of parameter space and up to close to merger. The accuracy degrades in the late inspiral for systems with very unequal masses ($m_2/m_1 \lesssim 0.1$), significant spins aligned with the orbital angular momentum ($|χ_\mathrm{eff}| \gtrsim 0.5$), and high eccentricities ($e \gtrsim 0.6$), where the PN expansion is expected to break down. pyEFPEHM represents a significant step toward physically complete and efficient waveform modeling of eccentric and precessing binaries, providing a foundation for future extensions including higher-order corrections, calibration to numerical relativity, and merger ringdown modeling.

</details>


### [156] [Distinguish Bardeen-like black holes by Gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11951)
*Limei Yuan,Chen-Hung Hsiao,Yidun Wan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过引力透镜效应分析无柯西视界（Cauchy horizon）的Bardeen类正则黑洞（regular black holes）。在弱场中，偏转角获得正$\ell$依赖修正，产生稍大的爱因斯坦环（Einstein ring）；在强场中，渐近位置$\theta_{\infty}$与史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black holes）相同，但SDL系数、角分离和相对流量比随$\ell$变化。时间延迟也随$\ell$轻微增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过引力透镜效应检验无柯西视界的Bardeen类正则黑洞，并探索其与史瓦西黑洞的可区分性。当前观测数据为这种检验提供了基础，而未来的强场测量可能提供更精确的测试手段。

Method: 研究方法采用引力透镜分析，分别在弱场和强场条件下计算偏转角、爱因斯坦环半径、渐近位置、SDL系数、角分离、相对流量比和时间延迟等可观测量。研究针对特定天体（ESO 325-G004、Sgr A*、M87*）进行数值计算。

Result: 弱场分析显示偏转角获得正$\ell$依赖修正，产生稍大的爱因斯坦环，对ESO 325-G004的预测环半径与当前观测一致。强场分析表明渐近位置$\theta_{\infty}$与史瓦西值相同，但SDL系数、角分离s随$\ell$增加而增加，相对流量比$r_{\mathrm{mag}}$随$\ell$增加而减少。Sgr A*和M87*的相对论像时间延迟也随$\ell$轻微增加。

Conclusion: 结论指出计算的可观测量与当前观测一致，未来对$\Delta T_{2,1}$、s和$r_{\mathrm{mag}}$的强场测量可能为无柯西视界的正则黑洞提供可行检验，并可能区分Bardeen类与史瓦西黑洞。

Abstract: We study Bardeen-like regular black holes without Cauchy horizons via gravitational lensing. In the weak field, the deflection angle receives a positive $\ell$-dependent correction, producing a slightly larger Einstein ring. For the galaxy ESO 325-G004, the predicted ring radius is consistent with current observations. In the strong field, for Sgr A* and M87*, the asymptotic position $θ_{\infty}$ remains identical to the Schwarzschild value; however, SDL coefficients are $\ell$-dependent, the angular separation s increases and the relative flux ratio $r_{\mathrm{mag}}$ decreases as $\ell$ increases. Time delays between relativistic images for Sgr A* and M87* also increase mildly with $\ell$. Our calculated values for these observables remain consistent with current observations. Future strong-field measurements of $ΔT_{2,1}$, s, and $r_{\mathrm{mag}}$ may offer a viable test for regular black holes free of Cauchy horizons and may distinguish Bardeen-like from Schwarzschild black holes.

### [157] [The balance problem for $n$ aligned black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12134)
*Jörg Hennig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种解决广义相对论中多黑洞平衡配置存在性问题的系统方法，通过将复杂的非线性偏微分方程系统简化为有限参数的有理函数分析，为任意数量n个对齐、旋转且可能带电的黑洞配置提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论中一个引人入胜的开放问题是：是否存在多个物理相关黑洞的静止平衡配置。在这种假设性设置中，引力吸引需要被自旋-自旋（spin-spin）和电磁相互作用所平衡。

Method: 通过采用孤子（soliton）方法研究爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein-Maxwell）方程的边界值问题，推导出对称轴上边界数据的最一般形式。得到的轴势（axis potentials）必然是特定形式的有理函数，依赖于有限数量的参数。

Result: 这一强大结果将寻找n-黑洞解的问题从求解高度非线性偏微分方程（PDE）系统简化为分析一个明确定义的有限参数候选解族。该方法适用于任意数量n个对齐、旋转且可能带电的黑洞在渐近平坦时空中的配置。

Conclusion: 研究回顾了特殊情况的已知结果，如真空或电真空（electrovacuum）中单个黑洞的构造性唯一性证明，以及真空中两个静止黑洞的非存在性证明，并提出了更一般配置的开放问题。

Abstract: An intriguing open problem in general relativity is whether a stationary equilibrium configuration of multiple, physically relevant black holes can exist. In such a hypothetical setup, the gravitational attraction would need to be balanced by the repulsive spin-spin and electromagnetic interactions. This contribution reports on a method to address this problem for an arbitrary number of $n$ aligned, rotating and possibly charged black holes in an asymptotically flat spacetime. By employing soliton methods to study the underlying boundary value problem for the Einstein-Maxwell equations, we derive the most general form of the boundary data on the symmetry axis. The resulting axis potentials are necessarily rational functions of a specific form, depending on a finite number of parameters. This powerful result reduces the search for $n$-black-hole solutions from solving a highly nonlinear PDE system to analysing a well-defined, finite-parameter family of candidate solutions. We briefly review known results for special cases, such as the constructive uniqueness proofs for a single black hole in vacuum or electrovacuum, and the non-existence proof for two stationary black holes in vacuum, before stating the open problem for more general configurations.

### [159] [Mixmaster chaos in a quantum scenario:a Deformed Algebra approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12760)
*Eleonora Giovannetti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Mixmaster模型在量子化后混沌行为的命运，发现两种量子引力方法（圈量子引力和弦理论）的变形对易关系均能消除经典混沌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究Mixmaster模型在量子化水平下的混沌命运，特别关注当系统提升到量子层面时，经典混沌行为是否会被保留或改变。

Method: 采用变形对易关系（Deformed Commutation Relations）处理Misner各向异性变量，其变形代数与两种量子引力方法相关：圈量子引力（Loop Quantum Gravity）和弦理论（String Theory）。该方法自然实现了空间变量（即各向异性）之间的非对易性（Non-Commutativity）。在半经典极限下，变形对易子变为变形泊松括号（Deformed Poisson Brackets）。

Result: 推导了两种情况下修正的Belinskii-Khalatnikov-Lifshitz映射，其性质决定了经典层面的动力学混沌行为。结果表明，两种情况下混沌均被消除：根据变形符号的不同，动力学要么稳定在两个几乎恒定角度之间的振荡，要么在有限次迭代后停止反射，并以最后一个简单的Kasner解达到奇点。

Conclusion: Mixmaster模型在量子化后，通过变形对易关系实现的量子引力效应能够消除经典混沌行为，具体表现为动力学要么进入稳定振荡，要么以简单Kasner解结束演化。

Abstract: In this work, we address the question about the fate of chaos in the Mixmaster model when we promote the system at a quantum level. We consider Deformed Commutation Relations for the Misner anisotropic variables, whose Deformed Algebras are related to two different Quantum Gravity approaches, i.e. Loop Quantum Gravity and String Theory. Also, this approach naturally implements a form of Non-Commutativity between the space variables, i.e. the anisotropies, that live in a two-dimensional space. In particular, we consider the deformation in the semiclassical limit, where the Deformed Commutators become Deformed Poisson Brackets. Then, we derive the modified Belinskii-Khalatnikov-Lifshitz map in both cases, whose properties determine the chaotic behavior for the dynamics at a classical level. The result is that chaos is removed in both cases. In fact, depending on the sign of the deformation, the dynamics will either settle into oscillations between two almost-constant angles, or stop reflecting after a finite number of iterations and reach the singularity as one last simple Kasner solution.

Conclusion: 暗物质加热机制不仅为第九行星提供可能的加热来源，还产生特定的观测特征，为探测这颗可能存在的暗天体提供了新的观测窗口，特别是通过红外辐射特征。

Since no optical counterpart of Planet 9 was observed, it is reasonable to assume that it has a very low luminosity. Various proposals on the nature of Planet 9 have been advanced, including the possibility that it is a black hole, an axion or a dark matter star. We propose that dark matter heating of Planet 9 could generate a thermal radio flux that could allow its observational detection, even if Planet 9 is a very dark object. We estimate the dark matter impact parameter, the mass and the kinetic energy deposition rates, as well as the surface temperature of Planet 9. By adopting a specific model for the time evolution of the planet, and assuming a long time capture of dark matter, the surface temperature of Planet 9, and the spectral features of the emitted radiation are obtained. Our results indicate that dark matter capture may provide an efficient mechanism for the heating of Planet 9, and also provide a specific observational signature of the planet. The numerical evaluations depend on the unknown value of the dark matter-ordinary matter interaction cross-section, with the estimates obtained as a function of its ratio and the saturation cross section for dark matter to deposit its entire energy. For a value of this ratio of $10^{-10}$, and for a dark matter density of the order of $1.32\times 10^{-17}$ g/cm$^3$, in a few Gyrs the surface temperature of Planet 9 can reach values of the order of 200 K, or even higher, with a maximum wavelength of around $λ_{max}=1.44\times 10^{-3}$ cm, situated in the infrared domain.

In this work, we model the spectral properties of analogue black holes sourced by broadband stochastic noise, a crucial aspect in realistic experiments that poses substantial challenges for established data-analysis techniques. ### [162] [Cosmologically viable non-polynomial quasi-topological gravity: explicit models, $Λ$CDM limit and observational constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13002)

Method: 首先建立宇宙学可行性的普遍条件，并构建明确实现，包括多项式、四次、幂律和非多项式模型。然后重点分析四次和幂律情况，使用贝叶斯MCMC分析将模型与Ia型超新星、宇宙计时器和重子声学振荡的观测数据进行对比。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological implications of non-polynomial quasi-topological gravity (NPQTG), a novel class of modified gravitational theories in which the background dynamics is encoded in a single function of the Hubble parameter. This framework provides a minimal and theoretically consistent extension of general relativity, incorporating higher-curvature effects while preserving second-order field equations and avoiding higher-derivative instabilities. We first establish the general conditions for cosmological viability and construct explicit realizations, including polynomial, quartic, power-law and non-polynomial models, demonstrating how different functional forms lead to distinct expansion histories. Focusing on the quartic and power-law cases, we show that the resulting cosmological evolution reproduces the standard thermal history of the Universe and gives rise to an effective dark-energy sector of geometric origin, with dynamical equation-of-state behavior that can lie in the quintessence or phantom regime. We then confront the models with observational data from Type Ia Supernovae, Cosmic Chronometers, and Baryon Acoustic Oscillations, using a Bayesian MCMC analysis. We find that both models provide an excellent fit to the data, remaining fully compatible with current constraints and statistically competitive with $Λ$CDM. Our results demonstrate that NPQTG offers a simple and efficient framework for describing late-time cosmic acceleration with dynamical dark energy, while maintaining theoretical consistency and observational viability.

### [163] [Buchdahl Limit and TOV Equations in Interacting Vacuum Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13011)

Conclusion: 结论表明，相互作用真空（interacting vacuum）提供了一种绕过经典几何界限的物理机制，有可能支持先前被认为是奇异的超致密天体（ultra-compact objects）。

Abstract: We investigate the stability of ultra-compact stellar configurations in the context of an interacting vacuum component. By extending the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations to include a covariant energy exchange between the fluid and vacuum sectors, we examine how the classical Buchdahl stability limit is modified. We analyze two phenomenological interaction models: a coupling to the matter energy density gradient and a direct coupling to the spacetime curvature. Numerical integration reveals that while standard General Relativity predicts a central pressure divergence as the compactness approaches the Buchdahl threshold, the interaction term $Q_ν$ relaxes the pressure gradient and maintains a finite, well-behaved central pressure for proper domains of the coupling parameter. These results demonstrate that an interacting vacuum provides a physical mechanism to bypass classical geometric bounds, potentially supporting ultra-compact objects in regimes previously considered singular.

</details>

### [164] [Raman response in superconducting multiorbital systems with application to nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11997)
*Matías Bejas,Jun Zhan,Xianxin Wu,Andreas P. Schnyder,Andrés Greco*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过电子拉曼散射（electronic Raman scattering）分析镍基超导体的超导能隙特征，针对三种不同轨道模型（双轨道单层、双轨道双层、单轨道双层）计算拉曼响应，以确定配对对称性（pairing symmetry）的特征指纹，为理解镍基超导机制提供理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压和薄膜镍基超导体中高温超导性的发现是凝聚态物理领域的重要课题。理解超导起源、多轨道物理（multiorbital physics）的作用，以及能隙大小和对称性对于揭示镍基超导机制至关重要。电子拉曼散射是研究能隙主要特征的有力工具。

Method: 研究分析了三种不同模型的超导相拉曼响应：包含d_{x^2-y^2}和d_{z^2}轨道的双轨道模型（单层和双层），以及仅含d_{x^2-y^2}轨道的双层模型。针对每种模型考虑了不同配对对称性，并确定其在拉曼响应中的特征指纹。对于双轨道模型，进行了包含轨道间和轨道内散射的全多轨道计算，并与将各能带分开考虑的加性拉曼响应结果进行比较。

Result: 研究确定了不同配对对称性在拉曼响应中的特征指纹，为讨论镍基超导的最小模型及其配对对称性提供了有用结果。获得的结果、讨论以及提出的形式体系对其他多轨道系统也具有普遍意义。

Conclusion: 该研究通过系统分析不同轨道模型和配对对称性的拉曼响应特征，为理解镍基超导体的超导机制和配对对称性提供了理论框架。研究方法和结果不仅适用于镍基超导体，也对其他多轨道超导系统具有参考价值。

Abstract: The recent discovery of high-$T_c$ superconductivity in pressurized and thin film nickelates is nowadays one of the most relevant and active topics in solid-state physics. The origin of superconductivity together with the relevance of multiorbital physics are highly discussed issues in this field. Knowledge of the size of the gap and its symmetry is of fundamental interest to uncover the superconducting mechanism at play in the nickelates. Electronic Raman scattering is a powerful tool to investigate the main characteristics of the gap. Here, we investigate the Raman response in the superconducting phase for three different models: Two-orbital models, including $d_{x^2-y^2}$ and $d_{z^2}$ orbitals, with one and two layers; as well as a bilayer model with the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital as the only active one. For each of these models, we consider different pairing symmetries and determine their characteristic fingerprints in the Raman response. For the two-orbital models, we perform full multiorbital calculations including interorbital and intraorbital scattering, and compare the results with those obtained using the additive Raman response where each band is considered separately. Our results should be useful for discussing the minimal model for superconductivity and its pairing symmetry in nickelates. The obtained results and discussions, as well as the presented formalism, are also of general interest for other multiorbital systems.

</details>


### [165] [Nanoscale electrothermal-switch superconducting diode for electrically programmable superconducting circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12313)
*Tianyu Li,Jiong Li,Chong Li,Peiyuan Huang,Nuo-Zhou Yang,Wuyue Xu,Wen-Cheng Yue,Yang-Yang Lyu,Yihuang Xiong,Xuecou Tu,Tao Tao,Xiaoqing Jia,Qing-Hu Chen,Huabing Wang,Peiheng Wu,Yong-Lei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文展示了一种电热开关超导二极管，通过栅极控制纳米热点动态破坏超导纳米线的反演对称性，实现了高达60%的效率，并能原位电控开关和极性反转，为可编程超导电路提供了可扩展平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管（superconducting diodes）可实现无耗散定向输运，但实现电可调性和可扩展性仍然是电路级集成的主要挑战。本研究旨在解决这一挑战，开发可电控、可扩展的超导二极管平台。

Method: 采用电热开关（electrothermal-switch）机制，通过栅极控制的纳米热点（nanoscale hotspot）动态破坏超导纳米线（superconducting nanowire）的反演对称性。该方法基于光刻兼容设计，利用栅极电流实现原位控制。

Result: 该二极管表现出两种共存的非互易输运机制：一种与非互易超导-正常态转变（nonreciprocal superconducting-to-normal transition）相关，另一种与棘轮状涡旋动力学（ratchet-like vortex dynamics）相关。两种机制效率分别高达42%和60%，并能通过小栅极电流实现原位开关和极性反转。

Conclusion: 该电热开关超导二极管的光刻兼容设计、高性能和栅极控制功能为可编程超导电子学和混合量子系统（hybrid quantum systems）建立了可扩展平台，实现了电可重构的全波和半波整流（full-wave and half-wave rectification）。

Abstract: Superconducting diodes enable dissipationless directional transport, yet achieving electrical tunability and scalability remains a major challenge for circuit-level integration. Here, we demonstrate an electrothermal-switch superconducting diode in which a gate-controlled nanoscale hotspot dynamically breaks inversion symmetry in a superconducting nanowire. This mechanism gives rise to two coexisting nonreciprocal transport regimes-one associated with a nonreciprocal superconducting-to-normal transition and the other with ratchet-like vortex dynamics-both originating from the same electrothermal-switch process. The diode exhibits efficiencies up to 42% and 60% for the two regimes, respectively, and can be electrically switched on, off, or reversed in polarity in situ by applying a small gate current. These capabilities enable programmable superconducting circuits that realize electrically reconfigurable full-wave and half-wave rectification. The lithography-compatible design, high performance, and gate-controlled functionality establish a scalable platform for programmable superconducting electronics and hybrid quantum systems.

</details>


### [166] [Charge-4e/6e superconductivity and chiral metal from 3D chiral superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12328)
*Chu-Tian Gao,Chen Lu,Yu-Bo Liu,Zhiming Pan,Fan Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维立方Oh点群系统中手性超导的热涨落导致的残留相（vestigial phases），揭示了与二维系统不同的相图拓扑结构，发现了手性金属相、电荷-4e和电荷-6e超导态等奇异相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非常规超导（unconventional superconductivity）中的多费米子有序态备受关注，但先前研究主要集中于二维系统或具有有效二维对称性的三维系统。本研究旨在探索三维立方Oh点群系统中手性超导热涨落导致的残留相。

Method: 通过Ginzburg-Landau分析构建低能有效哈密顿量，并采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）系统研究Eg和T2g/T1u不可约表示（irreducible representations）中手性有序的相涨落。

Result: 发现了与二维对应物不同的相图拓扑结构，多相交汇表现为四临界点（tetracritical point）而非二维常见的三相点。对于Eg和T2g/T1u不可约表示，主要手性有序可在特定参数区间熔化为手性金属相；Eg表示下相涨落可诱导电荷-4e相，而T2g和T1u表示下则导致高阶电荷-6e超导态。

Conclusion: 本研究为探索由非平凡三维晶体对称性驱动的奇异残留有序态（vestigial orders）开辟了新途径，揭示了三维系统中相涨落诱导的丰富相行为。

Abstract: Unconventional superconductivity (SC) characterized by multi-fermion orderings has attracted substantial attention. However, previous studies have largely focused on 2D systems or 3D systems with effective 2D symmetries. Here, we investigate the vestigial phases arising from thermal fluctuations of chiral SC in 3D systems governed by the cubic $O_h$ point group. By constructing low-energy effective Hamiltonians via Ginzburg-Landau analysis and conducting Monte Carlo simulations, we systematically investigate the phase fluctuations of chiral orders within the $E_g$ and $T_{2g}/T_{1u}$ irreducible representations (IRRPs). We identify a phase diagram topology different from 2D counterparts, where the multi-phase intersection manifests as a tetracritical point rather than the triple point typically found in 2D systems. We elucidate the evolution of these phases under thermal fluctuations. Our findings reveal that for both $E_g$ and $T_{2g}/T_{1u}$ IRRPs, the primary chiral orders could melt into a chiral metallic phase across specific parameter regimes. Moreover, for the $E_g$ IRRP, phase fluctuation could also induce a charge-$4e$ phase under certain regime, while for the $T_{2g}$ and $T_{1u}$ IRRPs, it leads to a higher-order charge-$6e$ SC state. Our work paves the way for exploring exotic vestigial orders driven by non-trivial 3D crystalline symmetries.

</details>


### [167] [Kinetic instability and superconductivity in Li$_2$AuH$_6$ and Li$_2$AgH$_6$ at ambient pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12367)
*Yucheng Ding,Haoran Chen,Junren Shi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过路径积分分子动力学模拟发现，Li₂AuH₆和Li₂AgH₆在常压下均存在动力学不稳定性。Li₂AgH₆发生晶格坍塌，而Li₂AuH₆虽保持萤石型Li-Au亚晶格稳定，但氢原子部分二聚化并在晶格内扩散。采用随机路径积分方法预测Li₂AuH₆在此状态下的超导转变温度为22K，远低于先前预测值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究已确认Li₂AuH₆和Li₂AgH₆在常压下的热力学不稳定性，但动力学稳定性尚未验证。这两种材料被认为是潜在的高温超导体候选材料，因此需要评估其在实际条件下的稳定性，这对超导性能预测至关重要。

Method: 采用路径积分分子动力学（path integral molecular dynamics）模拟评估Li₂AuH₆和Li₂AgH₆在常压下的动力学稳定性。对于存在扩散原子的Li₂AuH₆系统，使用非微扰的随机路径积分方法（stochastic path-integral approach）研究其超导性质。

Result: 两种化合物均表现出动力学不稳定性：Li₂AgH₆发生晶格坍塌，而Li₂AuH₆保持萤石型Li-Au亚晶格稳定，但氢原子部分二聚化（dimerization）并在主晶格内扩散。氢亚晶格坍塌和氢二聚化导致费米能级态密度降低，使得Li₂AuH₆的超导转变温度预测值为22K，远低于早期预测。

Conclusion: Li₂AuH₆和Li₂AgH₆在常压下均不具备动力学稳定性，这对其作为高温超导体的实际应用前景产生重要影响。氢亚晶格的结构变化显著降低了Li₂AuH₆的超导性能，表明材料稳定性评估对准确预测超导性质至关重要。

Abstract: Li$_2$AuH$_6$ and Li$_2$AgH$_6$ have been proposed as promising candidates for high-temperature superconductors under ambient pressure. While previous studies confirm the dynamic stability of these two thermodynamically unstable systems, their kinetic stability remains to be verified. In this work, we use path integral molecular dynamics simulations to examine the kinetic stability of Li$_2$AuH$_6$ and Li$_2$AgH$_6$ under ambient pressure. We find both compounds are kinetically unstable. Li$_2$AgH$_6$ undergoes lattice collapse, whereas Li$_2$AuH$_6$ retains a stable fluorite-type Li-Au sublattice, but hydrogen atoms partially dimerize into molecules and diffuse within the host lattice. Using the stochastic path-integral approach, which is a nonperturbative approach applicable to systems with diffusive atoms, we investigate the superconductivity of Li$_2$AuH$_6$ in this state. We predict a superconducting transition temperature of 22 K, well below earlier predictions, due to the low density of states at the Fermi level caused by the collapse of hydrogen sublattice and hydrogen dimerization.

</details>


### [168] [Surface-induced vortex core restructuring in a spin-triplet superfluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12682)
*Riku Rantanen,Mikael Huppunen,Erkki Thuneberg,Vladimir Eltsov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 数值模拟显示，自旋三重态（spin-triplet）超流体$^3$He中的量子化涡旋（quantized vortex）结构在表面附近发生显著改变，导致沿涡旋线方向的不均匀性，其核心结构与体材料中完全不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观测量子化涡旋结构可为超流体或超导体的配对性质提供证据并确定其序参量（order parameter）。自旋三重态超流体$^3$He支持多种涡旋结构，但此前主要在体材料中被计算和识别。

Method: 通过数值模拟方法研究$^3$He涡旋核心在表面附近的改变。分析结合了三重态配对中的自旋轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interaction）与表面引起的对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）效应。

Result: 涡旋核心在表面附近被强烈改变，导致沿涡旋线方向的结构不均匀性。该效应相对于核心序参量各向异性轴与表面法线的相对取向呈现不对称性。在广泛的外部条件下，表面处的涡旋结构与体材料中完全不同。

Conclusion: 表面受限的涡旋核心观测在三重态候选系统中可能无法反映体材料结构。研究提出通过测量超流体$^3$He-B薄板中涡旋结构的转变来进行实验验证。

Abstract: Observing the structure of quantized vortices can provide evidence for the pairing nature of a superfluid or superconductor and pinpoint its order parameter. Spin-triplet superfluid $^3$He supports a variety of vortices, calculated and identified so far in bulk fluid. We show numerically that the vortex core in $^3$He is strongly altered near a surface, resulting in a structure inhomogeneous along the vortex line. The effect is asymmetric with respect to the relative orientation of the core order parameter anisotropy axis and the surface normal. In a wide range of external conditions, the vortex structure at the surface is found to be completely different from that in bulk. The effect originates from the combination of spin-orbit interaction in triplet pairing with the symmetry breaking by the surface. As an implication, surface-limited vortex core observations in a triplet-candidate system may not reflect the bulk structure. We propose an experimental verification of the effect by measuring a transition in the vortex structure in thin slabs of superfluid $^3$He-B.

</details>


### [169] [Robust realization of spin-polarized specular Andreev reflection in V$_2$O-based altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12695)
*Yutaro Nagae,Andreas P. Schnyder,Satoshi Ikegaya*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该理论研究常规超导体与V₂O基交变磁体（altermagnet）结中的电荷输运，展示了具有独特自旋极化的镜面安德烈夫反射（specular Andreev reflection）的稳健出现，并提出了通过非局域电导测量检测该效应的多端装置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索常规超导体与V₂O基交变磁体结中的电荷输运特性，该交变磁体展现出独特的自旋分裂准一维费米面（spin-split quasi-one-dimensional Fermi surfaces）。

Method: 采用基于微观动机的六轨道模型（six-orbital model）描述交变磁体，该模型包含与V和O位点相关的亚晶格自由度（sublattice degrees of freedom）。在不同边界条件下进行计算，并提出多端装置（multiterminal setup）通过非局域电导测量（nonlocal conductance measurements）检测镜面安德烈夫反射。

Result: 研究结果表明镜面安德烈夫反射的稳健出现具有独特的自旋极化特性，证实V₂O基交变磁体是实现自旋分辨库珀对分裂（spin-resolved Cooper pair splitting）的有前景平台。

Conclusion: V₂O基交变磁体为产生能量纠缠电子对（energy-entangled electron pairs）所需的自旋分辨库珀对分裂提供了有前景的实现平台，该结论通过理论计算和多端检测方案得到验证。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate charge transport in a junction between a conventional superconductor and a V$_2$O-based altermagnet exhibiting distinctive spin-split quasi-one-dimensional Fermi surfaces. The altermagnet is described by a microscopically motivated six-orbital model that incorporates sublattice degrees of freedom associated with both V and O sites. Based on calculations performed under various boundary conditions, we demonstrate the robust emergence of specular Andreev reflection with a distinctive spin polarization. Furthermore, we propose an efficient multiterminal setup to detect this specular Andreev reflection through nonlocal conductance measurements. Our results establish V$_2$O-based altermagnets as a promising platform for realizing spin-resolved Cooper pair splitting, which is essential for generating energy-entangled electron pairs.

</details>


### [170] [Josephson coupling through a magnetic racetrack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12742)
*A. A. Mazanik,F. S. Bergeret*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了铁磁跑道中布洛赫型畴壁对超导约瑟夫森耦合的影响，揭示了畴壁位置和取向对超电流空间分布及临界电流的显著调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索超导性与铁磁跑道中布洛赫型畴壁（Bloch-like domain wall）之间的相互作用，为超导跑道器件设计提供原理指导，并确立畴壁作为跑道存储器架构中读出方案的可控元件。

Method: 通过理论分析研究两个超导电极之间由铁磁跑道连接的约瑟夫森耦合系统，重点关注布洛赫型畴壁与超导性的相互作用机制。

Result: 研究发现畴壁导致超电流呈现高度非平凡的空间分布，包括电流环的形成，且对畴壁位置和取向极为敏感。约瑟夫森临界电流可通过畴壁位置有效调控，表现出显著变化和可调的0-π转变。

Conclusion: 该研究为超导跑道器件提供了清晰的设计原则，并确立了畴壁作为跑道存储器架构中读出方案的有效控制元件，展示了超导-铁磁混合系统的调控潜力。

Abstract: We investigate the Josephson coupling between two superconducting electrodes connected by a ferromagnetic racetrack hosting a Bloch-like domain wall (DW). We show that the interplay between superconductivity and the DW leads to highly non-trivial spatial distributions of the supercurrent, including the formation of current loops and a strong sensitivity to the DW position and orientation. We further demonstrate that the Josephson critical current $I_c$ can be efficiently controlled by the DW position along the racetrack, exhibiting pronounced variations and tunable $0$--$π$ transitions. These results provide clear design principles for superconducting racetrack devices and establish domain walls as a viable control element for readout schemes in racetrack memory architectures.

### [171] [Generalized symmetries and emergence in axion effective field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11877)
*Dan Sehayek,Nathaniel Craig*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了轴子有效场论（axion EFT）中高阶对称性结构（higher-group and non-invertible symmetries）的现象学后果，揭示了这些对称性对红外能标出现的参数约束，并阐明这些约束通过拓扑缺陷（topological defects）上的反常流入（anomaly inflow）普遍饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索轴子有效场论中高阶对称性结构（包括高阶群和非可逆对称性）的现象学意义。这些对称性结构对红外能标处不同对称性的出现施加了参数约束，为理解紫外物理提供了指引。

Method: 研究方法包括澄清和分析轴子有效场论（耦合于阿贝尔和非阿贝尔规范玻色子，包含或不包含带电物质）中的涌现约束（emergence constraints）。通过分析反常流入机制和拓扑缺陷的作用，系统研究了这些约束的性质。

Result: 研究结果表明，涌现约束通过拓扑缺陷上的反常流入普遍饱和。在微扰紫外完备理论中，由于能标的参数分离，这些约束是冗余的（supererogatory）。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了轴子有效场论中高阶对称性结构对能标层次的重要约束作用，揭示了反常流入机制在实现这些约束中的普遍性，为理解紫外物理与红外现象之间的关系提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the phenomenological consequences of higher symmetry structures in axion effective field theories. Higher-group and non-invertible symmetries impose parametric constraints on the energy scales at which different symmetries can emerge in the infrared, providing a guide to the ultraviolet physics. We clarify and analyze these emergence constraints in axion EFTs coupled to abelian and non-abelian gauge bosons, with and without charged matter. We show that emergence constraints are universally saturated by anomaly inflow onto topological defects, while in perturbative UV completions they are supererogatory owing to the parametric separation of scales.

</details>


### [172] [Manifest duality and Lorentz covariance for linearised gravity as edge modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11884)
*Calvin Y. -R. Chen,Euihun Joung,Karapet Mkrtchyan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文首次提出了四维线性化引力的洛伦兹协变且对偶民主的表述，通过将四维共形代数视为AdS₅的等距对称性，将无质量自旋-2场实现为五维拓扑场的边缘模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有四维线性化引力理论缺乏同时满足洛伦兹协变性和对偶民主性的表述。对偶民主性要求电-磁对偶相关的两个框架被平等对待，这是理论构造中的重要目标。

Method: 关键洞见是将四维共形代数𝔰𝔬(2,4)视为AdS₅的等距对称性，并将无质量自旋-2场实现为五维拓扑场的边缘模。通过协变边界约化程序获得所需的四维作用量。

Result: 成功构建了首个同时满足洛伦兹协变性和对偶民主性的四维线性化引力表述。该表述将引力场视为五维拓扑理论在特定𝔰𝔬(2,4)有限维表示中的边界模式。

Conclusion: 该工作为四维线性化引力提供了新颖的几何理解框架，通过AdS/CFT对偶的视角将引力场实现为更高维拓扑理论的边缘激发模式。

Abstract: We present the first formulation of linearised gravity in four dimensions which is manifestly Lorentz covariant and democratic, i.e. treats the two frames related by electric-magnetic duality on equal footing. It is well-known that four-dimensional linearised gravity belongs to a class of singleton representations of the four-dimensional conformal algebra $\mathfrak{so}(2,4)$. Our key insight is viewing this algebra as the isometry of $\text{AdS}_5$ and realising the massless spin-2 field as an edge mode of a five-dimensional topological field taking values in a specific finite-dimensional representation of $\mathfrak{so}(2,4)$. The desired four-dimensional action is then found by a covariant boundary reduction procedure.

Method: 通过全息对偶方法，在AdS$_4 \times \mathbb{CP}^3$背景中分析基本弦（fundamental strings）围绕经典AdS$_2$解的涨落，将世界面激发映射到对偶dCFT中驱动流动的算符，并确定其标度维度（scaling dimensions），包括来自单圈世界面效应的次领头阶修正。

Result: 建立了不同弦坐标边界条件对应不同算符的对应关系，并通过插值边界条件实现了RG流动的几何实现。对于费米性1/2 BPS、玻色性1/6 BPS和非超对称Wilson loop，1/2 BPS环在红外（IR）稳定，1/6 BPS环作为鞍点，非超对称构型作为自然紫外（UV）不动点出现。

Abstract: Wilson loop operators in ABJM theory provide a rich arena for studying defect conformal field theories (dCFTs) and the renormalization group (RG) flows connecting them. While these are well understood at weak coupling, a complete strong-coupling picture remains an open problem. In this paper, we present a systematic analysis of defect RG flows in ABJM at strong coupling, via holography. By examining fluctuations of fundamental strings in the AdS$_4 \times \mathbb{CP}^3$ background around classical AdS$_2$ solutions, we map worldsheet excitations to the operators in the dual dCFT which are responsible for the flows and determine their scaling dimensions, including subleading corrections from one-loop worldsheet effects. We show how different boundary conditions on string coordinates correspond to distinct operators and provide a geometric realization of the RG flows through interpolating boundary conditions. We apply this framework to fermionic 1/2 BPS, bosonic 1/6 BPS, and non-supersymmetric Wilson loops, establishing a coherent strong-coupling picture in which the 1/2 BPS loop is IR stable, the 1/6 BPS loop acts as a saddle point, and the non-supersymmetric configuration emerges as a natural UV fixed point. We also advance a proposal for the holographic dual of a second non-supersymmetric loop, in terms of averaging over Dirichlet boundary conditions.

The method has been applied to the Airy and Bessel models, various minimal string and superstring theories, and their associated intersection theory settings, ordinary and various kinds of supersymmetric Weil-Petersson volumes, and more besides. For all these cases, their $W_{g,n}(\{z_i\})$ are just all specializations of the {\it same} universal formulae. A special variant of the method useful for ${N}{=}1$ supersymmetric cases is also presented. It allows for swift derivations of Norbury's three closed-form formulae for the volumes $V_{g,n}$ ($g{=}1,2,3$) of ${ N}{=}1$ supersymmetric Weil-Petersson volumes, and generalizations of them to a wider set of models. Moreover a new closed-form formula for the genus 4 case $V_{4,n}$ is derived. The straightforward method for how to derive such formulae for $g{>}4$ cases is described. ### [176] [From Vacuum to Nucleon: Exact Fixed-Scale Matching of Holographic Current Correlators to QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12037)
*Kiminad A. Mamo*

Main category: hep-th

Method: 从固定j的t道Witten图出发，推导出因子化的全息康普顿振幅（holographic Compton amplitude）。在共形极限下，该振幅的上顶点仅依赖于虚光子的纯AdS体波函数，产生精确的高斯超几何核（Gauss hypergeometric kernel）。

Abstract: Holographic QCD reproduces the leading short-distance vector-current two-point function in vacuum, fixing the bulk gauge coupling by matching the logarithmic $Q^2$ dependence of the boundary current correlator. We show that this vacuum matching extends to the off-forward hadronic current-current correlator relevant for DDVCS/DVCS. Starting from the fixed-$j$ $t$-channel Witten diagram, we derive a factorized holographic Compton amplitude whose ultraviolet photon vertex is universal and model independent, while all infrared sensitivity is isolated in hadronic conformal moments. In the conformal limit this upper vertex depends only on the pure-AdS bulk wave functions of the virtual photons and yields an exact Gauss hypergeometric kernel. In the collinear window and at a single matching scale $Q=μ=μ_0=μ_\ast$, this kernel matches exactly the $\pm$-basis Wilson coefficients of the singlet conformal operator product expansion in perturbative QCD. The channel dictionary is fixed dynamically: the closed-string branch matches the protected $(-)$ eigenchannel, while the open-string branch matches the unprotected $(+)$ eigenchannel, with the first physical even moment $j=2$ and the distinct $\sqrt{j-2}$ versus $\sqrt{j-1}$ branch points providing the sharpest anchor. The result is therefore an exact fixed-scale matching statement for the hadronic current-current correlator in the fixed-$j$ channel. It identifies the holographic DDVCS/DVCS amplitude as a hadronic generalization of the familiar vacuum current-correlator matching.

### [177] [Holographic Open/Closed Exchange in Double Deeply Virtual Compton Scattering: Fixed--$j$ Structural Matching to the $\pm$-Basis Wilson Coefficients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12038)

Method: 方法从t-通道维滕图（t-channel Witten diagram）出发，推导闭弦固定-j振幅，并通过平行替换规则获得偶自旋开弦通道。采用全息共线因子化（holographic collinear factorization），其中上光子顶点具有普适性和模型无关性，在共形极限下仅依赖于两个虚光子的纯AdS体波函数。

Abstract: We show that, in the collinear regime, the fixed--$j$ holographic double deeply virtual Compton scattering (DDVCS) amplitude contains the same hypergeometric hard kernel as the $\pm$-basis Wilson coefficients of perturbative QCD. Starting from the $t$--channel Witten diagram, we derive the closed-string fixed--$j$ amplitude and obtain the even-spin open-string channel by a parallel replacement rule. After holographic collinear factorization, the upper photon vertex is universal and model independent: in the conformal limit it depends only on the pure-AdS bulk wave functions of the two virtual photons and yields an exact Gauss hypergeometric function of $η^2/ξ^2$. The Mellin exponent $δ_X(j)=j+Δ_X(j)-2=2j+γ_X(j)$ is fixed by Witten-diagram $z$-power counting, while all infrared model dependence is isolated in lower hadronic conformal moments. Comparing with the singlet vector Compton form factor in the conformal operator product expansion, we find that at a single matching scale $Q=μ=μ_0=μ_\ast$ the open channel matches the $(+)$ eigenchannel and the closed channel matches the protected $(-)$ eigenchannel. The sharpest anchor is the first physical even moment $j=2$, together with the distinct $\sqrt{j-1}$ and $\sqrt{j-2}$ branch-point structure of the open and closed trajectories. Logarithmic running deforms only the scale dependence, not the channel dictionary. The result is a fixed--$j$, fixed-scale structural matching statement for holographic DDVCS/DVCS, not a claim of all-scale equality or a global fit.

Interestingly, this connection gives rise to a hermitian (self-adjoint) connection for a real gauge theory on the real bundle ${\rm End}(TX)$ for only specific directions in deformation space, which may be classified using Morse theory. We quantize the deformed theory around these instanton backgrounds, and derive explicit expressions for the partition function in the limit where the complex structure deformation is large. We study anomalies, and the $h$-dependece of the partition function. In particular, coupling the theory to additional gravitational degrees of freedom, we find that the special directions in deformation space give rise to novel anomaly free theories on ${\rm End}(T^{1,0}X)$.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The Euler ensemble was recently supported by large-scale ($4096^3$) direct numerical simulations as the universal statistical attractor of decaying fluid turbulence. Previous mathematical derivations of this ensemble relied on measure-theoretic limits of discrete polygonal loop equations. In this Letter, we present a continuous algebraic derivation. By reformulating the Navier-Stokes equation as a covariant derivative operator flow in the Lagrangian frame, we analytically eliminate advection. Applying Feynman's operational calculus, the 3D non-commutative operator algebra maps to ordering discontinuities (finite-difference jumps) on a 1D momentum loop. This continuous formalism reduces to the discrete, number-theoretic geometric quantization of the Euler ensemble via roots of unity without requiring spatial lattice approximations, demonstrating that macroscopic fluid chaos is a deterministic projection of the Farey sequence.

In both regimes, we obtain the differential and total cross sections and examine their behavior in the short-range ($m_φ \neq 0$) and long-range ($m_φ = 0$) limits, in order to analyze the influence of zero- and finite-temperature effects.

### [182] [Mixed-helicity bracket of celestial symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12854)
*Daniele Pranzetti,Domenico Giuseppe Salluce*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究从协变相空间视角分析了引力与规范理论中混合螺旋度（mixed-helicity）高阶自旋荷的代数结构，发现当限制一个螺旋度到楔形扇区（wedge sector）时，通过引入影子荷（shadow charge）概念可获得闭合代数。在引力情形下构建了BMS代数的对偶质量扩展，在麦克斯韦理论中通过纳入磁荷恢复了电磁中心荷（electromagnetic central charge）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前文献指出，在单螺旋度扇区中，引力与规范理论的celestial对称性可分别增强为$w_{1+\infty}$代数与$S$-代数，但在全理论中结合两个螺旋度扇区存在困难。本研究旨在从协变相空间（covariant phase space）视角解决这一混合螺旋度代数结构问题。

Method: 研究采用协变相空间框架，详细分析了引力与杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）中混合螺旋度高阶自旋荷（higher-spin charges）的括号结构。通过引入影子荷概念，并限制两个螺旋度中的一个到楔形扇区，探索闭合代数的构建方法。

Result: 当限制一个螺旋度到楔形扇区时，所有自旋的荷可通过影子荷概念形成闭合代数。在引力情形下，成功构建了BMS代数的对偶质量扩展（dual mass extension）；在麦克斯韦理论中，通过纳入磁荷（magnetic charges）恢复了先前通过不同方法获得的非零电磁中心荷表达式。

Conclusion: 该研究从协变相空间角度解决了混合螺旋度代数结构的难题，通过引入影子荷和限制条件获得了闭合代数。在低自旋子代数扇区，分别实现了引力中BMS代数的对偶质量扩展和电磁理论中中心荷的恢复，为celestial对称性的完整理解提供了新视角。

Abstract: Celestial symmetries of gravity and gauge theory can be enhanced to a $w_{1+\infty}$ algebra and an $S$-algebra respectively, when restricting to a single graviton/gluon helicity sector. Difficulties in combining both sectors in the full theory have been pointed out in the previous literature. In this work, we face this problem from the covariant phase space perspective and analyze in detail the structure of the mixed-helicity bracket of the higher-spin charges for both gravity and Yang--Mills theory. We show that, when restricting one of the two helicities to the wedge sector, a closed algebra can be obtained for all spins in terms of a notion of shadow charge we introduce. Furthermore, when focusing on the lower spin subalgebra sectors, in the case of gravity, we show that a dual mass extension of the BMS algebra can be consistently constructed; in the case of Maxwell theory, inclusion of magnetic charges allows us to recover a non-vanishing expression for the electromagnetic central charge previously obtained through different methods.

### [183] [The Hidden Symmetries of Yang-Mills Theory in (1+1)-dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12873)
*L. A. Ferreira,G. Luchini,H. Malavazzi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种(1+1)维闵可夫斯基时空中经典杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）与费米子和标量场耦合的积分表述，通过环路空间和乐（holonomy）重构局部动力学，揭示了和乐本征值的路径无关性构成守恒定律，产生无穷层次规范不变、动力学守恒荷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立精确的低维框架，以探究隐藏对称性的代数结构，并理解守恒荷作为物理可观测量（physical observables）的意义。这为探索其在量子体系（如强耦合晶格规范理论）中的作用奠定了经典基础。

Method: 采用环路空间和乐（loop-space holonomy）方法重构局部动力学，运用一阶辛形式主义（first-order symplectic formalism）分析守恒荷的生成作用。通过泊松代数（Poisson algebra）分析，严格证明这些变换保持物理动力学。

Result: 证明了和乐本征值的路径无关性构成守恒定律，产生无穷层次规范不变、动力学守恒荷。这些非阿贝尔荷（non-abelian charges）在基本相空间变量上生成全局对称变换，且这些变换保持物理动力学，使总哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）在至多一阶约束下不变。

Conclusion: 该精确低维框架为研究这些隐藏对称性的代数结构提供了高度可处理的设置，确立了守恒荷作为物理可观测量意义的经典基础，有助于探索其在量子体系（如强耦合晶格规范理论）中的作用。

Abstract: We present an integral formulation of classical Yang-Mills theory coupled to fermionic and scalar matter fields in (1+1)-dimensional Minkowski spacetime. By reformulating the local dynamics in terms of loop-space holonomies, we demonstrate that the path independence of the holonomy eigenvalues constitutes a conservation law, yielding an infinite hierarchy of gauge-invariant, dynamically conserved charges. While a zero-curvature equation is associated with a necessary condition for this path invariance, we note that it is not strictly sufficient on its own. Employing a first-order symplectic formalism, we show that these non-abelian charges generate global symmetry transformations on the fundamental phase-space variables. We rigorously prove that these transformations preserve the physical dynamics, leaving the total Hamiltonian invariant up to first-class constraints. Furthermore, an analysis of the Poisson algebra reveals that these conserved charges are in involution, provided the boundary integration constant lies within the center of the gauge group. This exact, lower-dimensional framework provides a highly tractable setting to investigate the algebraic structures of these hidden symmetries and the meaning of the conserved charges as physical observables, establishing a classical foundation for exploring their role in the quantum regime, such as in strongly coupled lattice gauge theories.

### [184] [Infrared Spectral Gap in a Gluonic Dark Sector as the Origin of the Galactic Acceleration Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12910)
*Gilles Cohen-Tannoudji,Jean-Pierre Gazeau,Hamed Pejhan,Jean-Pierre Treuil*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究提出银河系动力学中观测到的径向加速度关系（radial acceleration relation）源于暗物质（dark sector）的内在红外光谱特性，而非修正引力或星系形成历史。具体而言，QCD迹反常（QCD trace anomaly）通过维度嬗变（dimensional transmutation）在胶子暗物质（gluonic dark sector）中产生一个受表示论保护的红外能隙（infrared spectral gap），其关联长度（correlation length）自然导出观测到的特征加速度尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 银河动力学中的径向加速度关系揭示了一个近乎普适的加速度尺度（约$10^{-10}\,\mathrm{ms^{-2}}$），该尺度在传统的冷暗物质（cold dark matter）框架下无法解释。研究旨在探索这一观测尺度的起源，特别是其是否源于暗物质的内在物理特性而非修正引力理论。

Method: 研究假设一个长寿命、色中性（color-neutral）的胶子真空成分（gluonic vacuum component）在暴胀后（post-inflationary）时代存留，并在大距离尺度上形成光谱刚性（spectrally rigid）的最低权重结构（lowest-weight structure）。该红外组织的微观种子来自QCD迹反常，它打破经典标度不变性并通过维度嬗变在胶子暗物质中产生内在红外尺度。结合洛伦兹协变性（Lorentz covariance）和正能量最低权重幺正实现（positive-energy lowest-weight unitary realization），研究选择了反德西特代数（Anti de Sitter algebra）$\mathfrak{so}(2,3)$作为允许具有表示论保护能隙（representation-theoretically protected gap）的离散态塔（discrete tower of states）的最简对称性。

Result: 该理论框架引入了一个有限关联长度$r_{\texttt{c}}$，它控制暗物质的大尺度相干性（large-scale coherence）。一个由最低权重模式主导的自引力凝聚体（self-gravitating condensate）在标准牛顿引力下产生特征加速度$g^{}_\star = G M_h / r_{\texttt{c}}^2$，其量级与观测到的银河加速度尺度自然一致。

Conclusion: 银河加速度尺度表现为相干胶子暗物质中由迹反常种下的红外光谱能隙的引力印记（gravitational imprint），而非修正引力或逐个星系形成历史的结果。这一框架为观测到的普适加速度尺度提供了基于暗物质内在光谱特性的物理解释。

Abstract: The radial acceleration relation reveals a nearly universal acceleration scale of order $10^{-10}\,\mathrm{ms^{-2}}$ in galactic dynamics, whose origin remains unexplained within conventional cold dark matter scenarios. We propose that this scale arises from an intrinsic infrared spectral property of the dark sector. Specifically, we hypothesize that a long-lived, color-neutral gluonic vacuum component survives the post-inflationary expansion era and, at large distances, develops a spectrally rigid lowest-weight structure. The microscopic seed for this infrared organization is provided by the QCD trace anomaly, which breaks classical scale invariance and, through dimensional transmutation, generates an intrinsic infrared scale in the gluonic sector. Requiring Lorentz covariance together with a positive-energy lowest-weight unitary realization then selects the Anti de Sitter algebra $\mathfrak{so}(2,3)$ as the simplest symmetry admitting a discrete tower of states with a representation-theoretically protected gap. The associated gap introduces a finite correlation length $r_{\texttt{c}}$ that controls the large-scale coherence of the dark sector. A self-gravitating condensate dominated by the lowest-weight mode generates a characteristic acceleration $g^{}_\star = G M_h / r_{\texttt{c}}^2$, naturally of the same order as the observed galactic acceleration scale, within standard Newtonian gravity. In this framework, the galactic acceleration scale appears as the gravitational imprint of a trace-anomaly-seeded infrared spectral gap in a coherent gluonic dark sector, rather than as a consequence of modified gravity or of galaxy-by-galaxy formation histories.

### [185] [State counting in gravity and maximal entropy principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12980)
*Juan Hernandez,Mikhail Khramtsov*

TL;DR: 该论文证明，从引力路径积分（gravity path integral）视角看，黑洞贝肯斯坦-霍金熵（Bekenstein-Hawking entropy）的微观态计数与霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）纠缠熵的佩奇曲线（Page curve）这两个问题本质上是等价的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半经典近似（semiclassical approximation）可用于解释引力的某些量子特性，如黑洞熵的微观态解释和霍金辐射纠缠熵的佩奇曲线。本文旨在探讨这两个问题在引力路径积分框架下的内在联系。

Method: 通过引力路径积分视角，将两个问题联系起来；关键工具是霍金辐射冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropy）的凸优化问题（convex optimization problem）。

Result: 证明黑洞熵的微观态计数与霍金辐射佩奇曲线在引力路径积分框架下是等价的；只要考虑与黑洞熵兼容的（过）完备微观态基，霍金信息丢失问题（information loss puzzle）即可自动解决。

Conclusion: 从引力路径积分观点看，黑洞熵的态计数解释与霍金辐射的佩奇曲线是同一问题的两个方面，信息丢失问题的解决自然蕴含在与黑洞熵兼容的微观态基的构建中。

Abstract: It is known that the semiclassical approximation to the gravity path integral can be leveraged to explain certain inherently quantum aspects of gravity. One such aspect is the state-counting interpretation of the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of black holes. A second aspect is the Page curve for the entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation, which agrees with expectations from unitarity. We show that these two questions are equivalent from the gravity path integral point of view. In particular, the Hawking's information loss puzzle gets resolved automatically by considering any (over)complete basis of black hole microstates which is compatible with black hole entropy. The tool which relates the two questions is a convex optimization problem for the von Neumann entropy of Hawking radiation.

Method: 通过直接分析Parisi测度（Parisi measure），并利用Jagannath和Tobasco于2017年提供的特征化方法，对Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型在特定参数区域进行严格证明。

Abstract: We show that in the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model at inverse temperature $β$ with uniform external field $h>0$, replica symmetry holds in the regime $ β^2\mathrm{E}[ \mathrm{sech}^4(β\sqrt{q}Z+h)] \le 1$, where $Z$ is a standard Gaussian random variable. This confirms a prediction of de Almeida and Thouless (1978). The proof proceeds by a direct analysis of the Parisi measure using the characterization provided by Jagannath and Tobasco (2017).

### [187] [Integrability of Multispecies Long-Range Swap Models with Species-Dependent Interpolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12136)
*Eunghyun Lee*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文引入了一类具有长程交换相互作用的多物种排斥过程，其中物种间相互作用机制本身依赖于物种参数μ_i，在二元参数体系下证明了模型的可积性，并通过坐标Bethe ansatz推导了满足Yang-Baxter方程的散射矩阵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可积多物种模型通常通过跳跃速率体现物种依赖性，而本文旨在构建一个更一般的框架，使相互作用机制本身能够依赖于物种。这突破了传统模型中物种仅通过速率参数区分的限制，实现了异质系统中不同物种遵循不同微观相互作用机制。

Method: 采用具有长程交换相互作用的多物种排斥过程，为每个物种i分配参数μ_i来控制同物种相互作用，实现TASEP型和drop-push型动力学之间的物种依赖插值。使用坐标Bethe ansatz方法证明两粒子可约性，并推导相关的散射矩阵。

Result: 在二元参数体系μ_i∈{0,1}下，对于任意物种组成证明了模型的可积性。在连续参数体系μ_i∈(0,1)下，识别了多个保持可积性的非平凡物种组成类。进一步将模型扩展到包含双向运动，超越了完全不对称动力学。

Conclusion: 该模型框架实现了相互作用机制本身的物种依赖性，在二元参数体系下具有普遍可积性，其散射矩阵表现出真正的物种依赖性对角元，为研究异质多物种系统提供了新的可积模型。

Abstract: We introduce a class of multispecies exclusion processes with long-range swap interactions, incorporating species-dependent interpolation between TASEP-type and drop--push-type dynamics: each species $i$ is assigned a parameter $μ_i$ governing same-species interactions, resulting in a heterogeneous system in which different species follow distinct microscopic interaction mechanisms. In contrast to previously studied integrable multispecies models, where species dependence typically enters through jump rates, the present framework allows the interaction mechanism itself to depend on the species. Our main result establishes integrability of the model in the binary parameter regime $μ_i \in \{0,1\}$ for arbitrary species compositions. In the continuous parameter regime $μ_i \in (0,1)$, we identify several nontrivial classes of species compositions for which integrability is preserved. We further extend the model to include bidirectional motion, going beyond totally asymmetric dynamics. Using the coordinate Bethe ansatz, we prove two-particle reducibility and derive the associated scattering matrix, which is shown to satisfy the Yang--Baxter equation. The resulting scattering matrix exhibits genuinely species-dependent diagonal entries.

### [188] [Localization Lengths of Power-Law Random Band Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12248)
*Jiaqi Fan,Fan Yang,Jun Yin*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该研究针对具有幂律衰减方差的大规模随机带矩阵，建立了不同参数区间下本征向量局域化长度（localization length）的下界，验证了物理猜想中关于离域化侧的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于理解具有幂律衰减方差的随机带矩阵中本征向量的局域化性质。这类模型具有非平均场（non-mean-field）特性和方差分布的缓慢衰减，需要新的分析方法来验证物理文献中的相关猜想。

Method: 主要方法是通过对由哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的解析子（resolvent）条目对构成的T变量（T-variables）进行新的动力学分析。该方法不依赖于高阶解析子循环（higher-order resolvent loops），专门针对方差缓慢衰减的非平均场模型设计。

Result: 研究建立了不同参数α区间下本征向量局域化长度的下界：当-1<α<0时，ℓ=N；当0<α<1时，ℓ≥W^C（C为大常数）；当1<α<2时，ℓ≥W^{α/(α-1)}；当α>2时，ℓ≥W^2。这些结果验证了arXiv:cond-mat/9604163中关于离域化侧的物理猜想。

Conclusion: 该研究成功解决了具有幂律衰减方差的随机带矩阵中本征向量局域化性质的分析难题，通过创新的T变量动力学分析方法，为理解这类非平均场模型的离域化行为提供了严格的理论基础。

Abstract: We study large $N\times N$ power-law random band matrices $H=(H_{ij})$ with centered complex Gaussian entries, where the variances satisfy a power-law decay $\mathbb{E}|H_{ij}|^2\propto (|i-j|/W+1)^{-1-α}$, for some exponent $α>-1$ and bandwidth $W\gg 1$. We establish the following lower bounds, with high probability, on the localization length $\ell$ of bulk eigenvectors in the different regimes of $α$: (1) $\ell=N$ if $-1<α<0$; (2) $\ell \ge W^{C}$ for any large constant $C>0$ if $0 < α<1$; (3) $\ell \ge W^{α/(α-1)}$ if $1 < α<2$; (4) $\ell \ge W^{2}$ if $ α> 2$. These results verify the physical conjecture of arXiv:cond-mat/9604163 on the delocalized side. The main difficulty in the proof lies in handling the interplay between the non-mean-field nature of the model and the slow decay of the variance profile. To address this issue, a key technical ingredient is a new dynamical analysis of $T$-variables formed from pairs of resolvent entries of $H$. In contrast to the fundamental works on regular random band matrices with fast-decaying variances in arXiv:2501.01718 and arXiv:2506.06441, this approach does not rely on higher-order resolvent loops.

</details>
