### [189] [Systematic Design of Local Rules for Directing Emergent Structure in Bottom-Up Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12057)
*Andrew Slezak,Varda F. Hagh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个系统性框架，用于设计简单构建者的局部行为规则集，使得遵循这些规则时能够涌现出具有目标全局属性的结构。基于受帐篷毛虫启发的简化模型，展示了如何通过调整复杂系统中的局部自由度来引导全局行为，并验证了代理能够可靠地实现网络结构的面积覆盖率、平均线密度和前缘曲率等几何属性的目标值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多生物系统能够集体构建复杂、自适应且功能性的架构，其中功能通过自下而上的构建过程而非自上而下的规划或集中控制涌现。然而，在工程系统中编程和控制这种涌现功能的通用策略在很大程度上尚未被探索。

Method: 研究提出了一个系统性框架，用于设计简单构建者的局部行为规则集（local behavioral rule sets）。使用受帐篷毛虫启发的简化模型，研究配备有限感知能力、无记忆或全局知识的简单代理如何通过局部沉积线段来构建网络结构。该框架基于调整复杂系统中的局部自由度（local degrees of freedom）来改变全局行为。

Result: 通过识别影响特定属性的自由度并指定如何通过局部规则进行调整，研究证明可以引导相应的全局属性。具体探索了代理生成网络的三个几何属性：面积覆盖率（area coverage）、平均线密度（average line density）和前缘曲率（front curvature）。结果显示，代理能够在存在随机性的情况下可靠地实现这些属性的目标值，同时保持低变异性。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一种可推广的方法，用于在去中心化系统（decentralized systems）中编程涌现现象，并为在复杂、不确定环境中设计自适应材料（adaptive materials）和自主构建策略（autonomous construction strategies）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Many biological systems collectively construct complex, adaptive, and functional architectures, where function emerges from bottom-up building processes rather than top-down planning or centralized control. However, general strategies for programming and controlling such emergent function in engineered systems remain largely unexplored. In this work, we present a systematic framework for designing local behavioral rule sets for simple builders such that, when adhered to, structures with targeted global properties emerge. Using a minimal model inspired by tent caterpillars, we study how simple agents equipped with limited sensing and no memory or global knowledge construct networked structures through local deposition of line segments. We base our framework on tuning local degrees of freedom in a complex system to alter global behavior. By identifying the degrees of freedom that influence a given property and specifying how they are tuned through local rules, we demonstrate that the corresponding global properties can be directed. We explore this through three geometric properties of the agents' resulting networks, in particular area coverage, average line density, and front curvature. We show that agents can reliably achieve targeted values for these properties while maintaining low variability in the presence of stochasticity. These results establish a generalizable approach for programming emergence in decentralized systems and suggest new pathways for designing adaptive materials and autonomous construction strategies in complex, uncertain environments.

</details>


### [190] [Preserving elastic anisotropy with tessellations of granular packings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12098)
*Annie Z. Xia,Dong Wang,Catherine La Riviere,Rebecca Kramer-Bottiglio,Mark D. Shattuck,Corey S. O'Hern*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了具有高度各向异性弹性特性的多尺度周期性超材料，通过引入量化弹性各向异性的旋转不变归一化指标，并设计限制颗粒重排的镶嵌颗粒材料，实现了比典型晶体固体高100倍的弹性各向异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究主要关注优化介观结构以获得所需的整体各向同性特性，而本研究旨在开发具有高度各向异性弹性特性的材料，以扩展超材料在冲击吸收、声学隐身、光子带隙和机械逻辑门等应用中的性能边界。

Method: 引入两个旋转不变、归一化的量$A_G$和$A_C$分别量化剪切和压缩的各向异性响应；设计由多个连接的颗粒填充体素组成的镶嵌颗粒材料，限制颗粒重排；通过调控压力$p$和颗粒数$N$的参数$pN^2$来优化各向异性；进一步开发异质图案化体素配置和允许大边界变形的镶嵌方法。

Result: 典型晶体固体的平均弹性各向异性为$\overline{A}_G \approx 0.15$和$\overline{A}_C \approx 0.09$；堵塞颗粒材料可实现比原子晶体高几个数量级的弹性各向异性；在$pN^2\sim1$时获得最大各向异性，在大$pN^2$极限下变为各向同性；均匀镶嵌颗粒系统可在一定$pN^2$范围内继承组成体素配置的弹性响应，弹性各向异性可达晶体化合物的100倍。

Conclusion: 通过设计镶嵌颗粒材料限制颗粒重排，能够实现比传统晶体材料高得多的弹性各向异性；通过调控$pN^2$参数和设计异质图案化体素配置，可进一步调节弹性各向异性，为开发具有定制各向异性特性的先进超材料提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Multiscale periodic metamaterials have been designed for numerous applications, such as impact absorption, acoustic cloaking, photonic band gaps, and mechanical logic gates. This prior work has focused on optimizing mesoscale structure for desired bulk isotropic properties. In contrast, we seek to develop materials with highly anisotropic elastic properties. To quantify elastic anisotropy, we introduce two rotationally invariant, normalized quantities that characterize the anisotropic response to shear and compression, respectively, $A_G$ and $A_C$. We find that typical crystalline solids possess average elastic anisotropy $\overline{A}_G \approx 0.15$ and $\overline{A}_C \approx 0.09$. Compared to atomic crystals, jammed granular materials can attain elastic anisotropies that are several orders of magnitude larger. Since grain rearrangements reduce anisotropy in granular materials, to preserve strong elastic anisotropy, we design tessellated granular materials that consist of multiple connected grain-filled voxels, which limit rearrangements and enable highly anisotropic elastic properties. Bulk granular packings with $N$ grains prepared at pressure $p$ have maximal anisotropy for $pN^2\sim1$ and become isotropic in the large-$pN^2$ limit. We show that homogeneously tessellated granular systems can inherit the elastic response of the constituent voxel configurations with elastic anisotropy up to $100$ times that of crystalline compounds over a range of $pN^2$. We show further methods to tune the elastic anisotropy of tessellations by designing heterogeneously patterned voxel configurations and tessellations that allow large boundary deformations.

</details>


### [191] [Disentangling microstructural elements of shear thickening suspensions via computer simulations of a minimal model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12107)
*William C. J. Buchholtz,Daniel L. Blair,Jeffrey S. Urbach,H. A. Vinutha,Emanuela Del Gado*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过二维模拟探究了稠密悬浮液在增稠和减稠过程中的微观结构变化，发现接触网络中的特定结构单元在增稠时形成跨越性组装体并导致非高斯应力波动，而在减稠时这些结构发生变形并促进接触力的均匀空间重分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究稠密悬浮液在增稠（thickening）和减稠（thinning）过程中的微观结构变化，特别是接触网络中结构单元的演化及其与宏观应力行为的关联。

Method: 采用二维模拟方法，使用一个描述稠密悬浮液增稠和减稠过程的最小模型（minimal model），通过分析径向分布函数（radial distribution function）的尖峰信号来识别接触网络中的结构单元。

Result: 模拟显示稳态流中接触网络包含类似颗粒堵塞（granular jamming）的特定结构单元，这些单元在减稠时发生变形。增稠过程中出现的非高斯应力波动与局部接触力分布的幂律尾部（power law tails）相关，此时结构单元形成跨越性组装体（spanning assemblies）。表征为强接触力和足够大连接性的接触网络子集在增稠开始时更可能发生渗流（percolate），并在减稠时其跨越性和持久性显著降低。

Conclusion: 稠密悬浮液的增稠行为与接触网络中刚性或过约束结构单元形成跨越性组装体密切相关，而减稠过程则通过结构变形促进接触力的均匀空间重分布，从而显著降低宏观应力的时间波动。

Abstract: We use a minimal model for a dense suspension undergoing thickening and thinning to investigate microstructural changes in 2d simulations. Our simulations show that in steady flow the contact network contains distinct building blocks which are clearly signaled by sharp peaks in the radial distribution function, similar to what is observed in granular jamming. These structures {deform} during thinning. Non-Gaussian stress fluctuations that only emerge during thickening are associated to power law tails in the distribution of local contact forces, which tend to emerge when the flow-induced building blocks form large spanning assemblies. The subset of the contact network characterized by strong contact forces and connectivity large enough to be rigid or over-constrained is increasingly likely to percolate as the system starts to thicken, and to percolate over larger strain windows during thickening. The tendency of these structures to span the sample and to persist is dramatically reduced during thinning, where instead their deformation allows for a more homogeneous spatial redistribution of contact forces, significantly reducing the fluctuations of the macroscopic stress over time.

</details>

Abstract: Inspired by the structure of $srs$ Laves networks in $\mathbb{R}^3$ that underpin the celebrated gyroid surface, we construct a Laves network of identical three-coordinated vertices on $S^3$ with double-twist. ### [193] [Building and maintaining a System of Intracellular Compartments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12930)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细胞器模式化及其遗传性仍是细胞生物学的核心谜题，反映了遗传继承与自组装之间的基本张力。研究旨在探索高尔基复合体（Golgi complex）和内体（endosomes）在连续膜运输流中的非平衡组装和尺寸控制机制。

Method: 采用随机框架分析违反细致平衡（detailed balance）的机械化学融合-分裂循环（fusion-fission cycles）。运用动力学系统方法（dynamical systems approach）识别从固定点到具有确定相位关系的极限环（limit cycles）等不同稳健机制。

Result: 研究识别出与多种表型对应的动力学机制，从稳定囊泡到周期性、细胞周期依赖的溶解/重组装，再到囊泡进展（cisternal progression）。分析显示高尔基体组织的两种竞争模型——囊泡运输（vesicular transport）和囊泡进展——实际上是同一基础非平衡过程的两个相（phases）。

Conclusion: 该框架为通过调节糖基化酶（glycosylation enzymes）与膜分裂-融合动力学之间的相互作用来控制囊泡化学特性和数量提供了策略，揭示了非平衡过程在细胞器组织中的核心作用。

Abstract: Organelle patterning and its heritability remain central mysteries in cell biology, highlighting the fundamental tension between genetic inheritance and self-assembly. Here, we explore the nonequilibrium assembly and size control of the Golgi complex and endosomes, amid a continuous flux of membrane traffic, within a stochastic framework of mechanochemical fusion-fission cycles that violate detailed balance. Using a dynamical systems approach, we identify distinct, robust regimes, ranging from fixed points to limit cycles with definite phase relations. We identify these dynamical regimes with diverse phenotypes, from stable cisternae to periodic, cell-cycle-dependent dissolution/reassembly to cisternal progression. We analyse its dynamic response to systematic perturbations or driving protocols and make definite predictions that may be tested experimentally. Our analysis reveals that the two competing models of Golgi organization-vesicular transport and cisternal progression - are, in fact, two phases of the same underlying nonequilibrium process. Finally, our framework offers a strategy for controlling cisternal chemical identity and number and by modulating the interplay between glycosylation enzymes and membrane fission-fusion dynamics.

### [194] [Inverse design of a magneto-elastica for shape-morphing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12938)
*JiaHao Li,Yingchao Zhang,Weicheng Huang,Shenghao Ye,HengAn Wu,Dominic Vella,Mingchao Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究建立了磁弹性梁（magneto-elastica）逆设计的显式解析框架，基于力矩平衡方程的积分形式，系统表征了可行设计空间，获得了夹持-自由和夹持-夹持配置下产生目标形状所需的梁锥度剖面封闭解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细长磁性元件为远程磁驱动下的可编程形状变形提供了多功能平台，但缺乏在指定边界条件下磁弹性梁逆设计的通用且物理可解释的框架。现有方法无法系统地表征可行设计空间。

Method: 基于力矩平衡方程的积分形式，建立了磁弹性梁逆设计的显式解析公式。该方法直接约束了允许的曲率和旋转场，并识别了控制磁扭矩与弹性恢复力矩竞争的关键无量纲参数。进一步提出了基于刚度剪裁的镶嵌策略用于离散化变形表面设计。

Result: 获得了夹持-自由和夹持-夹持配置下产生目标驱动形状所需梁锥度剖面的封闭解（closed-form solutions），后者包含边界反力的解析表达式。公式在无磁场时恢复经典逆弹性曲线，并揭示了曲率偏差与磁失配之间的线性缩放关系。理论预测通过离散弹性杆模拟和代表性几何实验得到验证。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了磁弹性梁逆设计的一致解析框架，为细长结构中磁诱导形状编程提供了新的见解。该框架系统地表征了可行设计空间，揭示了边界条件在磁弹性设计中的关键作用。

Abstract: Slender magnetic elements provide a versatile platform for programmable shape-morphing under remote magnetic actuation. However, a general and physically interpretable framework for the inverse design of a `magneto-elastica' under prescribed boundary conditions remains lacking. In this work, we develop an explicit analytical formulation for the inverse design of a magneto-elastica based on the integral form of the moment equilibrium equations. This approach yields direct constraints on the admissible curvature and rotation fields, enabling a systematic characterization of the feasible design space. We identify the key dimensionless parameters that govern the competition between magnetic torques and elastic restoring moments and show that the applied boundary conditions are an essential ingredient. We obtain closed-form solutions for the beam tapering profiles required to generate desired actuated shapes in the cases of clamped--free and clamped--clamped configurations; in the latter case, this includes analytical expressions for the boundary reactions. The formulation recovers the classical inverse elastica in the absence of magnetic fields and reveals a linear scaling between curvature deviation and magnetic mismatch. A tessellation strategy based on stiffness tailoring is further proposed for the design of discretized morphing surfaces. The theoretical predictions are validated against discrete elastic rod simulations and experiments across representative geometries. This work establishes a consistent analytical framework for the inverse design of a magneto-elastica and provides new insight into magnetically-induced shape programming in slender structures.

### [195] [Limits of Statistical Models of Ultracold Complex Lifetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12063)
*Kevin B. Xu,John L. Bohn*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种统计模型来模拟分子碰撞中的"粘性碰撞"现象，通过随机矩阵理论和量子缺陷理论计算散射性质与寿命，发现在密集共振极限下与RRKM理论一致，而在稀疏共振极限下物理机制由阈值行为主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子碰撞中"粘性碰撞（sticky collisions）"现象——碰撞复合体表现出长寿命——仍是一个未解之谜。主要挑战在于传统的紧耦合计算（close-coupling calculations）受限于计算成本，难以考虑碰撞涉及的所有自由度。

Method: 提出一个统计模型来模拟紧耦合计算，通过随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）数值采样共振，并利用量子缺陷理论（quantum defect theory）计算散射性质和寿命。

Result: 在密集共振极限下，该理论与Rice-Ramsperger-Kassel-Markus（RRKM）预测一致；在稀疏共振极限下，物理机制由阈值行为而非共振效应主导。通过与两个极限下的实验结果比较，表明仅靠紧耦合计算可能不足以解决长寿命问题。

Conclusion: 紧耦合计算本身可能不足以解决粘性碰撞的长寿命问题，需要结合统计模型方法。该研究揭示了不同共振密度极限下的物理机制差异，为理解分子碰撞动力学提供了新视角。

Abstract: The puzzle of "sticky collisions," in which molecular collision complexes exhibit long lifetimes, remains an unresolved mystery. A central challenge is that traditional close-coupling calculations remain limited by the vast computational cost needed to take into account all the degrees of freedom involved in the collision. In this work, we propose a statistical model designed to simulate close-coupling calculations, with the goal of collecting statistics about reasonable lifetimes of collision complexes. To do so, we numerically sample resonances using random matrix theory and utilize results from quantum defect theory to calculate scattering properties and lifetimes. We find that in the limit of dense resonances, our theory agrees well with the Rice-Ramsperger-Kassel-Markus (RRKM) prediction, whereas in the limit of sparse resonances, the physics is governed by threshold behavior rather than resonant effects. By comparing these predictions to experimental results in two limits, we argue that close-coupling calculations alone may be insufficient to resolve the issue of long lifetimes.

</details>


### [196] [Experimental Determination of the $D1$ Magic Wavelength for $^{40}$K](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12448)
*Guy Hay Kalifa,Dor Kopelevitch,Amir Stern,Yoav Sagi*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 该论文首次实验确定了费米子⁴⁰K原子D1跃迁的魔幻波长（magic wavelength）为1227.54(3) nm，解决了中性原子阵列中因光频移导致的冷却和探测保真度下降问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中性原子阵列（neutral-atom arrays）在量子模拟中具有广阔前景，但费米子⁴⁰K的潜力受到状态依赖光频移（state-dependent light shifts）的限制，这会降低冷却和探测保真度。通过寻找魔幻波长（magic wavelength）可以消除差分光频移（differential light shift），从而解决这一问题。

Method: 采用波长可调光学镊子（wavelength-tunable optical tweezer）进行阱内损耗光谱（in-trap loss spectroscopy）测量，通过扫描不同阱功率和波长来映射差分交流斯塔克位移（differential AC Stark shift）。将位移转换为差分标量极化率（differential scalar polarizabilities），并与相对论全阶计算（relativistic all-order calculations）进行比较。

Result: 首次实验确定了费米子⁴⁰K原子D1跃迁的魔幻波长为1227.54(3) nm。测量结果与相对论全阶计算高度一致。在1064.49 nm基准测量中，揭示了标准阱波长存在的显著强度采样系统误差（intensity-sampling systematics），而魔幻条件则提供了"机械清洁"（mechanically clean）的环境。

Conclusion: 该研究为实现高保真度的阱内D1冷却（in-trap D1 cooling）、荧光成像（fluorescence imaging）和光辅助加载（light-assisted loading）提供了重要基础，为扩展费米子中性原子阵列在量子信息科学（quantum information science）中的应用建立了可靠路径。

Abstract: Neutral-atom arrays offer a promising path for quantum simulation, yet the potential of fermionic $^{40}$K remains largely constrained by state-dependent light shifts that degrade cooling and detection fidelities. This problem can be resolved by working at a magic wavelength, where the differential light shift vanishes. We report the first experimental determination of the magic wavelength for the D1 transition in fermionic $^{40}$K at 1227.54(3) nm. Using in-trap loss spectroscopy in a wavelength-tunable optical tweezer, we map the differential AC Stark shift across a range of trapping powers and wavelengths. By converting these shifts to differential scalar polarizabilities, we find excellent agreement with relativistic all-order calculations. Benchmark measurements at 1064.49 nm further reveal the significant intensity-sampling systematics that plague standard trapping wavelengths, contrasting with the "mechanically clean" environment provided by the magic condition. Our results provide an important step toward high-fidelity in-trap D1 cooling, fluorescence imaging, and light-assisted loading, establishing a robust path toward scaling fermionic neutral-atom arrays for quantum information science.

</details>
